### [139] [Latent Causal Void: Explicit Missing-Context Reconstruction for Misinformation Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12156)
*Hui Li,Zhongquan Jian,Jinsong Su,Junfeng Yao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Latent Causal Void (LCV)的检索引导型检测方法，用于在信息缺失的语境下更有效地识别虚假信息。该方法通过检索时间对齐的背景文章，并利用冻结的指令微调大模型生成每个目标句子缺失的上下文描述，进而将这些具体缺失事实作为文本关系引入异构图中进行推理。相比现有方法，LCV在英文和中文双语基准上分别提升了2.56和2.84的宏F1分数，表明显式建模缺失事实比仅附加证据或预测遗漏信号更具优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的遗漏感知方法通常只是附加检索到的背景信息或预测一个类别化的遗漏信号，而无法显式表达具体的缺失事实。然而，许多误导性内容在局部上看似合理，只有在与同期报道对比时才显现出问题。因此，需要一种能够显式重建缺失事实的方法来提升虚假信息检测性能。

Method: LCV首先检索时间对齐的上下文文章，然后使用一个冻结的指令微调的大语言模型为每个目标句子-文章对生成一段简短的缺失上下文描述，最后将这些描述作为文本关系输入到包含目标句子和上下文文章的异构图中进行图推理。

Result: 在Sheng等人提出的双语基准测试中，LCV在英文和中文数据集上的宏F1分数分别优于最强的遗漏感知基线2.56和2.84点，验证了显式建模缺失事实的有效性。

Conclusion: 显式重建跨源缺失事实并将其作为文本关系用于图推理，是一种比仅附加证据或预测遗漏信号更有效的遗漏感知虚假信息检测方法。

Abstract: Automatic misinformation detection performs well when deception is visible in what an article explicitly states. However, some misinformation articles remain locally coherent and only become misleading once compared with contemporaneous reports that supply background facts the article omits. We study this omission-relevant setting and observe that current omission-aware approaches typically either attach retrieved context as auxiliary evidence or infer a categorical omission signal, leaving the specific missing fact implicit. We propose \emph{Latent Causal Void} (LCV), a retrieval-guided detector that explicitly reconstructs the missing fact for each target sentence and uses it as a textual cross-source relation in graph reasoning. Concretely, LCV retrieves temporally aligned context articles, asks a frozen instruction-tuned large language model to generate a short missing-context description for each sentence--article pair, and feeds the resulting relation text into a heterograph over target sentences and context articles. On the bilingual benchmark of Sheng et al., LCV improves over the strongest omission-aware baseline by $2.56$ and $2.84$ macro-F1 points on the English and Chinese splits, respectively. The results indicate that modeling the missing cross-source fact itself, rather than only attaching retrieved evidence or predicting an omission signal, is a useful representation for omission-aware misinformation detection.

### [140] [Mitigating Context-Memory Conflicts in LLMs through Dynamic Cognitive Reconciliation Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12185)
*Yigeng Zhou,Wu Li,Yifan Lu,Yequan Wang,Xuebo Liu,Wenya Wang,Jun Yu,Min Zhang,Jing Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为动态认知调和解码（DCRD）的两阶段解码方法，以预测并缓解上下文与记忆之间的知识冲突。该方法首先通过分析注意力图评估上下文保真度并预测潜在冲突，随后根据预测结果选择贪婪解码或基于上下文保真度的动态解码路径。该设计在存在冲突时高效处理问题，同时在无冲突情况下保持高准确率和解码效率。为模拟频繁知识更新场景，作者构建了冲突知识问答基准 ConflictKG。在四个大语言模型和六个问答数据集上的实验表明，DCRD显著优于所有基线方法，达到当前最佳性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在处理上下文与参数化知识冲突时存在局限性：静态方法在无冲突场景中破坏输出分布，而动态方法在复杂现实情境下仍难以准确衡量冲突程度。因此需要一种既能有效应对冲突，又能在无冲突时保持高效与准确的动态解码机制。

Method: 提出两阶段动态认知调和解码（DCRD）方法：第一阶段分析注意力图以评估上下文保真度并预测冲突；第二阶段根据预测结果选择贪婪解码或上下文保真度驱动的动态解码路径，实现自适应解码策略。

Result: 在四个大语言模型和六个问答数据集上的实验验证表明，DCRD在各类场景下均表现优异，显著优于现有基线方法，实现了更高的准确率与解码效率，尤其在存在知识冲突的情况下优势明显。

Conclusion: DCRD通过智能预测与自适应解码路径选择，有效解决了大语言模型中的知识冲突问题，在保证无冲突场景下的高效性的同时，提升了有冲突场景下的鲁棒性，为解决模型记忆与外部知识间的不一致提供了新范式。

Abstract: Large language models accumulate extensive parametric knowledge through pre-training. However, knowledge conflicts occur when outdated or incorrect parametric knowledge conflicts with external knowledge in the context. Existing methods address knowledge conflicts through contrastive decoding, but in conflict-free scenarios, static approaches disrupt output distribution. Other dynamic decoding methods attempt to measure the degree of conflict but still struggle with complex real-world situations. In this paper, we propose a two-stage decoding method called Dynamic Cognitive Reconciliation Decoding (DCRD), to predict and mitigate context-memory conflicts. DCRD first analyzes the attention map to assess context fidelity and predict potential conflicts. Based on this prediction, the input is directed to one of two decoding paths: (1) greedy decoding, or (2) context fidelity-based dynamic decoding. This design enables DCRD to handle conflicts efficiently while maintaining high accuracy and decoding efficiency in conflict-free cases. Additionally, to simulate scenarios with frequent knowledge updates, we constructed ConflictKG, a knowledge conflict QA benchmark. Experiments on four LLMs across six QA datasets show that DCRD outperforms all baselines, achieving state-of-the-art performance.

### [141] [Mechanistic Interpretability of ASR models using Sparse Autoencoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12225)
*Dan Pluth,Zachary Nicholas Houghton,Yu Zhou,Vijay K. Gurbani*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究首次将稀疏自编码器（SAE）应用于基于Transformer的自动语音识别模型Whisper，通过在帧级嵌入上训练高维稀疏潜在空间，揭示了跨语言和非语言边界的单义特征，并实现了跨语言特征控制。结果表明Whisper编码了丰富的语言信息，验证了SAE在音频处理模型中的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前深度Transformer-based NLP模型虽广泛应用，但其内部机制仍不清晰。尽管稀疏自编码器（SAE）已被用于解释文本型大语言模型，但尚未有研究将其应用于自动语音识别（ASR）模型。因此，亟需探索SAE在音频处理模型中的适用性，以理解如Whisper这类ASR模型的内部表征机制。

Method: 在Whisper模型的编码器中提取帧级嵌入，使用稀疏自编码器（SAE）对其进行训练，构建高维稀疏潜在空间，以发现并分析其中的单义特征。进一步通过特征操纵实现跨语言特征控制，验证模型内部表示的可解释性。

Result: 成功在Whisper中发现了多种跨越语言与非语言边界的单义特征，且可通过特征操纵实现跨语言控制。实验表明，Whisper的编码空间富含语言信息，且SAE能有效揭示其内部表征结构。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了稀疏自编码器在自动语音识别模型中的有效性，为理解Whisper等音频处理模型的内部工作机制提供了新的可解释性工具，拓展了SAE的应用边界至语音领域。

Abstract: Understanding the internal machinations of deep Transformer-based NLP models is more crucial than ever as these models see widespread use in various domains that affect the public at large, such as industry, academia, finance, health. While these models have advanced rapidly, their internal mechanisms remain largely a mystery. Techniques such as Sparse Autoencoders (SAE) have emerged to understand these mechanisms by projecting dense representations into a sparse vector. While existing research has demonstrated the viability of the SAE in interpreting text-based Large Language Models (LLMs), there are no equivalent studies that demonstrate the application of a SAE to audio processing models like Automatic Speech Recognizers (ASRs). In this work, a SAE is applied to Whisper, a Transformer-based ASR, training a high-dimensional sparse latent space on frame-level embeddings extracted from the Whisper encoder. Our work uncovers diverse monosemantic features across linguistic and non-linguistic boundaries, and demonstrates cross-lingual feature steering. This work establishes the viability of a SAE model and demonstrates that Whisper encodes a rich amount of linguistic information.

### [142] [Combining On-Policy Optimization and Distillation for Long-Context Reasoning in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12227)
*Miguel Moura Ramos,Duarte M. Alves,André F. T. Martins*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出dGRPO方法，结合GRPO与OPD，通过强教师提供密集指导，提升长上下文推理的稳定性与效果；引入LongBlocks数据集，涵盖多跳推理、上下文定位和长文本生成。实验表明，联合优化目标在长上下文任务中表现更优，同时保持短上下文能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长上下文适配方法存在局限：离策略方法如SFT和KD受暴露偏差影响，难以纠正模型生成错误；在线策略RL方法如GRPO因奖励稀疏而不稳定且样本效率低；在线策略蒸馏（OPD）虽有密集指导但无法直接优化任意奖励信号。需要一种能结合密集指导与有效奖励优化的新方法。

Method: 提出dGRPO，将GRPO与OPD结合，在政策优化中引入强教师提供的密集知识蒸馏信号，形成统一目标函数，实现对长上下文任务的稳定高效训练。同时构建LongBlocks数据集，用于支持多跳推理、上下文定位和长文本生成等任务的评估。

Result: dGRPO在长上下文任务中显著优于传统离策略方法和GRPO，具备更高的准确性和连贯性；实验验证了联合优化框架的优越性，且未牺牲模型在短上下文任务上的表现。

Conclusion: 将基于结果的策略优化与知识蒸馏结合于单一目标，是实现长上下文推理的更稳定、高效路径，为大语言模型的长文本理解提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Adapting large language models (LLMs) to long-context tasks requires post-training methods that remain accurate and coherent over thousands of tokens. Existing approaches are limited in several ways: 1) off-policy methods such as supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and knowledge distillation (KD) suffer from exposure bias and limited recovery from model-generated errors over long horizons; 2) on-policy reinforcement learning methods such as Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) better align training with model-generated states, but are unstable and sample-inefficient due to sparse rewards; 3) on-policy distillation (OPD) provides dense token-level guidance, but does not directly optimize arbitrary reward signals. In this paper, we propose Distilled Group Relative Policy Optimization (dGRPO), a method for long-context reasoning that augments GRPO with dense guidance from a stronger teacher via OPD. We also introduce LongBlocks, a synthetic long-context dataset spanning multi-hop reasoning, contextual grounding, and long-form generation. We conduct extensive experiments and ablations comparing off-policy training, sparse-reward GRPO, and our combined approach, leading to an improved recipe for long-context alignment. Overall, our results show that combining outcome-based policy optimization with knowledge distillation in a single objective provides a more stable and effective path to long-context reasoning, while preserving short-context capabilities.

### [143] [Mind the Pause: Disfluency-Aware Objective Tuning for Multilingual Speech Correction with LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12242)
*Deepak Kumar,Baban Gain,Asif Ekbal*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种多语言语音识别转录文本的流畅性修正管道，结合序列标注器标记不流畅词元，并通过指令微调大语言模型进行重写，同时引入对比学习以抑制不流畅词元的重现，从而在保持语法和语义的同时去除冗余内容。实验在印地语、孟加拉语和马拉地语上验证了该方法优于现有基线，证明仅依赖检测策略不足，而融合标记信号与指令微调及对比学习是高效且可扩展的解决方案。代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ASR转录文本中的不流畅现象（如填充词、重复、误启）影响可读性并损害下游应用可靠性，传统方法仅识别并移除不流畅词元，常破坏语法结构和语义连贯性；现有基于大语言模型的研究多集中于检测或数据增强，缺乏对完整修正的系统探索。

Method: 提出一个多语言修正流水线：首先使用序列标注器标记不流畅词元；随后利用这些标记信号对大语言模型进行指令微调，实现转录文本的流畅重写；进一步引入对比学习目标，惩罚模型再现不流畅词元，强化对语义与语法的保留。

Result: 在印地语、孟加拉语和马拉地语上的实验显示，该方法持续优于强基线模型（包括多语言序列到序列模型），证明了检测-修正联合策略的有效性。

Conclusion: 仅靠检测不流畅词元不足以实现高质量修正；结合词元级标记信号、指令微调与对比学习，能够有效提升多语言语音驱动NLP系统的流畅性与可靠性，是一种实用且可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: Automatic Speech Recognition (ASR) transcripts often contain disfluencies, such as fillers, repetitions, and false starts, which reduce readability and hinder downstream applications like chatbots and voice assistants. If left unaddressed, such disfluencies can significantly degrade the reliability of downstream systems. Most existing approaches rely on classical models that focus on identifying disfluent tokens for removal. While this strategy is effective to some extent, it often disrupts grammatical structure and semantic coherence, leading to incomplete or unnatural sentences. Recent literature explored the use of large language models (LLMs); however, these efforts have primarily focused on disfluency detection or data augmentation, rather than performing comprehensive correction. We propose a multilingual correction pipeline where a sequence tagger first marks disfluent tokens, and these signals guide instruction fine-tuning of an LLM to rewrite transcripts into fluent text. To further improve reliability, we add a contrastive learning objective that penalizes the reproduction of disfluent tokens, encouraging the model to preserve grammar and meaning while removing disfluent artifacts. Our experiments across three Indian languages, namely Hindi, Bengali, and Marathi show consistent improvements over strong baselines, including multilingual sequence-to-sequence models. These results highlight that detection-only strategies are insufficient. Combining token-level cues with instruction tuning and contrastive learning provides a practical and scalable solution for multilingual disfluency correction in speech-driven NLP systems. We make the codes publicly available at https://github.com/deepak-kumar-98/Mind-the-Pause.

### [144] [PreScam: A Benchmark for Predicting Scam Progression from Early Conversations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12243)
*Weixiang Sun,Shang Ma,Yiyang Li,Tianyi Ma,Zehong Wang,Colby Nelson,Xusheng Xiao,Yanfang Ye*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出PreScam基准，用于建模对话式诈骗（如情感和投资诈骗）在早期对话中的进展。基于用户提交的诈骗报告，将177,989条原始记录筛选并结构化为11,573个跨20类诈骗的对话实例，每个实例按提出的诈骗杀伤链生命周期分层，并在每轮对话中标注诈骗者心理行为与受害者回应。在两个任务上评估模型：实时终止预测（判断对话是否接近结束）和诈骗者行为预测（预测下一步行为）。结果表明，尽管监督编码器在终止预测上优于零样本大模型，但大模型在行为预测上仍表现一般，说明当前模型虽能捕捉部分诈骗线索，但在追踪风险升级和操纵过程方面仍有显著不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多关注静态诈骗检测或合成诈骗，缺乏对真实世界多轮对话诈骗如何随时间演变的理解，亟需一个能刻画诈骗发展过程的基准。

Result: 监督编码器在实时终止预测任务上显著优于零样本大语言模型；而即使在强语言模型下，下一步行为预测也仅达到中等水平，表明当前模型难以有效追踪诈骗风险的动态演化和操纵机制。

Conclusion: 当前语言模型虽能识别部分诈骗特征，但在理解诈骗随对话进程逐步升级的动态机制方面仍存在明显不足，需要更深入的进展建模能力。

Abstract: Conversational scams, such as romance and investment scams, are emerging as a major form of online fraud. Unlike one-shot scam lures such as fake lottery or unpaid toll messages, they unfold through multi-turn conversations in which scammers gradually manipulate victims using evolving psychological techniques. However, existing research mainly focuses on static scam detection or synthetic scams, leaving open whether language models can understand how real-world scams progress over time. We introduce PreScam, a benchmark for modeling scam progression from early conversations. Built from user-submitted scam reports, PreScam filters and structures 177,989 raw reports into 11,573 conversational scam instances spanning 20 scam categories. Each instance is hierarchically structured according to the scam lifecycle defined by the proposed scam kill chain, and further annotated at the turn level with scammer psychological actions and victim responses. We benchmark models on two tasks: real-time termination prediction, which estimates whether a conversation is approaching the termination stage, and scammer action prediction, which forecasts the scammer's subsequent actions. Results show a clear gap between surface-level fluency and progression modeling: supervised encoders substantially outperform zero-shot LLMs on real-time termination prediction, while next-action prediction remains only moderately successful even for strong LLMs. Taken together, these results show that current models can capture some scam-related cues, yet still struggle to track how risk escalates and how manipulation unfolds across turns.

### [145] [What makes a word hard to learn? Modeling L1 influence on English vocabulary difficulty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12281)
*Jonas Mayer Martins,Zhuojing Huang,Aaricia Herygers,Lisa Beinborn*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究影响英语词汇学习难度的因素及其与学习者母语之间的关系，以优化词汇教学设计。

Method: 采用梯度提升模型，基于词汇的熟悉度、意义、表面形式及跨语言迁移等特征进行建模，并利用Shapley值分析各特征组的重要性。

Result: 词汇熟悉度对所有母语群体均是主导因素；西语和德语学习者受拼写迁移影响显著，而汉语学习者不受此影响，其难度主要由熟悉度和表面特征决定。

Abstract: What makes a word difficult to learn, and how does the difficulty depend on the learner's native language? We computationally model vocabulary difficulty for English learners whose first language is Spanish, German, or Chinese with gradient-boosted models trained on features related to a word's familiarity (e.g., frequency), meaning, surface form, and cross-linguistic transfer. Using Shapley values, we determine the importance of each feature group. Word familiarity is the dominant feature group shared by all three languages. However, predictions for Spanish- and German-speaking learners rely additionally on orthographic transfer. This transfer mechanism is unavailable to Chinese learners, whose difficulty is shaped by a combination of familiarity and surface features alone. Our models provide interpretable, L1-tailored difficulty estimates that can be used to design vocabulary curricula.

### [146] [TokenRatio: Principled Token-Level Preference Optimization via Ratio Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12288)
*Truong Nguyen,Tien-Phat Nguyen,Linh Ngo Van,Duy Minh Ho Nguyen,Khoa Doan,Trung Le*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Token-level Bregman Preference Optimization (TBPO)的新方法，旨在从标准的序列级成对比较中恢复逐标记（token-level）的偏好最优性。与现有方法不同，TBPO在前缀条件下的下一个标记动作上建立逐标记的Bradley-Terry偏好模型，并推导出一种基于Bregman散度的密度比匹配目标，该目标推广了逻辑回归和DPO损失，同时保持逐标记模型所诱导的最优策略并维持类似DPO的简洁性。文中提出了两种实现方式：TBPO-Q显式学习一个轻量级状态基线，而TBPO-A通过优势归一化去除了基线。在指令遵循、有用性/无害性以及摘要生成等多个基准测试中，TBPO在对齐质量、训练稳定性和输出多样性方面均优于强序列级和逐标记基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有直接偏好优化（DPO）方法虽广泛用于语言模型对齐，但其建模的是完整序列层面的偏好，而实际生成过程是基于逐标记决策。虽然已有逐标记扩展方法存在，但它们通常将序列级Bradley-Terry目标分解到各个时间步，导致前缀（状态）层面的最优性隐含未显式建模。因此，迫切需要一种能从序列级成对比较中显式恢复逐标记偏好最优性的方法，以提升模型生成的质量与稳定性。

Method: 提出Token-level Bregman Preference Optimization (TBPO)，构建了一个在给定前缀条件下对下一个标记动作的逐标记Bradley-Terry偏好模型，并推导出一个基于Bregman散度的密度比匹配目标函数。该目标函数能够统一处理序列级和逐标记级的偏好信息，同时保留逐标记模型所诱导的最优策略。具体包括两个变体：TBPO-Q引入轻量级状态基线以增强稳定性；TBPO-A通过优势归一化去除基线，进一步简化结构。

Result: 在多个基准任务（如指令跟随、有用性/无害性判断、文本摘要）上的实验表明，TBPO显著提升了模型对齐质量、训练稳定性及输出多样性。相较于当前主流的序列级（如DPO）和逐标记级方法，TBPO在各项指标上均表现更优，且具有良好的可扩展性和实用性。

Conclusion: TBPO成功地从标准序列级成对比较中恢复了逐标记层面的偏好最优性，通过引入新的目标函数和两套实现方案，在不牺牲计算效率的前提下，实现了更高质量、更稳定的语言模型对齐。该方法为无需强化学习的偏好优化提供了新思路，具有广泛的应用潜力。

Abstract: Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) is a widely used RL-free method for aligning language models from pairwise preferences, but it models preferences over full sequences even though generation is driven by per-token decisions. Existing token-level extensions typically decompose a sequence-level Bradley-Terry objective across timesteps, leaving per-prefix (state-wise) optimality implicit. We study how to recover token-level preference optimality using only standard sequence-level pairwise comparisons. We introduce Token-level Bregman Preference Optimization (TBPO), which posits a token-level Bradley-Terry preference model over next-token actions conditioned on the prefix, and derive a Bregman-divergence density-ratio matching objective that generalizes the logistic/DPO loss while preserving the optimal policy induced by the token-level model and maintaining DPO-like simplicity. We introduce two instantiations: TBPO-Q, which explicitly learns a lightweight state baseline, and TBPO-A, which removes the baseline through advantage normalization. Across instruction following, helpfulness/harmlessness, and summarization benchmarks, TBPO improves alignment quality and training stability and increases output diversity relative to strong sequence-level and token-level baselines.

</details>


### [147] [Overview of the MedHopQA track at BioCreative IX: track description, participation and evaluation of systems for multi-hop medical question answering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12313)
*Rezarta Islamaj,Joey Chan,Robert Leaman,Jongmyung Jung,Hyeongsoon Hwang,Quoc-An Nguyen,Hoang-Quynh Le,Harikrishnan Gurushankar Saisudha,Ganesh Chandrasekar,Rustam R. Taktashov,Nadezhda Yu. Bizyukova,Sofia I. R. Conceição,Paulo R. C. Lopes,Reem Abdel Salam,Mary Adewunmi,Zhiyong Lu*

Result: 顶级系统在MedCPT指标上获得89.30% F1和87.30%精确匹配，远超零样本基线的67.40% F1和60.20%精确匹配；表明检索增强策略对提升性能至关重要；概念级评估有效提升了对不同表达形式正确答案的识别能力。

Abstract: Multi-hop question answering (QA) remains a significant challenge in the biomedical domain, requiring systems to integrate information across multiple sources to answer complex questions. To address this problem, the BioCreative IX MedHopQA shared task was designed to benchmark in multi-hop reasoning for large language models (LLMs). We developed a novel dataset of 1,000 challenging QA pairs spanning diseases, genes, and chemicals, with particular emphasis on rare diseases. Each question was constructed to require two-hop reasoning through the integration of information from two distinct Wikipedia pages. The challenge attracted 48 submissions from 13 teams. Systems were evaluated using both surface string comparison and conceptual accuracy (MedCPT score). The results showed a substantial performance gap between baseline LLMs and enhanced systems. The top-ranked submission achieved an 89.30% F1 score on the MedCPT metric and an 87.30% exact match (EM) score, compared with 67.40% and 60.20%, respectively, for the zero-shot baseline. A central finding of the challenge was that retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) and related retrieval-based strategies were critical for strong performance. In addition, concept-level evaluation improved answer assessment when correct responses differed in surface form. The MedHopQA dataset is publicly available to support continued progress in this important area. ### [148] [Output Composability of QLoRA PEFT Modules for Plug-and-Play Attribute-Controlled Text Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12345)
*Michela Lorandi,Anya Belz*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文探讨了参数高效微调（PEFT）技术在多任务场景下的泛化能力，提出三种方法：联合训练多个相关数据集、推理时组合已独立训练的PEFT模块权重矩阵、以及推理时组合输出。实验表明，输出相加的组合方式表现优异，在多种任务下均优于或等同于单任务专用模块，尤其在情感控制任务中平均性能提升2个百分点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有PEFT方法虽成本低，但需为每个新任务单独微调，缺乏跨任务泛化能力；本文旨在探索如何通过组合策略实现多任务通用性，减少重复微调开销。

Method: 1. 在多个相关数据集上联合训练PEFT模型；2. 推理阶段组合不同任务训练的PEFT模块权重矩阵；3. 推理阶段组合各PEFT模块的输出结果。采用QLoRA作为PEFT方法，在三个大语言模型上验证。

Result: 输出相加的组合策略表现最佳，显著优于其他组合方式；在单任务测试集上，三模块输出组合平均提升2%性能，且在情感、主题和多属性控制任务中均保持稳定优势。

Conclusion: 通过推理阶段组合多个独立训练的PEFT模块输出，可有效实现多任务泛化，显著降低微调成本，同时保持甚至超越单任务专用模型的性能，为高效多任务应用提供可行路径。

Abstract: Parameter-efficient fine-tuning (PEFT) techniques offer task-specific fine-tuning at a fraction of the cost of full fine-tuning, but require separate fine-tuning for every new task (combination). In this paper, we explore three ways of generalising beyond single-task training/inference: (i) training on combinations of multiple, related datasets; (ii) at inference, composing the weight matrices of separately trained PEFT modules; and (iii) at inference, composing the outputs of separately trained PEFT modules. We test these approaches on three different LLMs, QLoRA as the PEFT technique, and three sets of controlled text generation datasets for sentiment control, topic control, and multi-attribute control. We find that summing PEFT module outputs is a particularly strong composition method, which consistently either outperforms or matches the performance of alternative approaches. This is the case even when comparing against single-task specialised modules on the single-task test set, where three-module output composition achieves an average 2% point performance increase across all models for sentiment control.

</details>


### [149] [MedHopQA: A Disease-Centered Multi-Hop Reasoning Benchmark and Evaluation Framework for LLM-Based Biomedical Question Answering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12361)

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: MedHopQA is a disease-centered, multi-hop reasoning benchmark with 1,000 expert-curated questions requiring synthesis across two Wikipedia articles, designed to evaluate biomedical LLMs in reasoning over complex information. It uses open-ended answers and ontology-grounded synonyms for robust evaluation, constructed via human annotation and LLM-as-a-judge validation. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing biomedical QA benchmarks fail to distinguish between reasoning and pattern matching, suffer from performance saturation, and are vulnerable to training data contamination. Multi-hop reasoning—essential for clinical tasks like diagnosis and hypothesis generation—is underrepresented.

Method: MedHopQA was developed through a structured process including human annotation, triage, iterative verification, and validation using LLM-as-a-judge. Questions require integrating information from two distinct Wikipedia articles. Answers are free-text and evaluated using lexical and concept-level matches via MONDO, NCBI Gene, and NCBI Taxonomy ontologies.

Result: MedHopQA provides a discriminative, saturation-resistant, and contamination-resilient benchmark for evaluating biomedical LLMs. The dataset includes 1,000 scored questions embedded in a larger 10,000-question set with withheld answers, accessible via CodaBench.

Conclusion: MedHopQA establishes a new standard for biomedical QA evaluation by prioritizing compositional reasoning, resistance to model overfitting, and long-term validity. It also offers a reusable framework for future benchmark development.

Abstract: Evaluating large language models (LLMs) in the biomedical domain requires benchmarks that can distinguish reasoning from pattern matching and remain discriminative as model capabilities improve. Existing biomedical question answering (QA) benchmarks are limited in this respect. Multiple-choice formats can allow models to succeed through answer elimination rather than inference, while widely circulated exam-style datasets are increasingly vulnerable to performance saturation and training data contamination. Multi-hop reasoning, defined as the ability to integrate information across multiple sources to derive an answer, is central to clinically meaningful tasks such as diagnostic support, literature-based discovery, and hypothesis generation, yet remains underrepresented in current biomedical QA benchmarks. MedHopQA is a disease-centered multi-hop reasoning benchmark consisting of 1,000 expert-curated question-answer pairs introduced as a shared task at BioCreative IX. Each question requires synthesis of information across two distinct Wikipedia articles, and answers are provided in an open-ended free-text format. Gold annotations are augmented with ontology-grounded synonym sets from MONDO, NCBI Gene, and NCBI Taxonomy to support both lexical and concept-level evaluation. MedHopQA was constructed through a structured process combining human annotation, triage, iterative verification, and LLM-as-a-judge validation. To reduce leaderboard gaming and contamination risk, the 1,000 scored questions are embedded within a publicly downloadable set of 10,000 questions, with answers withheld, on a CodaBench leaderboard. MedHopQA provides both a benchmark and a reusable framework for constructing future biomedical QA datasets that prioritize compositional reasoning, saturation resistance, and contamination resistance as core design constraints.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 由高收敛性句子构成的段落显著提高答案准确率；按收敛性降序排列句子可轻微提升性能，表明模型更依赖早期信息丰富的提示。

Abstract: While Large Language Models (LLMs) are widely used in open-domain Question Answering (QA), their ability to handle inferential questions-where answers must be derived rather than directly retrieved-remains still underexplored. This study investigates how the structure and quality of passages influence LLM performance on such questions. We focus on convergence, a measure of how effectively sentences (hints) eliminate incorrect answers, as a criterion for constructing passages. Using subsets of the TriviaHG dataset, we form passages by combining sentences with varying convergence levels and evaluate six LLMs of different sizes and architectures. Our results show that passages built from higher convergence sentences lead to substantially better answer accuracy than those selected by cosine similarity, indicating that convergence captures meaningful relevance for inferential reasoning. Additionally, ordering sentences by descending convergence slightly improves performance, suggesting that LLMs tend to prioritize earlier, information-rich cues. ### [151] [Pretraining Exposure Explains Popularity Judgments in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12382)
*Jamshid Mozafari,Bhawna Piryani,Adam Jatowt*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究首次基于可完全观测的预训练数据（Dolma语料库）对大语言模型（LLM）中的流行度偏差进行了大规模分析，发现模型对实体的偏好主要由预训练期间的数据暴露决定，而非外部真实世界流行度。预训练暴露与维基百科浏览量高度相关，但模型对实体的判断更接近暴露统计，尤其在成对比较中表现明显，且大型模型和长尾实体中这一趋势更为显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解大语言模型中系统性偏好于知名实体的原因，特别是这种偏好是源于真实世界的流行度还是预训练数据中的统计暴露，由于多数训练语料不可访问，这一问题长期难以解答。

Method: 利用开放的OLMo模型及其完整预训练语料库Dolma，对7.4万亿个词元进行实体级暴露统计分析，选取2000个涵盖人物、地点、组织、艺术作品和产品五类的实体，将预训练暴露与维基百科页面浏览量以及两种大语言模型的流行度信号（直接标量估计和成对比较）进行对比分析。

Result: 预训练暴露与维基百科流行度高度相关，但大语言模型的流行度判断更贴近预训练暴露，尤其是在成对比较中；该现象在大模型和长尾实体中尤为突出，表明模型偏好主要由数据暴露驱动而非外部流行度信号。

Conclusion: 大语言模型中的流行度偏差主要由预训练数据中的统计暴露塑造，而非真实世界流行度，数据暴露是驱动模型偏见的核心机制。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) exhibit systematic preferences for well-known entities, a phenomenon often attributed to popularity bias. However, the extent to which these preferences reflect real-world popularity versus statistical exposure during pretraining remains unclear, largely due to the inaccessibility of most training corpora. We provide the first direct, large-scale analysis of popularity bias grounded in fully observable pretraining data. Leveraging the open OLMo models and their complete pretraining corpus, Dolma, we compute precise entity-level exposure statistics across 7.4 trillion tokens. We analyze 2,000 entities spanning five types (Person, Location, Organization, Art, Product) and compare pretraining exposure against Wikipedia pageviews and two elicited LLM popularity signals: direct scalar estimation and pairwise comparison. Our results show that pretraining exposure strongly correlates with Wikipedia popularity, validating exposure as a meaningful proxy for real-world salience during the training period. More importantly, we find that LLM popularity judgments align more closely with exposure than with Wikipedia, especially when elicited via pairwise comparisons. This alignment is strongest for larger models and persists in the long tail, where Wikipedia popularity becomes unreliable. Overall, our findings demonstrate that popularity priors in LLMs are primarily shaped by pretraining statistics rather than external popularity signals, offering concrete evidence that data exposure plays a central role in driving popularity bias.

While step-level analysis is commonly used to detect internal hallucinations, it suffers from limited granularity and poor scalability due to its reliance on step segmentation. To address these limitations, we propose TokenHD, a holistic pipeline for training token-level hallucination detectors. Specifically, TokenHD consists of a scalable data engine for synthesizing large-scale hallucination annotations along with a training recipe featuring an importance-weighted strategy for robust model training. To systematically assess the detection performance, we also provide a rigorous evaluation protocol. Through training within TokenHD, our detector operates directly on free-form text to identify hallucinations, eliminating the need for predefined step segmentation or additional text reformatting. Our experiments show that even a small detector (0.6B) achieves substantial performance gains after training, surpassing much larger reasoning models (e.g., QwQ-32B), and detection performance scales consistently with model size from 0.6B to 8B. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Estimating question difficulty is a critical component in evaluating and improving large language models (LLMs) for question answering (QA). Overall, Q-DAPS provides an interpretable, scalable, and bias-resilient approach to question difficulty estimation in modern QA systems.

### [155] [Stories in Space: In-Context Learning Trajectories in Conceptual Belief Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12412)
*Eric Bigelow,Raphaël Sarfati,Daniel Wurgaft,Owen Lewis,Thomas McGrath,Jack Merullo,Atticus Geiger,Ekdeep Singh Lubana*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出大型语言模型（LLMs）在上下文中更新行为可被视为贝叶斯推理，其潜在假设空间为低维几何结构——概念信念空间。通过故事理解任务，研究发现信念更新表现为在低维、有结构的流形上的轨迹，且这种结构同时体现在模型行为和内部表征中，可用简单线性探测器预测行为。对表征的干预可因果性地引导信念轨迹，其效果可由概念空间的几何结构预测。整体结果为LLMs中的信念动态提供了几何解释，将贝叶斯视角下的上下文学习建立在结构化的概念表征基础上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解大型语言模型在上下文中如何动态更新信念，特别是其背后的假设空间结构尚不明确，需要揭示其内在的几何与概念基础。

Method: 结合行为分析与内部表示分析，利用故事理解任务研究模型在上下文中的信念更新轨迹；使用线性探测器解码表征，并通过干预实验验证信念轨迹的可预测性与因果性。

Result: 1. 信念更新可被描述为在低维、有结构的流形上的轨迹；2. 这种结构在行为与内部表征中一致存在，且可通过线性探针预测行为；3. 对内部表示的干预能因果性地引导信念轨迹，其效果可由概念空间几何结构预测。

Conclusion: 本研究为大型语言模型中的信念动态提供了一个几何解释框架，将贝叶斯视角下的上下文学习建立在结构化的概念表征之上，揭示了模型内部信念演化的深层机制。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) update their behavior in context, which can be viewed as a form of Bayesian inference. However, the structure of the latent hypothesis space over which this inference operates remains unclear. In this work, we propose that LLMs assign beliefs over a low-dimensional geometric space - a conceptual belief space - and that in-context learning corresponds to a trajectory through this space as beliefs are updated over time. Using story understanding as a natural setting for dynamic belief updating, we combine behavioral and representational analyses to study these trajectories. We find that (1) belief updates are well-described as trajectories on low-dimensional, structured manifolds; (2) this structure is reflected consistently in both model behavior and internal representations and can be decoded with simple linear probes to predict behavior; and (3) interventions on these representations causally steer belief trajectories, with effects that can be predicted from the geometry of the conceptual space. Together, our results provide a geometric account of belief dynamics in LLMs, grounding Bayesian interpretations of in-context learning in structured conceptual representations.

### [156] [ORBIT: Preserving Foundational Language Capabilities in GenRetrieval via Origin-Regulated Merging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12419)
*Neha Verma,Nikhil Mehta,Shao-Chuan Wang,Naijing Zhang,Alicia Tsai,Li Wei,Lukasz Heldt,Lichan Hong,Ed Chi,Xinyang Yi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ORBIT 是一种用于缓解大语言模型在生成式检索任务微调过程中灾难性遗忘的新方法，通过监控模型权重与初始模型的差异并采用权重平均策略来限制模型漂移，有效保持了语言推理和检索性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决大语言模型在特定任务微调时快速遗忘其通用语言推理能力的问题，特别是在生成式检索任务中，防止因参数变化过大导致的性能下降。

Method: 提出 ORBIT 方法，实时跟踪微调模型与原始模型之间的权重距离，当该距离超过预设阈值时，采用权重平均策略来约束模型漂移，从而减少灾难性遗忘。

Result: ORBIT 在文本理解和检索性能方面均优于常见的持续学习基线和采用权重平均的正则化方法，有效保留了模型的通用能力。

Conclusion: ORBIT 通过动态控制模型参数漂移，显著缓解了大语言模型在特定任务微调中的灾难性遗忘问题，为保持模型通用性提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Despite the rapid advancements in large language model (LLM) development, fine-tuning them for specific tasks often results in the catastrophic forgetting of their general, language-based reasoning abilities. This work investigates and addresses this challenge in the context of the Generative Retrieval (GenRetrieval) task. During GenRetrieval fine-tuning, we find this forgetting occurs rapidly and correlates with the distance between the fine-tuned and original model parameters. Given these observations, we propose ORBIT, a novel approach that actively tracks the distance between fine-tuned and initial model weights, and uses a weight averaging strategy to constrain model drift during GenRetrieval fine-tuning when this inter-model distance exceeds a maximum threshold. Our results show that ORBIT retains substantial text and retrieval performance by outperforming both common continual learning baselines and related regularization methods that also employ weight averaging.

</details>


### [157] [Predicting Disagreement with Human Raters in LLM-as-a-Judge Difficulty Assessment without Using Generation-Time Probability Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12422)
*Yo Ehara*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新方法，用于预测大语言模型生成的难度评级中哪些可能与人类评分存在分歧，从而实现针对性重评。该方法不依赖生成时的概率信号，而是基于难度为有序尺度的特性，利用如ModernBERT等独立嵌入空间，通过评分集的几何一致性识别潜在分歧案例。在英语CEFR句子难度评估任务上，使用GPT-OSS-120B和Qwen3-235B-A22B进行实验，结果表明该方法在预测分歧方面的AUC优于基于概率的基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前利用大语言模型自动生成教育材料虽普遍，但其难度评级仍需大量人工参与；尽管LLM作为评判者受到关注，但与人类评分的分歧仍是主要挑战。现有方法依赖生成时的概率信号，难以跨模型比较且收集困难。因此亟需一种无需依赖生成概率、可有效识别分歧案例的新方法。

Method: 利用难度作为有序尺度的特性，采用独立嵌入空间（如ModernBERT）对文本进行表示，通过分析多个评分之间的几何一致性来判断是否存在与人类评分的潜在分歧。该方法不依赖生成过程中的概率信号，适用于不同大语言模型间的统一评估。

Result: 在英文CEFR句子难度评估任务中，针对GPT-OSS-120B和Qwen3-235B-A22B的实验表明，所提方法在预测与人类评分分歧方面表现出更高的AUC值，显著优于基于概率信号的基线方法。

Conclusion: 本研究提出了一种无需依赖生成概率信号、基于几何一致性的方法，有效识别大语言模型生成难度评级中与人类评分可能不一致的案例，为提升自动难度评估的准确性提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Automatic generation of educational materials using large language models (LLMs) is becoming increasingly common, but assigning difficulty levels to such materials still requires substantial human effort. LLM-as-a-Judge has therefore attracted attention, yet disagreement with human raters remains a major challenge. We propose a method for predicting which LLM-generated difficulty ratings are likely to disagree with human raters, so that such cases can be sent for re-rating. Unlike prior approaches, our method does not rely on generation-time probability signals, which must be collected during rating generation and are often difficult to compare across LLMs. Instead, exploiting the fact that difficulty is an ordinal scale, we use a separate embedding space, such as ModernBERT, and identify disagreement candidates based on the geometric consistency of the rating set. Experiments on English CEFR-based sentence difficulty assessment with GPT-OSS-120B and Qwen3-235B-A22B showed that the proposed method achieved higher AUC for predicting disagreement with human raters than probability-based baselines.

### [158] [Geometric Factual Recall in Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12426)
*Shauli Ravfogel,Gilad Yehudai,Joan Bruna,Alberto Bietti*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文探讨了Transformer语言模型如何记忆事实关联，提出了一种基于几何结构的新型记忆机制，而非传统的线性参数依赖的关联记忆。在单层Transformer中，通过极低维度的嵌入（对数级别）即可实现随机双射关系的记忆，其中主体嵌入为属性向量的线性叠加，小型MLP作为条件选择器通过ReLU门控提取相关属性，而非传统键值映射。研究扩展至多跳推理场景，证明存在容量与深度之间的可证明权衡，并给出信息论下界。实验表明梯度下降能发现符合预测结构的解，且训练后的MLP可在零样本条件下泛化到新双射关系，说明其学习的是通用选择机制而非具体事实。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为Transformer通过权重矩阵存储事实对，需要线性增长的参数量。但实际中模型以更高效方式记忆事实，需解释其内在机制，尤其在低维嵌入下的记忆能力。

Method: 理论分析结合实验验证：在受控环境中设计单层Transformer记忆随机双射任务，证明对数维度嵌入足以完成记忆；引入线性叠加嵌入与ReLU门控选择机制；扩展至多跳推理，构建无/有思维链的构造并分析容量-深度权衡；使用梯度下降训练模型，验证结构有效性并测试零样本迁移能力。

Result: 理论证明嵌入维度仅需对数规模即可实现记忆；实验证明梯度下降能发现符合预测结构的解；训练后MLP可零样本泛化至新双射关系，证实其学习的是通用选择机制而非特定事实。

Conclusion: Transformer语言模型通过几何结构化的嵌入编码关系，而非直接存储键值对；小型MLP充当通用的关系条件选择器，具有显著的泛化能力，揭示了模型高效记忆的本质机制。

Abstract: How do transformer language models memorize factual associations? A common view casts internal weight matrices as associative memories over pairs of embeddings, requiring parameter counts that scale linearly with the number of facts. We develop a theoretical and empirical account of an alternative, \emph{geometric} form of memorization in which learned embeddings encode relational structure directly, and the MLP plays a qualitatively different role. In a controlled setting where a single-layer transformer must memorize random bijections from subjects to a shared attribute set, we prove that a logarithmic embedding dimension suffices: subject embeddings encode \emph{linear superpositions} of their associated attribute vectors, and a small MLP acts as a relation-conditioned selector that extracts the relevant attribute via ReLU gating, and not as an associative key-value mapping. We extend these results to the multi-hop setting -- chains of relational queries such as ``Who is the mother of the wife of $x$?'' -- providing constructions with and without chain-of-thought that exhibit a provable capacity-depth tradeoff, complemented by a matching information-theoretic lower bound. Empirically, gradient descent discovers solutions with precisely the predicted structure. Once trained, the MLP transfers zero-shot to entirely new bijections when subject embeddings are appropriately re-initialized, revealing that it has learned a generic selection mechanism rather than memorized any particular set of facts.

</details>


### [159] [A Causal Language Modeling Detour Improves Encoder Continued Pretraining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12438)
*Rian Touchent,Eric de la Clergerie*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 通过在微调过程中临时切换到因果语言建模（CLM）并随后进行短时掩码语言建模（MLM）衰减，相比传统仅使用MLM的方法，显著提升了生物医学文本任务的下游性能。该方法在多个法语和英语生物医学任务中表现出色，尤其在低层Transformer中由CLM带来的密集监督更有效。冻结底层会消除优势，而冻结中间层则保留该优势。表示学习的变化在后续的MLM衰减阶段仍持续存在，并随模型容量增加而增强。研究团队发布了ModernCamemBERT-bio和ModernBERT-bio两个高性能生物医学编码器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统在新领域适应编码器时采用持续的掩码语言建模（MLM）训练，但其效果有限；本文旨在探索更有效的微调策略以提升模型在生物医学领域的表现。

Method: 在标准MLM训练前引入短暂的因果语言建模（CLM）阶段，随后进行短时MLM衰减，观察对下游任务的影响，并分析不同层冻结策略及表示学习变化的持久性。

Result: 在8个法语和11个英语生物医学任务上，该方法相比纯MLM基线分别提升+1.2-2.8pp和+0.3-0.8pp，且性能提升与模型规模相关。低层（0-7）受CLM影响更大，冻结底层会损失增益，而冻结中层仍可保持优势。表示学习变化在后续MLM阶段持续存在。

Conclusion: 临时采用CLM作为过渡策略并配合短时MLM衰减，是一种高效提升生物医学领域预训练模型性能的方法，尤其适用于深层模型。该方法揭示了低层表示学习对监督方式的敏感性，为未来模型微调提供了新思路。

Abstract: When adapting an encoder to a new domain, the standard approach is to continue training with Masked Language Modeling (MLM). We show that temporarily switching to Causal Language Modeling (CLM) followed by a short MLM decay improves downstream performance. On biomedical texts with ModernBERT, this CLM detour outperforms MLM baselines trained on identical data and compute across 8 French and 11 English biomedical tasks, by +1.2-2.8pp and +0.3-0.8pp respectively, depending on model size. We investigate the reasons for these gains. We find that CLM's dense supervision impacts low transformer layers (0-7) far more than MLM does. Freezing low layers during CLM eliminates the downstream benefit; freezing mid layers preserves it. The representational changes persist through the MLM decay phase, even when it matches the CLM phase in length, and they scale with model capacity. We release ModernCamemBERT-bio and ModernBERT-bio as state-of-the-art biomedical encoders in Base and Large sizes.

</details>


### [160] [The Algorithmic Caricature: Auditing LLM-Generated Political Discourse Across Crisis Events](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12452)
*Gunjan,Sidahmed Benabderrahmane,Talal Rahwan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究从计算社会科学视角出发，对比了真实与生成的政治话语在九个危机事件中的表现，发现尽管大语言模型生成的内容流利，但在情感强度、结构规律性、词汇-意识形态框架和跨事件依赖性等方面缺乏群体现实感。合成话语更负面、情感分布更集中、结构更规则、词汇更抽象，而真实话语则表现出更广泛的情感变化、更长尾的结构分布和更多情境相关的口语化标记。这些差异随事件类型变化：在快速传播、去中心化的危机中更为明显，在正式或制度化事件中较弱。研究提出‘漫画差距’（Caricature Gap）作为事件层面的量化指标，强调合成内容的主要缺陷并非语法或流畅性，而是缺乏群体真实性。该方法为评估生成文本的社会现实性提供了新的审计框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型能够大规模生成流畅的政治文本，其在危机和社交冲突期间可能引发虚假舆论的风险日益突出。传统AI文本检测依赖句级特征如困惑度、突发性或词元异常，但这些信号在生成技术进步后可能减弱。因此，亟需一种新方法来评估生成内容的社会现实性，特别是其是否符合真实在线群体的行为模式。

Method: 构建了一个包含1789406条帖子的配对语料库，涵盖九个重大危机事件（如新冠疫情、国会山骚乱、美国选举等），比较同一情境下真实社交媒体发言与大语言模型生成的合成发言。从四个维度进行分析：情感强度、结构规律性、词汇-意识形态框架、跨事件依赖性，通过均值差距与离散度证据识别差异。采用事件级指标‘漫画差距’总结差异，并进行跨事件比较。

Result: 合成政治话语虽然语言流畅，但整体上不符合真实人群行为特征。具体表现为：情绪更负面、情感分布更集中、结构更规则、词汇更抽象；而真实话语则具有更丰富的情感波动、更长尾的结构分布以及更多上下文相关的口语表达。这些差异在快速扩散、去中心化的危机中尤为显著，在正式或机构主导的事件中较小。研究提出的‘漫画差距’能有效量化这种非现实性。

Conclusion: 合成政治话语的核心问题不在于语言流畅性或语法正确性，而在于缺乏群体现实感。本研究提出以群体层面审计作为传统文本检测的补充，为评估生成内容的社会真实性提供了一种基于计算社会科学的系统框架。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) can generate fluent political text at scale, raising concerns about synthetic discourse during crises and social conflict. Existing AI-text detection often focuses on sentence-level cues such as perplexity, burstiness, or token irregularities, but these signals may weaken as generative systems improve. We instead adopt a Computational Social Science perspective and ask whether synthetic political discourse behaves like an observed online population. We construct a paired corpus of 1,789,406 posts across nine crisis events: COVID-19, the Jan. 6 Capitol attack, the 2020 and 2024 U.S. elections, Dobbs/Roe v. Wade, the 2020 BLM protests, U.S. midterms, the Utah shooting, and the U.S.-Iran war. For each event, we compare observed discourse from social platforms with synthetic discourse generated for the same context. We evaluate four dimensions: emotional intensity, structural regularity, lexical-ideological framing, and cross-event dependency, using mean gaps and dispersion evidence. Across events, synthetic discourse is fluent but population-level unrealistic. It is generally more negative and less dispersed in sentiment, structurally more regular, and lexically more abstract than observed discourse. Observed discourse instead shows broader emotional variation, longer-tailed structural distributions, and more context-specific, colloquial lexical markers. These differences are event-dependent: larger for fast-moving, decentralized crises and smaller for formal or institutionally mediated events. We summarize them with a simple event-level measure, the Caricature Gap. Our findings suggest that the main limitation of synthetic political discourse is not grammar or fluency, but reduced population realism. Population-level auditing complements traditional text-detection and provides a CSS framework for evaluating the social realism of generated discourse.

</details>


### [161] [Task-Adaptive Embedding Refinement via Test-time LLM Guidance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12487)
*Ariel Gera,Shir Ashury-Tahan,Gal Bloch,Ohad Eytan,Assaf Toledo*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种LLM引导的查询精炼范式，通过生成式大模型对少量文档的反馈来实时优化嵌入模型的查询表示，显著提升嵌入模型在零样本搜索与分类任务中的表现。实验表明，该方法在多个基准测试中均带来一致性能提升，最高达25%的相对改进，改善了排序质量并增强了嵌入空间的语义区分能力。该方法扩展了嵌入模型的应用场景，使其在无需大规模昂贵LLM流水线的情况下仍具实用性。代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有嵌入模型在复杂零样本任务（如文献搜索、意图识别）中表现受限，难以适应任务特定的细微语义需求。为提升其泛化能力，需引入动态适应机制以增强查询表示的准确性与任务相关性。

Method: 利用生成式大模型对少量文档进行反馈，指导用户查询的嵌入表示精炼，实现嵌入空间的实时任务自适应调整。该过程不依赖大规模标注数据，可快速响应不同任务需求。

Result: 在多个挑战性搜索与分类基准上，所有嵌入模型均获得显著性能提升，尤其在文献搜索、意图检测、关键点匹配和指令遵循任务中相对提升最高达25%；精炼后的查询提升了排名质量，并使嵌入空间呈现更清晰的二元分离结构。

Conclusion: LLM引导的查询精炼有效增强了嵌入模型在复杂零样本任务中的适用性，使其在资源受限或无法部署大规模LLM的场景下仍具备强大竞争力，为高效、低成本的智能检索系统提供了新路径。

Abstract: We explore the effectiveness of an LLM-guided query refinement paradigm for extending the usability of embedding models to challenging zero-shot search and classification tasks. Our approach refines the embedding representation of a user query using feedback from a generative LLM on a small set of documents, enabling embeddings to adapt in real time to the target task. We conduct extensive experiments with state-of-the-art text embedding models across a diverse set of challenging search and classification benchmarks. Empirical results indicate that LLM-guided query refinement yields consistent gains across all models and datasets, with relative improvements of up to +25% in literature search, intent detection, key-point matching, and nuanced query-instruction following. The refined queries improve ranking quality and induce clearer binary separation across the corpus, enabling the embedding space to better reflect the nuanced, task-specific constraints of each ad-hoc user query. Importantly, this expands the range of practical settings in which embedding models can be effectively deployed, making them a compelling alternative when costly LLM pipelines are not viable at corpus-scale. We release our experimental code for reproducibility, at https://github.com/IBM/task-aware-embedding-refinement.

### [162] [Steering Without Breaking: Mechanistically Informed Interventions for Discrete Diffusion Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10971)
*Hanhan Zhou,Shamik Roy,Rashmi Gangadharaiah*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了离散扩散语言模型（DLM）中的可控生成问题，发现传统均匀干预策略因未考虑不同属性在生成过程中的动态形成时间而降低质量，尤其在多属性联合控制时问题更严重。通过训练稀疏自编码器分析发现，不同属性（如主题、情感）的“承诺”时间分布差异显著：主题快速形成，而情感缓慢演变。为此，提出一种自适应调度器，仅在属性活跃形成阶段进行干预，避免资源浪费。理论分析表明，该方法的优势由承诺分布的方差决定。实验显示，在四种DLM和七个任务中，该方法实现精准控制，且在三属性联合控制下达到93%的控制强度，优于基线15个百分点，同时保持生成质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有控制生成方法在离散扩散语言模型中采用统一的干预策略，忽视了不同属性在生成过程中不同的出现时机与演化规律，导致控制效率下降，尤其在多属性联合控制时性能退化严重。

Method: 通过训练稀疏自编码器分析不同属性在扩散过程中的承诺时间分布；提出一种自适应调度器，根据属性形成阶段动态调整干预时机，集中于其活跃形成期，其余阶段保持不变；利用分散度统计量对控制成本与效果进行理论建模。

Result: 在四个不同规模的DLM（124M-8B参数）上验证，本方法在七项控制任务中均实现精确控制，尤其在三属性联合控制下达到93%的控制强度，比最强基线提升15个百分点，且生成质量无明显下降。

Conclusion: 统一的干预策略不适合离散扩散语言模型的可控生成，因其忽略属性动态形成特性。自适应调度器通过聚焦属性形成关键阶段，显著提升控制精度与强度，同时维持生成质量，为多属性可控生成提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Discrete diffusion language models (DLMs) generate text by iteratively denoising all positions in parallel, offering an alternative to autoregressive models. Controlled generation methods for DLMs, imported from autoregressive models, apply uniform intervention at every denoising steps. We show this uniform schedule degrades quality, and the damage compounds when multiple attributes are steered jointly. To diagnose the failure, we train sparse autoencoders on four DLMs (124M-8B parameters) and find that different attributes commit on distinct schedules, varying in timing, sharpness, and magnitude. For instance, topic commits within the first 2\% of denoising, whereas sentiment emerges gradually over 20\% of the process. Consequently, uniform intervention wastes steering capacity on steps where the target attribute has already solidified or has yet to emerge. We propose a novel adaptive scheduler that concentrates interventions on the steps where an attribute is actively forming and leaves the rest of generation untouched. The cost-control trade-off admits a closed-form characterization: the advantage of adaptive over uniform scheduling is governed by a single dispersion statistic of the commitment distribution. Across four DLMs and seven steering tasks, our method achieves precise control without the degradation typical of uniform interventions. Especially on challenging simultaneous three-attribute control, it reaches up to 93\% steering strength, beating the strongest baseline by up to 15\% points while preserving generation quality.

</details>


### [163] [Vertex-Softmax: Tight Transformer Verification via Exact Softmax Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10974)
*Navid Rezazadeh,Arash Gholami Davoodi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出Vertex-Softmax方法，通过证明softmax优化问题的最优解位于约束盒的顶点，并建立阈值结构定理，显著降低计算复杂度至序列长度的对数线性级别。该方法在不依赖下游目标的情况下提供最紧致的可证明边界，且在多个基准数据集上显著提升认证率和下界紧致性，同时远优于现有方法如alpha-CROWN和分支定界法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有验证器在处理transformer注意力机制时，对softmax函数的松弛独立于下游目标，导致不必要的松弛。为提高验证精度与效率，需更精确地界定softmax输出范围。

Method: 提出Vertex-Softmax方法，基于数学证明表明最优解必在约束盒顶点处，并利用排序后的系数结构缩小候选解数量，实现对数线性复杂度；结合CROWN凸松弛框架，保证形式化正确性。

Result: 在MNIST、Fashion-MNIST和CIFAR-10上的注意力模型中，该方法显著提升了认证准确率，大幅收紧了下界，且运行成本仅为alpha-CROWN和分支定界法的一小部分。

Conclusion: Vertex-Softmax是仅基于分数区间所能获得的最紧致的可靠边界，其性能极限由分数相关性和分数-值耦合等额外结构决定，未来改进需引入此类结构。

Abstract: Certified verification of transformer attention requires bounding the softmax function over interval constraints on the pre-softmax scores. Existing verifiers relax softmax ndependently of the downstream objective, leaving avoidable slack. We prove that the exact optimum of this score-box problem is attained at a vertex of the constraint box, and establish a threshold structure theorem showing that, after sorting the objective coefficients, the optimum lies among only linearly many candidates, yielding the Vertex-Softmax primitive with log-linear complexity in the sequence length. We further prove a formal optimality result showing that Vertex-Softmax is the tightest sound bound obtainable from score intervals alone, characterizing precisely what additional structure (score correlations, score-value coupling) is needed for further improvement. Integrated into a CROWN Convex Relaxation based Optimization for Worst-case Neurons)-style verifier with a formal soundness guarantee, Vertex-Softmax significantly improves certified rates and substantially tightens lower bounds across MNIST, Fashion-MNIST, and CIFAR-10 attention models, while consistently matching or outperforming alpha-CROWN and branch-and-bound baselines at a fraction of their cost.

### [164] [$ξ$-DPO: Direct Preference Optimization via Ratio Reward Margin](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10981)
*Zhengyuan Fan,Zhonghua Wu,Yuxuan Du,Qun Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对参考模型无关的偏好优化方法中，SimPO存在超参数$\beta$和$\gamma$联合调优困难的问题，提出$\xi$-DPO方法。通过重新构建偏好目标，将优化从最大化奖励差距似然转为最小化奖励差距与最优边际之间的距离，并引入比例形式的奖励边际$\xi$，使边际具有明确的相对分离意义且可直接由初始奖励差距分布确定，避免了繁琐的试错调参。

Method: 提出$\xi$-DPO：通过等价变换重构偏好目标，采用选择与拒绝响应的奖励比值形式定义新边际$\xi$，实现边际的可解释性与可设定性，消除$\beta$的影响并稳定优化过程。

Result: 实验表明，$\xi$-DPO在多个基准数据集上优于或相当优于SimPO，且无需复杂调参，边际$\xi$可基于初始奖励分布直接设定，显著提升效率与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: $\xi$-DPO通过引入可解释的比例奖励边际$\xi$，解决了SimPO中超参数调优难题，为参考式偏好优化提供了更稳定、高效的替代方案。

Abstract: Reference-free preference optimization has emerged as an efficient alternative to reinforcement learning from human feedback, with Simple Preference Optimization(SimPO) demonstrating strong performance by eliminating the explicit reference model through a simple objective. However, the joint tuning of the hyperparameters $β$ and $γ$ in SimPO remains a central challenge. We argue that this difficulty arises because the margin formulation in SimPO is not easily interpretable across datasets with different reward gap structures. To better understand this issue, we conduct a comprehensive analysis of SimPO and find that $β$ implicitly controls sample filtering, while the effect of $γ$ depends on the reward gap structure of the dataset. Motivated by these observations, we propose $ξ$-DPO: Direct preference optimization via ratio reward margin. We first reformulate the preference objective through an equivalent transformation, changing the optimization target from maximizing the likelihood of reward gaps to minimizing the distance between reward gaps and optimal margins. Then, we redefine the reward in a ratio form between the chosen and rejected, which effectively cancels the effect of $β$ and yields a bounded and interpretable margin. This margin is called the ratio reward margin and is denoted by $ξ$. Unlike the margin $γ$ in SimPO, $ξ$ explicitly represents the desired relative separation between chosen and rejected responses and can be determined from the initial reward gap distribution, avoiding repeated trial-and-error tuning. ....

### [165] [TMPO: Trajectory Matching Policy Optimization for Diverse and Efficient Diffusion Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10983)
*Jiaming Li,Chenyu Zhu,Zhiyuan Ma,Nanxi Yi,Youjun Bao,Li Sun,Quanying Lv,Xiang Fang,Daizong Liu,Jianjun Li,Kun He,Bowen Zhou*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为轨迹匹配策略优化（TMPO）的新方法，用于解决扩散模型在强化学习对齐任务中因奖励劫持导致的生成多样性下降问题。传统方法因追求高奖励路径而引发模式坍缩，而TMPO通过轨迹级奖励分布匹配替代标量奖励最大化，引入Softmax-TB目标函数，利用前向KL散度的覆盖特性保持多种可接受轨迹的分布，从而提升生成多样性。此外，为加速训练，还设计了动态随机树采样机制，共享去噪前缀并动态调度分支点，减少冗余计算。实验表明，TMPO在人类偏好、组合生成和文本渲染等任务上比现有最优方法提升9.1%的生成多样性，并在奖励与多样性之间实现最佳权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于强化学习的扩散模型对齐方法存在严重的奖励劫持问题，导致生成多样性下降和视觉模式坍缩，其根源在于方法倾向于最大化期望奖励而缺乏对可接受轨迹分布的有效约束。

Method: 提出轨迹匹配策略优化（TMPO），采用轨迹级奖励分布匹配取代标量奖励最大化；引入Softmax-TB目标函数，使策略对K条轨迹的概率分布匹配由奖励诱导的Boltzmann分布；结合动态随机树采样，共享去噪前缀并在动态调度步骤分支，降低大规模流匹配模型的训练时间。

Result: 在人类偏好、组合生成和文本渲染等多种对齐任务中，TMPO相比现有最优方法提升了9.1%的生成多样性，在下游性能和效率指标上均表现优异，实现了奖励与多样性的最优平衡。

Conclusion: TMPO通过轨迹分布匹配有效缓解了奖励劫持带来的模式坍缩问题，显著提升了生成多样性，同时保持高效训练能力，是当前扩散模型对齐任务中的先进方法。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) has shown extraordinary potential in aligning diffusion models to downstream tasks, yet most of them still suffer from significant reward hacking, which degrades generative diversity and quality by inducing visual mode collapse and amplifying unreliable rewards. We identify the root cause as the mode-seeking nature of these methods, which maximize expected reward without effectively constraining probability distribution over acceptable trajectories, causing concentration on a few high-reward paths. In contrast, we propose Trajectory Matching Policy Optimization (TMPO), which replaces scalar reward maximization with trajectory-level reward distribution matching. Specifically, TMPO introduces a Softmax Trajectory Balance (Softmax-TB) objective to match the policy probabilities of K trajectories to a reward-induced Boltzmann distribution. We prove that this objective inherits the mode-covering property of forward KL divergence, preserving coverage over all acceptable trajectories while optimizing reward. To further reduce multi-trajectory training time on large-scale flow-matching models, TMPO incorporates Dynamic Stochastic Tree Sampling, where trajectories share denoising prefixes and branch at dynamically scheduled steps, reducing redundant computation while improving training effectiveness. Extensive results across diverse alignment tasks such as human preference, compositional generation and text rendering show that TMPO improves generative diversity over state-of-the-art methods by 9.1%, and achieves competitive performance in all downstream and efficiency metrics, attaining the optimal trade-off between reward and diversity.

### [166] [AESOP: Adversarial Execution-path Selection to Overload Deep Learning Pipelines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10987)
*Tingxi Li,Mingfang Ji,Ravishka Shemal Rathnasuriya,Simin Chen,Yitao Hu,Wei Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了动态推理流水线中多模型组合的效率与安全问题，提出了一种名为AESOP的框架，通过路径感知攻击显著提升计算开销（最高达2407倍FLOPs），揭示了现有单模型防御方法在复杂流水线中的局限性。在真实系统部署条件下，即使存在批处理、缓冲限制和置信度阈值等防御机制，攻击仍能迫使系统在吞吐量崩溃或数据丢失之间做出权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代机器学习系统越来越多地采用动态推理流水线，其中上游组件的输出决定下游组件的工作负载，导致整体成本由多个组件的调用频率和单次推理开销共同决定。现有针对单个模型的攻击和防御方法无法有效应对这种耦合结构带来的新型攻击面，因此亟需新的分析框架来理解并应对路径选择层面的安全威胁。

Method: 提出对抗路径选择问题的形式化建模，设计AESOP框架，结合漏洞引导的路径排序与自适应损失加权策略，实现对最优攻击路径的智能选择和高效放大系统开销。

Result: 在五个不同流水线及一个生产级部署变体上评估，AESOP在白盒设置下实现最高2407倍FLOPs和419倍延迟膨胀；灰盒设置下仍达到58倍FLOPs和17倍延迟膨胀。即便在系统级防御下，攻击未被消除，而是被重定向，导致系统必须在吞吐量暴跌（从0.578降至0.006输入/秒）或96.7%数据丢失之间抉择。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了动态推理流水线中存在的路径感知攻击面，证明了传统单模型安全方法的不足，并展示了AESOP在实际系统中强大的攻击能力。这表明未来系统设计必须考虑路径选择层面的鲁棒性，以防止因恶意路径引导导致的系统级失效。

Abstract: Modern machine learning deployments increasingly compose specialized models into dynamic inference pipelines, where upstream components produce intermediate predictions that determine the workload and inputs of downstream components. The cost of processing an input is therefore not determined by any single model, but by two coupled factors: the per-inference cost of each invoked component and its workload volume. Because these pipelines run under hard real-time constraints, efficiency is a fundamental requirement for system availability. We show that this structure creates an efficiency-attack surface that existing methods targeting single models cannot exploit: on identical inputs and budgets, path-aware targeting inflates FLOPs by $2,407\times$ while the strongest single-model baseline achieves $117\times$ -- a $20\times$ gap attributable entirely to where the attack is directed. We formalize this as the adversarial path-selection problem and present AESOP, a framework combining vulnerability-guided path ranking with adaptive loss weighting. We evaluate AESOP on five pipelines plus a production-realistic deployment variant with batching, bounded buffering, and confidence-threshold defenses. AESOP achieves up to $2,407\times$ FLOPs and $419\times$ latency inflation in white-box setting and 58$\times$ FLOPs / 17$\times$ latency in gray-box settings. Under system-level defenses, the attack is not neutralized but redirected: pipelines are forced to choose between throughput collapse ($0.578 \to 0.006$ input/s) and $96.7\%$ data loss to sustain throughput.

### [167] [Test-Time Personalization: A Diagnostic Framework and Probabilistic Fix for Scaling Failures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10991)
*Linhai Zhang,Yulan He*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究测试时个性化（TTP），通过从个性化策略模型中采样N个候选并使用个性化奖励模型选择最优解来扩展推理计算。理论证明了理想选择下期望效用随采样数量对数增长，确立了测试时扩展的理论上限。然而，标准奖励模型无法实现这一潜力。为此，作者提出统一缩放定律，将任何奖励模型的Best-of-N曲线分解为四个可测量量，并揭示两种失效模式：用户级坍塌（某些用户预测几乎恒定）和查询级奖励欺骗（某些查询的真实质量负相关）。基于此定律，提出一种概率性个性化奖励模型，其学习到的方差有效缓解了这两种失效模式。实验验证了框架的有效性：TTP在多个策略模型和文本生成任务中表现出一致的缩放特性，且缩放定律与不同奖励模型变体的实际缩放曲线高度吻合。

Result: TTP在多种策略模型和个性化文本生成任务中表现出稳定且可扩展的性能增益；所提出的缩放定律能准确预测不同奖励模型的性能表现，实验证明该框架显著优于传统方法，尤其在高采样数量下优势更明显。

Abstract: Existing approaches to LLM personalization focus on constructing better personalized models or inputs, while treating inference as a single-shot process. In this work, we study Test-Time Personalization (TTP) along an unexplored axis: scaling inference-time computation by sampling N candidates from a personalized policy model and selecting the best with a personalized reward model. We prove that oracle selection yields expected utility growing logarithmically with the number of sampled candidates, establishing a theoretical ceiling for test-time scaling. However, standard reward models fail to realize this potential. To diagnose why, we derive a unified scaling law that decomposes any reward model's Best-of-N curve into four measurable quantities and reveals two failure modes, user-level collapse (near-constant prediction for some users) and query-level reward hacking (negative correlation with true quality for some queries). Guided by this law, we propose a probabilistic personalized reward model whose learned variance effectively mitigates both failure modes. Experiments confirm both elements of our framework: TTP delivers consistent scaling across multiple policy models and personalized text generation tasks, and our scaling law closely matches observed scaling curves across reward-model variants.

Abstract: We show that the core components of the Transformer block -- attention, residual connections, and normalization -- arise naturally from a single geometric estimation problem. Modeling the latent state as a direction on the hypersphere, with noise defined in the tangent plane at the current estimate, yields a precision-weighted directional inference procedure in which attention aggregates evidence, residual connections implement incremental state updates, and normalization retracts the updated state back onto the hypersphere. ### [169] [When and How to Canonize: A Generalization Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11008)
*Yonatan Sverdlov,Benjamin Friedman,Snir Hordan,Nadav Dym*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一个理论框架，用于分析通过群平均或规范化（canonization）实现不变性的非不变骨干模型的泛化误差。研究发现，规范化模型的误差界至多与结构不变或群平均模型相当，最差时等同于非不变基线模型。文中证明了存在最优规范化可达到最优误差界，而劣质规范化则可能退化为非不变性能。以点云处理中的置换群为例，证明字典序排序的覆盖数随维度指数增长，而希尔伯特曲线规范化保证多项式增长，首次为希尔伯特曲线在点云架构中的成功提供了理论支持。实验验证了理论结论。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建基于覆盖数的理论分析框架，通过数学推导建立规范化模型、群平均模型与非不变模型之间的泛化误差比较关系；针对点云处理中的置换群，具体分析字典序与希尔伯特曲线两种规范化方式的覆盖数增长行为。

Result: 1. 规范化模型的泛化误差界不超过结构不变或群平均模型，且可能退化为非不变模型水平；2. 存在最优与劣质规范化方式，其性能取决于规范化的正则性；3. 字典序排序的覆盖数呈指数增长，希尔伯特曲线规范化保持多项式增长，解释了其在点云模型中的有效性。

Conclusion: 该理论框架为规范化策略提供了严格的泛化性能分析工具，揭示了其性能依赖于规范化方式的正则性，并为希尔伯特曲线在点云处理中的成功提供了首个形式化理论依据。

Abstract: While invariant architectures are standard for processing symmetric data, there is growing interest in achieving invariance by applying group averaging or canonization to non-invariant backbones. However, the theoretical generalization properties of these alternative strategies remain poorly understood. We introduce a theoretical framework to analyze the generalization error of these methods by bounding their covering numbers. We establish a rigorous generalization hierarchy: the error bounds of canonized models are at best equal to the error bounds of structurally invariant and group-averaged models, and at worst equal to the bounds of non-invariant baselines. Furthermore, we show that there exist optimal canonizations which attain the optimal error bounds, and poor canonizations which attain the non-invariant error bounds, and that this depends on the regularity of the canonization. Finally, applying this framework to permutation groups in point cloud processing, we rigorously prove that the covering number of lexicographical sorting grows exponentially with point cloud dimension, whereas Hilbert curve canonization guarantees polynomial growth. This provides the first formal theoretical justification for the empirical success of Hilbert curve serialization in state-of-the-art point cloud architectures. We conclude with experiments that support our theoretical claims.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Long-horizon, sparse-reward tasks pose a fundamental challenge for reinforcement learning, since single-step TD learning suffers from bootstrapping error accumulation across successive Bellman updates. Actor-critic methods with action chunking address this by operating over temporally extended actions, which reduce the effective horizon, enable fast value backups, and support temporally consistent exploration. However, existing methods rely on a fixed chunk size and therefore cannot adaptively balance reactivity against temporal consistency. A large fixed chunk size reduces responsiveness to new observations, while a small one produces incoherent motions, forcing task-specific tuning of the chunk size. To address this limitation, we propose Adaptive Chunk Size Actor-Critic (ACSAC). ACSAC leverages a causal Transformer critic to evaluate expected returns for action chunks of different sizes. At each chunk boundary, it adaptively selects the chunk size that maximizes the expected return, supporting flexible, state-dependent chunk sizes without task-specific tuning. We prove that the ACSAC Bellman operator is a contraction whose unique fixed point is the action-value function of the adaptive policy. Experiments on OGBench demonstrate that ACSAC achieves state-of-the-art performance on long-horizon, sparse-reward manipulation tasks across both offline RL and offline-to-online RL settings.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联邦学习的性能受服务器端模型更新聚合策略的显著影响，而现有研究对不同聚合策略在多种数据分布下的系统行为和性能表现缺乏系统性比较，因此需要开展全面的实验评估以揭示其优劣与适用场景。

Method: 基于基准图像分类数据集，设计实验对比多种主流联邦聚合策略，分别在同质与异质数据分布条件下评估其在中央精度、损失及系统效率（聚合、训练、通信时间）方面的表现，通过定量分析揭示策略间的差异与依赖关系。

Result: 不同聚合策略在不同数据分布和数据集上表现各异，存在明显的性能-效率权衡；某些策略在高异质性下表现更优，而另一些则在同质数据中更具优势，且系统效率指标也随策略选择显著变化。

Conclusion: 联邦学习中的聚合策略并非普适最优，其效果高度依赖于数据分布特性与系统运行条件，应根据具体应用场景选择合适的聚合机制以实现性能与效率的最佳平衡。

Abstract: Federated Learning has emerged as a transformative paradigm for collaborative machine learning across distributed environments. However, its performance is strongly influenced by the aggregation strategy used to combine local model updates at the server, which directly affects learning performance, robustness, and system behavior. This work presents a comprehensive experimental comparison of widely used federated aggregation strategies under both homogeneous and heterogeneous data distributions. Using benchmark image classification datasets, we analyze how different aggregation mechanisms respond to varying degrees of data heterogeneity, examining their impact on centralized accuracy and loss, and system-level efficiency metrics, including aggregation, training, and communication time. The results demonstrate that aggregation strategies exhibit distinct trade-offs across datasets and data distributions, with their effectiveness varying according to dataset characteristics and operating conditions.

### [172] [LoopUS: Recasting Pretrained LLMs into Looped Latent Refinement Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11011)
*Taekhyun Park,Yongjae Lee,Dohee Kim,Hyerim Bae*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有循环计算方法需从头训练或进行破坏性改造，成本高且可能损害预训练模型性能，因此需要一种高效、低侵入性的后训练方案来提升大模型的推理能力。

Method: 将预训练模型重构为编码器-循环推理块-解码器结构，引入块分解（基于分阶段表示动态）、输入依赖的选择性门控、随机深度监督和置信度头以实现稳定循环与自适应提前退出。

Result: LoopUS在不增加生成轨迹长度的前提下显著提升了大模型的推理性能，同时避免了计算瓶颈和表征崩溃，实现了高效稳定的循环推理。

Conclusion: LoopUS成功将标准非循环模型转化为稳定高效的循环架构，为提升大模型推理能力提供了一种低成本、高兼容性的后训练解决方案。

Abstract: Looped computation shows promise in improving the reasoning-oriented performance of LLMs by scaling test-time compute. However, existing approaches typically require either training recurrent models from scratch or applying disruptive retrofits, which involve substantial computational costs and may compromise pretrained capabilities. To address these limitations, we introduce \textbf{Looped Depth Up-Scaling} (LoopUS), a post-training framework that converts a standard pretrained LLM into a looped architecture. As a key technical contribution, LoopUS recasts the pretrained LLM into an encoder, a looped reasoning block, and a decoder. It operationalizes this latent-refinement architecture through four core components: (1) block decomposition, guided by staged representation dynamics; (2) an input-dependent selective gate to mitigate hidden-state drift; (3) random deep supervision for memory-efficient learning over long recursive horizons; and (4) a confidence head for adaptive early exiting. Collectively, these mechanisms transform a standard non-looped model into a looped form while stabilizing it against both computational bottlenecks and representation collapse. Through stable latent looping, LoopUS improves reasoning-oriented performance without extending the generated traces or requiring recurrent training from scratch. For more details, see https://thrillcrazyer.github.io/LoopUS

### [173] [Enabling Performant and Flexible Model-Internal Observability for LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11093)
*Nengneng Yu,Sixian Xiong,Yibo Zhao,Wei Wang,Zaoxing Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Modern inference workloads require timely access to model internal states for monitoring, debugging, and optimization, but existing solutions introduce significant latency and memory overhead. The need for efficient, scalable observability without compromising performance drives the development of DMI-Lib.

Method: DMI-Lib uses Ring^2, a GPU-CPU memory abstraction, to asynchronously capture and stage tensors. An policy-controlled host backend exports these tensors, decoupling observability from the inference hot path. This design allows flexible placement of observation points across various internal signals and inference backends.

Result: DMI-Lib achieves only 0.4%--6.8% overhead in offline batch inference and an average of 6% in moderate online serving. It reduces latency overhead by 2x–15x compared to existing baselines with similar observability capabilities.

Conclusion: DMI-Lib successfully treats internal observability as a first-class systems primitive, enabling efficient, low-overhead monitoring of deep models across diverse inference scenarios while preserving performance and memory constraints.

Abstract: Today's inference-time workloads increasingly depend on timely access to a model's internal states. We present DMI-Lib, a high-speed deep model inspector that treats internal observability as a first-class systems primitive, decoupling it from the inference hot path via an asynchronous observability substrate built from Ring^2, a GPU-CPU memory abstraction for capturing and staging tensors, and a policy-controlled host backend that exports them. DMI-Lib enables the placement of observation points across a rich space of internal signals and diverse inference backends while preserving serving optimizations and adhering to tight GPU memory budgets. Our experiments demonstrate that DMI-Lib incurs only 0.4%--6.8% overhead in offline batch inference and an average of 6% in moderate online serving, reducing latency overhead by 2x-15x compared to existing baselines with similar observability features. DMI-Lib is open-sourced at https://github.com/ProjectDMX/DMI.

### [174] [Newton's Lantern: A Reinforcement Learning Framework for Finetuning AC Power Flow Warm Start Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11102)
*Shourya Bose,Helgi Hilmarsson,Dhruv Suri*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Neural warm starts reduce Newton-Raphson iterations for AC power flow, but fail on heavily loaded systems. This paper proves a lower bound on iterations dependent on error direction, not magnitude, showing failure near voltage collapse. To address this, the authors propose Newton's Lantern—a finetuning method using group relative policy optimization and a reward model trained on perturbations, with iteration count as feedback. It outperforms others across multiple benchmarks by consistently converging and minimizing average iterations.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing supervised neural warm starts generalize poorly on heavily loaded power system instances near voltage collapse, where the Jacobian becomes ill-conditioned. The motivation is to understand why these methods fail and design a more robust approach.

Method: The authors derive a theoretical lower bound on Newton-Raphson iterations based on the direction of warm start error. They then introduce Newton's Lantern: a finetuning pipeline combining group relative policy optimization with a learned reward model trained on perturbations of initial predictions, using actual iteration count as supervisory signal.

Result: Newton's Lantern achieves convergence on every test snapshot across IEEE 118-bus, GOC 500-bus, and GOC 2000-bus benchmarks, while attaining the lowest mean iteration count compared to all other methods.

Conclusion: The failure of supervised warm starts near voltage collapse is due to directional sensitivity in error, not magnitude. Newton's Lantern effectively addresses this by leveraging iterative feedback through a reward model, enabling robust performance even under extreme loading conditions.

Abstract: Neural warm starts can sharply reduce the number of Newton-Raphson iterations required to solve the AC power flow problem, but existing supervised approaches generalize poorly on heavily loaded instances near voltage collapse. We prove a lower bound on the Newton-Raphson iteration count that depends on the direction of the warm start error rather than on its magnitude, and show as a corollary that the bound becomes vacuous as the smallest singular value of the power-flow Jacobian shrinks, identifying the failure mode of supervised regression near the saddle-node bifurcation. Motivated by this analysis, we introduce Newton's Lantern, a finetuning pipeline that combines group relative policy optimization with a learned reward model trained on perturbations of the base model's predictions, using the iteration count itself as the supervisory signal. Across IEEE 118-bus, GOC 500-bus, and GOC 2000-bus benchmarks, Newton's Lantern is the only method that converges on every test snapshot while attaining the smallest mean iteration count.

### [175] [Language Modeling with Hyperspherical Flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11125)
*Justin Deschenaux,Caglar Gulcehre*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种新的基于超球面的流语言模型（$\mathbb{S}$-FLM），通过在单位超球面上旋转向量进行序列生成，避免了传统一热编码的高维开销和语义模糊的高斯噪声。该方法在推理任务中显著优于以往连续流模型，在大词汇量推理任务上接近掩码扩散模型的表现，但在低温度采样下仍存在差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有离散扩散语言模型因因子化分布限制表达能力，而连续流语言模型（FLMs）虽具确定性生成优势，但依赖高维一热向量表示，计算成本高且噪声添加缺乏语义意义。因此需要一种更高效、更具语义表达力的语言建模框架。

Method: $\\mathbb{S}$-FLM将语言表示嵌入到单位超球面$\\mathbb{S}^{d-1}$上，利用学习的向量速度场沿球面旋转生成序列，避免显式构造一热向量，并采用交叉熵损失训练速度场，实现高效、语义合理的生成。

Result: 在标准温度采样（T=1）下，$\\mathbb{S}$-FLM在数学与代码等可验证推理任务中显著提升性能，接近掩码扩散模型表现；但在优化后的低温度采样（T=0.1）下仍落后于掩码扩散模型。

Conclusion: $\\mathbb{S}$-FLM通过引入超球面表示与旋转机制，有效克服了传统流语言模型的计算瓶颈与语义缺陷，在大词汇量推理任务中展现出更强的生成能力，为非自回归语言建模提供了新方向。

Abstract: Discrete Diffusion Language Models progressed rapidly as an alternative to autoregressive (AR) models, motivated by their parallel generation abilities. However, for tractability, discrete diffusion models sample from a factorized distribution, which is less expressive than AR. Recent Flow Language Models (FLMs) apply continuous flows to language, transporting noise to data with a deterministic ODE that avoids factorized sampling. FLMs operate on one-hot vectors whose dimension scales with the vocabulary size, making FLMs costly to train. Moreover, since all distinct one-hot embeddings are equidistant in $\ell_2$, adding Gaussian noise does not have a clear semantic interpretation (unlike images, where Gaussian noise progressively degrades structure). We introduce $\mathbb{S}$-FLM, a latent FLM in the hypersphere. $\mathbb{S}$-FLM generates sequences by rotating vectors in $\mathbb{S}^{d-1}$ along a velocity field learned with cross-entropy, avoiding the overhead of materializing one-hot vectors. Previous FLMs match AR in Generative Perplexity (Gen.\ PPL), but samples with high likelihood are not necessarily correct in verifiable domains such as math and code. $\mathbb{S}$-FLM substantially improves continuous flow language models on large-vocabulary reasoning and closes the gap to masked diffusion under standard-temperature sampling ($T=1$), while a gap remains under optimized low-temperature ($T=0.1$) decoding.

### [176] [HEPA: A Self-Supervised Horizon-Conditioned Event Predictive Architecture for Time Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11130)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用基于联合嵌入预测架构（JEPA）的时序条件化预测器，在无标签数据上预训练因果 Transformer 编码器，学习未来表示而非具体值；随后冻结编码器，仅微调预测器以输出随时间递增的生存 CDF，实现事件预测。

Abstract: Critical events in multivariate time series, from turbine failures to cardiac arrhythmias, demand accurate prediction, yet labeled data is scarce because such events are rare and costly to annotate. We introduce HEPA (Horizon-conditioned Event Predictive Architecture), built on two key principles. First, a causal Transformer encoder is pretrained via a Joint-Embedding Predictive Architecture (JEPA): a horizon-conditioned predictor learns to forecast future representations rather than future values, forcing the encoder to capture predictable temporal dynamics from unlabeled data alone. Second, we freeze the encoder and finetune only the predictor toward the target event, producing a monotonic survival cumulative distribution function (CDF) over horizons. With fixed architecture and optimiser hyperparameters across all benchmarks, HEPA handles water contamination, cyberattack detection, volatility regimes, and eight further event types across 11 domains, exceeding leading time-series architectures including PatchTST, iTransformer, MAE, and Chronos-2 on at least 10 of 14 benchmarks, with an order of magnitude fewer tuned parameters and, on lifecycle datasets, an order of magnitude less labeled data.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 所提模型具备 $G$-等变性，可统一多种现有连续模型，为在齐性空间上学习向量值特征的等变动态提供几何基础。

Abstract: We introduce steerable neural ordinary differential equations on homogeneous spaces $M=G/H$. These models constitute a novel geometric extension of manifold neural ordinary differential equations (NODEs) that transport associated feature vectors transforming under the local symmetry group $H$. We interpret features as sections of associated vector bundles over $M$, and describe their evolution as parallel transport. This results in a coupled system of ODEs consisting of a flow equation on $M$ and a steering equation acting on features. We show that steerable NODEs are $G$-equivariant whenever the vector field generating the flow and the connection governing parallel transport are both $G$-invariant. Furthermore, we demonstrate how steerable NODEs incorporate existing NODE models and continuous normalizing flows on Lie groups. Our framework provides the geometric foundation for learning continuous-time equivariant dynamics of general vector-valued features on homogeneous spaces.

However, these models inevitably suffer from absolute boundary constraints during optimization. Conversely, without such constraints, relation regions expand indefinitely. To address the limitation, we propose \textbf{CORE} (Cyclic Orthotope Relation Embedding), a novel KGC model that embeds entities and relations onto a boundary-less torus manifold.CORE represents relations as cyclic orthotopes on the torus manifold, allowing regions to seamlessly wrap around spatial boundaries to ensure smooth gradient conduction. Furthermore, an adaptive width regularization is introduced to prevent unconditional region expansion. Theoretical analysis proves that CORE can capture various complex relation patterns such as subsumption and intersection. Extensive experiments on four benchmark datasets demonstrate that CORE achieves highly competitive performance, significantly improving link prediction accuracy in dense semantic environments.

### [180] [Unlearning with Asymmetric Sources: Improved Unlearning-Utility Trade-off with Public Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11170)
*Ahmed Mehdi Inane,Vincent Quirion,Gintare Karolina Dzugaite,Ioannis Mitliagkas*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为ALU的新型无监督学习框架，利用公开数据降低噪声需求，从而在保证模型效用的同时实现大规模高效删除。通过理论证明，公开数据可将未学习成本降低至$O(1/n_{\mathrm{pub}}^2)$，显著优于重新训练。即使存在分布偏移，该方法仍能有效防御隐私攻击并保持高实用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于噪声的认证机器遗忘方法因需高噪声而严重损害模型性能，尤其在大规模删除请求下更为明显；尽管公开数据在差分隐私中被广泛用于缓解隐私-效用权衡，但在遗忘机制中的作用尚未探索。

Method: 提出Asymmetric Langevin Unlearning（ALU）框架，利用公开数据注入来抑制遗忘过程中的隐私成本，通过不对称的朗之万采样机制实现高效且安全的模型遗忘。
