Abstract: Noise-based certified machine unlearning currently faces a hard ceiling: the noise magnitude required to certify unlearning typically destroys model utility, particularly for large-scale deletion requests.
  While leveraging public data is a standard technique in differential privacy to relax this tension, its role in unlearning remains unexplored. We address this gap by introducing Asymmetric Langevin Unlearning (ALU), a framework that uses public data to mitigate privacy costs. We prove that public data injection suppresses the unlearning cost by a factor of $O(1/n_{\mathrm{pub}}^2)$, guaranteeing a strict computational advantage over retraining. This establishes a new control mechanism: practitioners can mitigate the need for high noise-and the associated utility loss-by increasing the volume of public data. Crucially, we analyze the realistic setting of distribution mismatch, explicitly characterizing how shifts between public and private sources impact utility.
  We show that ALU enables mass unlearning of constant dataset fractions -- a regime where standard symmetric methods become impractical -- while maintaining high utility. Empirical evaluations using variational Rényi divergence and membership inference attacks confirm that ALU effectively thwarts privacy attacks while preserving utility under reasonable distribution shifts.

</details>

Abstract: We introduce SODA, a generalization of Optimistic Dual Averaging, which provides a common perspective on state-of-the-art optimizers like Muon, Lion, AdEMAMix and NAdam, showing that they can all be viewed as optimistic instances of this framework. ### [182] [Oversmoothing as Representation Degeneracy in Neural Sheaf Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11178)
*Arif Dönmez,Axel Mosig,Ellen Fritsche,Katharina Koch*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Neural Sheaf Diffusion (NSD) extends graph neural networks by using sheaf Laplacians with learnable restriction maps to adapt geometry to tasks. This work interprets NSD through quiver theory, linking sheaves on graphs to representations of incidence quivers. Learned sheaf geometries are viewed as points in a representation space, and their decompositions correspond to harmonic space splits in the diffusion limit. Oversmoothing is reinterpreted as degeneration of representations toward low-complexity summands that lose discriminative power. The paper connects sheaf diffusion to Geometric Invariant Theory, introducing moment-map-inspired regularizers for balanced geometries. It reveals a structural issue in uniform stalk architectures: equal dimensions force trivial summands onto stability walls, but non-uniform stalks remove this barrier, enabling adaptive stability. Experiments on heterophilic benchmarks support this—breaking symmetry improves performance and adaptive regularization works better in rectangular settings.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Oversmoothing in graph neural networks limits model expressiveness, especially in heterophilic graphs. Existing methods struggle to interpret or control this phenomenon algebraically. This paper aims to understand the underlying representation-theoretic structure of Neural Sheaf Diffusion (NSD), particularly how learned sheaf geometries affect the harmonic space in the diffusion limit, and to provide a principled way to mitigate oversmoothing via geometric regularization.

Method: The authors use quiver representation theory to reinterpret cellular sheaves on graphs as representations of incidence quivers. They analyze direct-sum decompositions of these representations and relate them to decompositions of the harmonic space. By applying concepts from Geometric Invariant Theory—specifically moment maps—they design regularizers that encourage balanced, stable sheaf geometries. A theoretical analysis identifies a structural obstruction in uniform-stalk architectures and proposes non-uniform stalk dimensions as a solution.

Result: The framework successfully reframes oversmoothing as representation degeneration. Experiments show that breaking stalk symmetry reduces variance and improves validation performance, and adaptive stability regularization is more effective in non-uniform (rectangular) architectures. Theoretical results confirm that non-uniform stalk dimensions avoid the stability wall issue present in uniform cases.

Conclusion: This work provides a deep algebraic understanding of Neural Sheaf Diffusion by linking it to quiver representations and Geometric Invariant Theory. It shows that oversmoothing arises from degeneration in the learned representation geometry and introduces a principled method to prevent it via moment-map-inspired regularizers. Non-uniform stalk dimensions are crucial for meaningful adaptive stability, offering a new design principle for robust GNNs.

Abstract: Neural Sheaf Diffusion (NSD) generalizes diffusion-based Graph Neural Networks by replacing scalar graph Laplacians with sheaf Laplacians whose learned restriction maps define a task-adapted geometry. While the diffusion limit of NSD is known to be the space of global sections, the representation-theoretic structure of this harmonic space remains largely implicit. We develop a quiver-theoretic interpretation of NSD by identifying cellular sheaves on graphs with representations of the associated incidence quiver. Under this correspondence, learned sheaf geometries become points in a finite-dimensional representation space. We show that direct-sum decompositions of the underlying incidence-quiver representation induce decompositions of the harmonic space reached in the diffusion limit. This gives an algebraic interpretation of oversmoothing as representation degeneration: learned sheaves may collapse toward low-complexity summands whose global sections fail to preserve discriminative information. Building on this viewpoint, we connect sheaf diffusion to stability and moment-map principles from Geometric Invariant Theory. We introduce moment-map-inspired regularizers that bias restriction maps toward balanced representation geometries, and identify a structural obstruction in equal-stalk architectures: when $d_v = d_e$, admissibility for learnable stability parameters forces the trivial all-object summand onto a stability wall. Non-uniform stalk dimensions remove this obstruction, making adaptive stability meaningful. Experiments on heterophilic benchmarks are consistent with this mechanism: breaking stalk symmetry can reduce variance or improve validation behavior, and adaptive stability becomes more effective in selected rectangular settings. Overall, our framework reframes oversmoothing as a degeneration phenomenon in the representation geometry underlying learned sheaf diffusion.

### [183] [Muon is Not That Special: Random or Inverted Spectra Work Just as Well](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11181)
*Zakhar Shumaylov,Nathaël Da Costa,Peter Zaika,Bálint Mucsányi,Alex Massucco,Yoav Gelberg,Carola-Bibiane Schönlieb,Yarin Gal,Philipp Hennig*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文挑战了非欧几里得优化中几何结构主导性能的传统观点，提出Freon（基于Schatten范数的优化器）和Kaon（随机噪声替代奇异值的优化器），实证表明即使缺乏精确几何结构，优化器仍可表现优异。最终指出性能主要由局部量‘对齐度’和‘下降潜力’决定，而非几何结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为非欧几里得优化的成功源于其与二阶方法及线性最小化预言机（LMO）理论的几何相似性，但本文质疑这一几何叙事，试图揭示真正影响优化性能的关键因素。

Method: 提出Freon，利用QDWH迭代逼近实现Schatten（拟）范数优化；引入无几何结构的Kaon，以随机噪声替代奇异值；通过随机特征模型分析局部量对优化性能的影响。

Result: Freon在GPT-2上最佳参数位于拟范数区域，无法用单位不变的LMO表示；Kaon虽无几何结构却媲美Muon；性能由对齐度和下降潜力决定，而非几何结构。

Conclusion: 优化性能的核心并非精确的几何结构，而是局部量对齐度与下降潜力的调控，关键在于步长选择的合理性。

Abstract: The recent empirical success of the Muon optimizer has renewed interest in non-Euclidean optimization, typically justified by similarities with second-order methods, and linear minimization oracle (LMO) theory. In this paper, we challenge this geometric narrative through three contributions, demonstrating that precise geometric structure is not the key factor affecting optimization performance. First, we introduce Freon, a family of optimizers based on Schatten (quasi-)norms, powered by a novel, provably optimal QDWH-based iterative approximation. Freon naturally interpolates between SGD and Muon, while smoothly extrapolating into the quasi-norm regime. Empirically, the best-performing Schatten parameters for GPT-2 lie strictly within the quasi-norm regime, and thus cannot be represented by any unitarily invariant LMO. Second, noting that Freon performs well across a wide range of exponents, we introduce Kaon, an absurd optimizer that replaces singular values with random noise. Despite lacking any coherent geometric structure, Kaon matches Muon's performance and retains classical convergence guarantees, proving that strict adherence to a precise geometry is practically irrelevant. Third, having shown that geometry is not the primary driver of performance, we demonstrate it is instead controlled by two local quantities: alignment and descent potential. Ultimately, each optimizer must tune its step size around these two quantities. While their dynamics are difficult to predict a-priori, evaluating them within a stochastic random feature model yields a precise insight: Muon succeeds not by tracking an ideal global geometry, but by guaranteeing step-size optimality.

### [184] [CATS: Cascaded Adaptive Tree Speculation for Memory-Limited LLM Inference Acceleration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11186)
*Yuning Han,Yangchenchen Jin,Dylan Zhao,Jingwei Sun*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CATS是一种自推测解码框架，专为内存受限的边缘设备设计，通过级联验证和修正机制，在不增加峰值内存占用的前提下，显著提升生成速度和吞吐量。它解决了传统推测解码在有限内存下无法同时加载目标模型与辅助模型的问题，实测在真实边缘设备上实现最高5.08倍的加速，且生成质量无下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推测解码方法依赖于充足的高带宽内存（HBM）以同时存放目标模型和辅助草稿模型，但在内存受限的边缘设备上这一假设失效。因此需要一种能在有限内存下高效运行的新型推理框架。

Method: 提出CATS框架，采用基于内存预算和参数卸载策略的级联验证与修正机制，动态调整草稿生成与验证过程，使峰值内存使用仅相当于目标模型自身大小。

Result: 在五种基准测试中，CATS在真实边缘设备上实现了最高5.08倍的时钟时间加速，相比当前最优方法提速达1.45倍，且生成质量未下降。

Conclusion: CATS成功在内存受限环境下实现了高效的自推测解码，为边缘部署大语言模型提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Auto-regressive decoding in Large Language Models (LLMs) is inherently memory-bound: every generation step requires loading the model weights and intermediate results from memory (e.g., High-Bandwidth Memory (HBM) for GPU servers), making throughput bottlenecked by memory bandwidth rather than compute. Speculative decoding addresses this by enabling parallel verification of multiple draft tokens, effectively amortizing the cost of each target-model call. However, existing speculative decoding methods are designed under the assumption that HBM is sufficiently large to hold both the target model and an auxiliary draft model simultaneously -- an assumption that breaks down on memory-constrained devices such as edge platforms with limited DRAM. We analyze the inference bottleneck in this memory-limited regime and propose CATS, a self-speculative decoding framework that conducts cascaded verification and correction based on the memory budget and parameter offloading patterns on memory-limited devices. This design maximizes token acceptance rate and end-to-end speedup while keeping the peak memory footprint on the device equal to that of the target model alone. We evaluate CATS on different models across five benchmarks on real edge devices. CATS can achieve a wall-clock speedup of up to 5.08x with no degradation in generation quality, outperforming the SOTA method by up to 1.45x under edge memory constraints.

### [185] [Variational Linear Attention: Stable Associative Memory for Long-Context Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11196)
*Vishal Pandey,Gopal Singh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出Variational Linear Attention (VLA)，通过将记忆更新重新建模为带有自适应惩罚矩阵的在线正则化最小二乘问题，解决了标准线性注意力中状态范数随序列长度增长导致的渐进干扰问题。理论证明了归一化写入方向可使递归雅可比谱范数恒为1，并保证状态范数在有界输入下自我限制。实验显示，VLA在长序列（T=1000）下将记忆范数降低109倍，实现近乎完美的多查询关联召回准确率，在内存负载增加时仍优于DeltaNet和标准线性注意力，且在每头容量边界保持62%准确率。Triton融合内核实现14倍加速，$\mathcal{O}(T)$扩展性使其在约43,000个词元时低于softmax注意力延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准线性注意力虽将复杂度从二次降至线性，但其记忆状态的弗罗贝尼乌斯范数随序列长度增长，导致存储关联间的渐进干扰，影响长期记忆性能。因此需要一种能控制状态增长并保持高记忆能力的新机制。

Method: 将记忆更新视为在线正则化最小二乘问题，利用Sherman-Morrison公式动态维护自适应惩罚矩阵；通过归一化写入方向，确保递归过程的雅可比谱范数恒为1，从而抑制状态发散。

Result: VLA在序列长度T=1000时，记忆范数相比标准线性注意力降低109倍；在有效每头记忆范围内实现接近100%的精确匹配准确率；在高内存负载下显著优于DeltaNet和标准线性注意力；在每头容量极限处仍保持62%准确率；Triton融合内核实现14倍速度提升，$\mathcal{O}(T)$扩展性使其在约43,000词元时超越softmax注意力延迟。

Conclusion: Variational Linear Attention通过理论保障状态稳定性与高效计算，实现了高性能、低内存增长的长序列建模，是线性注意力的重要改进，具备实际部署潜力。

Abstract: Linear attention reduces the quadratic cost of softmax attention to $\mathcal{O}(T)$, but its memory state grows as $\mathcal{O}(T)$ in Frobenius norm, causing progressive interference between stored associations. We introduce \textbf{Variational Linear Attention} (VLA), which reframes the memory update as an online regularised least-squares problem with an adaptive penalty matrix maintained via the Sherman-Morrison rank-1 formula. We prove that normalising the write direction to unit length gives the recurrence Jacobian spectral norm exactly $1$ for all sequence lengths and head dimensions (Proposition 2), and that the state norm is self-limiting under bounded inputs (Proposition 1). Empirically, VLA reduces $\|S_t\|_F$ by $109\times$ relative to standard linear attention at $T{=}1{,}000$, achieves near-perfect exact-match accuracy on multi-query associative recall within the effective per-head memory regime ($n_\text{pairs} < d_h$), maintaining substantially higher retrieval performance than DeltaNet and standard linear attention under increasing memory load, and maintains 62\% accuracy at the per-head capacity boundary. A Triton-fused kernel achieves $14\times$ speedup over sequential Python and $\mathcal{O}(T)$ scaling, crossing below softmax attention latency at approximately 43\,000 tokens.

*Noah Trupin,Yexiang Xue*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统投影方法（如末尾或每步投影）忽视了投影本身会改变状态分布，从而影响后续更新的采样动态，导致虽可行但不一致的样本。因此需要更精细地控制约束施加的时间点。

Method: 将约束强制建模为生成轨迹上的校正调度问题，利用一步约束缺陷作为局部几何失配信号，设计状态依赖的自适应校正策略，动态决定何时进行投影以最小化对采样轨迹的扰动。

Conclusion: 约束施加的时间并非次要因素，而应被视为生成采样中的第一类设计变量；仅保证可行性不足以维持预期的约束采样动态。

Abstract: Hard constraints in generative sampling are typically enforced by projection, applied either once at the end of sampling or after every update. This binary framing overlooks a fundamental issue: projection changes the distribution of states which future updates depend on. As a result, delayed projection can produce samples that are feasible but inconsistent with the intended sampling dynamics, even after final projection. We formalize constraint enforcement as a correction scheduling problem over the generative rollout. Using one-step constraint defect as a local signal of geometric mismatch, we introduce adaptive correction scheduling, a state-dependent policy that allocates projection budget to the steps that most strongly perturb the trajectory. Terminal and stepwise projection arise as limiting cases of this family. Across controlled manifold rollouts and a learned projected diffusion sampler, adaptive scheduling improves the cost-accuracy frontier at matched projection budgets, recovering 71.2% of full stepwise benefit with 75% fewer corrections. These results show that constraint timing is a first-class design variable in generative sampling, and that enforcing feasibility alone is insufficient to preserve the intended constrained sampling dynamics.

Thus, to improve refusal guardrails against such attacks without drastically increasing computational overhead, we introduce Retrieval Augmented Generation for Pref erence alignment (RAG-Pref), a simple RAG-based alignment algorithm which conditions on preferred and dispreferred samples to leverage contrastive information during inference. Abstract: Quantization is an effective strategy to reduce the storage and computation footprint of large language models (LLMs). Post-training quantization (PTQ) is a leading approach for compressing LLMs. Popular weight quantization procedures, including GPTQ and RTN, suffer in model utility, especially at aggressive quantization levels (sub-4-bit). We propose ADMM-Q, a novel weight quantization algorithm that considers the layer-wise quantization problem. Our algorithm is based on a combinatorial variant of the Alternating Direction Method of Multipliers (ADMM). Our operator-splitting procedure updates weights continuously to minimize the layer-wise reconstruction error, while gradually enforcing the quantization constraints with convergence guarantees. We propose additional algorithmic enhancements (e.g., penalty scheduling, preconditioning, and a local search post-processing step) to make ADMM-Q efficient at LLM scale. ADMM-Q is modular and can be used as a drop-in replacement for any weight quantizer within existing quantization pipelines: ADMM-Q is fully composable with existing techniques including range clipping, learned or random rotations, and activation scaling. ### [189] [LiBaGS: Lightweight Boundary Gap Synthesis for Targeted Synthetic Data Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11231)
*Abhishek Moturu,Anna Goldenberg,Babak Taati*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LiBaGS是一种轻量级、生成器无关的靶向合成训练数据选择方法，通过结合决策边界接近度、预测不确定性、真实数据密度和支持有效性来评分候选合成样本，确保所选样本既具有信息量又可能保持在真实数据流形上。它采用边界间隙分配规则，专注于稀疏但现实的决策边界邻域，而非简单增加数据或仅选择最不确定的样本。此外，LiBaGS通过边际价值停止规则判断何时停止添加合成样本，对模糊边界附近使用软标签，并利用多样性目标避免重复选择近似样本。实验表明，相比传统过采样、硬增强、不确定性与密度消融以及靶向生成选择标准，LiBaGS显著提升了准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 合成数据的有效性取决于其能否填补对下游任务重要的训练分布缺失部分。现有方法往往盲目增加数据或仅关注高不确定性样本，导致冗余或偏离真实数据分布。因此需要一种能精准选择有意义且符合真实数据结构的合成样本的方法。

Method: LiBaGS结合决策边界接近度、预测不确定性、真实数据密度和支持有效性对候选合成样本进行评分；采用边界间隙分配规则聚焦稀疏但真实的决策边界区域；引入边际价值停止规则判断停止添加合成样本的时机；使用软标签处理边界模糊情况；并通过多样性目标避免近似重复样本的选择。

Result: 在多个实验中，LiBaGS在分类准确率上优于经典过采样、硬增强、不确定性与密度消融以及靶向生成选择方法，证明了其在提升模型性能方面的有效性。

Conclusion: LiBaGS是一种高效、智能的合成数据选择方法，能够精准补充关键缺失数据分布，同时保持数据的真实性与多样性，显著提升下游任务性能。

Abstract: Synthetic data is useful only when the added samples fill missing parts of the training distribution that matter for the downstream task. We introduce LiBaGS, a lightweight, generator-agnostic method for targeted synthetic training data selection. LiBaGS scores candidate synthetic samples by combining decision-boundary proximity, predictive uncertainty, real-data density, and support validity, so that selected samples are both informative and likely to remain on the real data manifold. We then use a boundary-gap allocation rule that targets sparse but realistic decision-boundary neighborhoods, rather than simply adding more data or selecting only the most uncertain candidates. LiBaGS also learns when enough synthetic samples have been added through a marginal-value stopping rule, assigns softer labels near ambiguous boundaries, and uses a diversity objective to avoid redundant near-duplicate selections. Experiments show that LiBaGS improves accuracy over classical oversampling, hard augmentation, uncertainty and density ablations, and targeted-generation selection criteria.

</details>


### [190] [A Comparative Study of Model Selection Criteria for Symbolic Regression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11233)
*Ali Soltani,Gabriel Kronberger,Fabricio Olivetti de Franca,Mattia Billa,Alessandro Lucantonio*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究系统比较了多种模型选择准则在符号回归中的表现，发现MDL在多数数据集上能识别出测试误差最低、表达式最短的模型，且MDL和BIC对真实表达式的选取概率最高。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 符号回归中有效模型选择对平衡精度与复杂度、降低未见数据上的期望误差至关重要，但现有方法在自动选择泛化能力强的解方面仍存在挑战，尤其缺乏在不同数据条件下对各类信息准则的全面比较。

Method: 在七个含高斯噪声的合成数据集上，通过扰动真实函数生成候选表达式，并利用AIC、AICc、BIC、MDL及Efron自助法评估其预测误差，通过排名候选解并分析其泛化误差与真实表达式的选择概率来评估各准则表现。

Result: MDL在大多数数据集中表现出最低的测试误差和最短的表达式长度；尽管无单一准则全面领先，但MDL和BIC对真实表达式的选取概率最高。

Conclusion: MDL和BIC是符号回归中较为可靠的模型选择准则，尤其在提升泛化性能和准确恢复真实表达式方面表现突出。

Abstract: Effective model selection is critical in symbolic regression (SR) to identify mathematical expressions that balance accuracy and complexity, and have low expected error on unseen data. Many modern implementations of genetic programming (GP) for SR generate a set of Pareto optimal candidate solutions, but reliable automatic selection of solutions that generalize well remains an open issue. Current literature offers various information-theoretic and Bayesian approaches, yet comprehensive comparisons of their performance across different data regimes are limited. This study presents a systematic empirical comparison of widely used selection criteria: the Akaike information criterion (AIC), the corrected AIC (AICc), the Bayesian information criterion (BIC), minimum description length (MDL), as well as Efron's bootstrap estimate for the in-sample prediction error on seven synthetic datasets with Gaussian noise. We rank candidate expressions generated by perturbing ground-truth functions to assess generalization error and selection probability of the ground-truth expression. Our findings reveal that MDL consistently identifies models with the lowest test error and the shortest length across most datasets. While no single criterion dominates all results, MDL and BIC produced the highest probability of selecting the ground-truth expressions.

### [191] [Internalizing Curriculum Judgment for LLM Reinforcement Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11235)
*Han Zheng,Yining Ma,Karthick Gunasekaran,Bharathan Balaji,Zheng Du,Shiv Vitaladevuni,Cathy Wu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: METIS introduces an internalized curriculum learning framework for LLM reinforcement fine-tuning by using within-prompt reward variance as a metric for prompt informativeness. It predicts this metric via lightweight in-context learning and dynamically allocates training based on self-judgment, while jointly optimizing standard RFT rewards and self-judgment rewards to enable metacognitive learning. This closed-loop approach improves performance and accelerates convergence by up to 67% across multiple benchmarks.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Current LLM RFT methods rely on external heuristics or auxiliary models for curriculum judgment, which can misalign with the policy's training dynamics. There is a need for an internalized, adaptive, and efficient curriculum mechanism that aligns with the policy's learning process.

Method: METIS uses within-prompt reward variance as a proxy for prompt informativeness. It leverages recent training outcomes as in-context examples to predict this variance and guide dynamic training allocation. A self-judgment reward is introduced and jointly optimized with standard RFT rewards to form a closed-loop system enabling metacognitive learning.

Result: METIS achieves superior performance and up to 67% faster convergence across diverse RFT benchmarks including mathematical reasoning, code generation, and agentic function-calling, without relying on handcrafted heuristics or auxiliary models.

Conclusion: METIS establishes a simple, closed-loop, and highly efficient paradigm for internalizing curriculum learning in LLM RFT, enabling the model to learn what to learn next through intrinsic self-judgment and metacognition.

Abstract: In LLM Reinforcement Fine-Tuning (RFT), curriculum learning drives both efficiency and performance. Yet, current methods externalize curriculum judgment via handcrafted heuristics or auxiliary models, risking misalignment with the policy's training dynamics. In this paper, we introduce METIS (METacognitive Internalized Self-judgment), a novel framework that internalizes curriculum judgment as a native capability. Leveraging a critical observation that within-prompt reward variance effectively gauges prompt informativeness, METIS predicts this metric based on recent training outcomes as lightweight in-context learning examples. This intrinsic self-judgment then dynamically dictates the training allocation. Moreover, METIS closes the loop between judgment and optimization by jointly optimizing the standard RFT rewards and a self-judgment reward. This allows the policy to learn what to learn next, as a form of metacognition. Across extensive discrete and continuous RFT benchmarks from mathematical reasoning, code generation, to agentic function-calling, METIS consistently delivers superior performance while accelerating convergence by up to 67%. By bypassing handcrafted heuristics and auxiliary models, our work establishes a simple, closed-loop, and highly efficient curriculum internalization paradigm for LLM reinforcement fine-tuning.

### [192] [DeconDTN-Toolkit: A Library for Evaluation and Enhancement of Robustness to Provenance Shift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11237)
*Yongsen Tan,Zhecheng Sheng,Xiruo Ding,Serguei V. S. Pakhomov,Trevor Cohen*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 出处漂移（provenance shift）——即数据来源与标签之间的关系在部署阶段发生变化——在现有研究中缺乏充分理解与应对策略，亟需系统性分析与解决方案。

Method: 通过建立出处漂移与反事实不变性、不变学习之间的形式化联系，推导出鲁棒性学习目标；设计并实现DeconDTN-Toolkit，用于模拟不同强度的出处漂移，支持在不改变原有训练流程的前提下进行评估与修复。

Result: 发现经验风险最小化在出处漂移下表现脆弱；提出一种新的鲁棒性OoD性能评估指标；通过全面实验验证了多种现有算法的局限性，并展示了所提方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 本研究不仅从理论上阐明了出处漂移与不变学习的关系，还提供了可落地的工具与方法，为应对由出处混淆引发的模型鲁棒性问题提供了完整解决方案。

Abstract: Despite the burgeoning body of work on distribution shifts, provenance shift-where the relationship between data source and label changes at deployment-remains poorly understood and under-addressed. In this paper, we establish a formal connection between provenance shift, counterfactual invariance, and invariant learning to derive a learning objective for robustness. We then introduce \textsc{DeconDTN-Toolkit}, a specialized evaluation and remediation suite designed to simulate provenance shifts of varying degrees while maintaining the training protocol and the infrastructure of existing benchmarks. We reveal the vulnerability of Empirical Risk Minimization under provenance shift, introduce a robust out-of-distribution performance indicator, and conduct a comprehensive evaluation on existing algorithms. Our work provides both the theoretical grounding and the practical tools necessary to characterize the problem of confounding by provenance, and implementations of methods to mitigate it.

### [193] [Extending Kernel Trick to Influence Functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11239)
*Zhenhuan Sun,Shahrokh Valaee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了影响函数的双重表示，其计算复杂度随数据集大小增长，而非模型大小。该表示在模型规模远大于数据集时，或在参数空间中评估原始影响函数不可行时，可高效替代原影响函数以估计移除数据点对参数、模型输出和损失的影响。但该方法仅适用于线性化模型，且需存储一个大小与模型输出维度和数据集大小乘积成正比的矩阵。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当模型规模远大于数据集时，传统影响函数的计算成本过高，难以在参数空间中有效评估。因此需要一种计算效率更高的替代方法，特别是在大规模模型场景下。

Method: 提出影响函数的双重表示，利用模型的线性化特性，将影响函数的计算从依赖于模型大小转化为依赖于数据集大小，并通过构造特定矩阵实现高效估计。

Result: 双重表示在理论和实验上均证明了其有效性，能够高效估算数据点移除对模型参数、输出和损失的影响，尤其在大模型小数据场景下优势明显。

Conclusion: 双重表示为大规模模型中的影响函数提供了高效的计算替代方案，但其适用范围受限于线性化模型假设，且需处理较大规模的中间矩阵。

Abstract: In this paper, we present a dual representation of the influence functions, whose computational complexity scales with dataset size rather than model size. Both analytically and experimentally, we show that this representation can be an efficient alternative to the original influence functions for estimating changes in parameters, model outputs and loss due to data point removal, when model size is large relative to dataset size, or when evaluating the original influence functions in parameter space is infeasible. The dual representation, however, is limited to linearizable models, which are models whose behavior can be approximated by their linearizations throughout training, and requires materializing a matrix, whose size grows with the product of model output dimension and dataset size.

### [195] [Curriculum Learning-Guided Progressive Distillation in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11260)
*Jincheng Cao,Fanzhi Zeng,Leqi Liu,Aryan Mokhtari*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出CLPD框架，通过显式数据难度排序和隐式教师能力渐进调度，联合优化知识蒸馏中的学习顺序与模型容量匹配问题，显著提升小模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有知识蒸馏方法忽视训练数据的学习顺序和教师-学生模型之间的容量差异，导致强教师无法生成更优学生模型的反直觉现象。

Method: CLPD框架通过构建从易到难的数据课程，并逐步使用能力递增的教师进行监督，实现显式与隐式双课程引导的渐进式蒸馏。

Result: 在多个推理基准测试中，CLPD显著优于标准蒸馏、仅数据排序或仅教师调度的方法，证明了联合考虑数据顺序与教师容量的重要性。

Abstract: Knowledge distillation is a key technique for transferring the capabilities of large language models (LLMs) into smaller, more efficient student models. Existing distillation approaches often overlook two critical factors: the learning order of training data and the capacity mismatch between teacher and student models. This oversight limits distillation performance, as manifested by the counter-intuitive phenomenon where stronger teachers fail to produce better students. In this work, we propose Curriculum Learning-Guided Progressive Distillation (CLPD), a unified framework that explicitly accounts for both factors by aligning data difficulty with teacher strength. CLPD constructs an explicit curriculum by organizing training examples from easy to hard, while simultaneously applying an implicit curriculum over supervision signals by progressively scheduling teachers of increasing capacity. Our framework is modular and can be integrated into standard distillation algorithms with minimal overhead. Empirical results on the reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that CLPD consistently outperforms standard distillation, data ordering alone, and teacher scheduling alone across multiple settings. These findings highlight the importance of jointly considering data ordering and teacher capacity when distilling reasoning abilities into small language models.

### [196] [Latent Chain-of-Thought Improves Structured-Data Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11262)
*Carson Dudley,Samet Oymak*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文探讨了隐式思维链（latent chain-of-thought）在时间序列和表格数据上的应用，提出一种递归机制，通过将初始前向传播的查询位置隐藏状态压缩为反馈标记并追加到输入中，实现多轮潜在计算。在36个数据集上的实验表明，该方法在时间序列预测（8/9数据集表现更优，平均提升10.99%）和表格预测（22/27数据集表现更优，平均提升5.31%）上均显著优于基线模型，且整体性能最优，证明了思维链是扩展结构化数据测试时计算能力的有效途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究表明，思维链和测试时计算能显著增强语言模型的表达能力和推理能力。本文旨在探索这种机制在时间序列和表格数据中的适用性，特别是通过隐式思维链、深度和循环机制来提升模型对结构化数据的处理能力。

Method: 提出一种递归方案：先对结构化数据的Transformer进行一次前向传播，然后将查询位置的隐藏状态压缩为反馈标记，并将其附加到原始输入中再次处理，从而实现多轮潜在计算。对比了无思维链的同深度基线、深度匹配的更深基线以及权重共享循环但无额外思维链标记的模型。

Result: 在36个数据集（时间序列9个，表格27个）上，隐式思维链在时间序列任务中于8/9数据集上优于基线，平均提升10.99%；在表格任务中于22/27数据集上优于基线，平均提升5.31%。总体而言，思维链模型在两类任务中均表现最佳。

Conclusion: 思维链机制是一种有效扩展结构化数据测试时计算能力的途径，尤其在时间序列和表格预测任务中展现出显著优势。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought and more broadly test-time compute are known to augment the expressive capabilities of language models and have led to major innovations in reasoning. Motivated by this success, this paper explores latent chain-of-thought as well as the impact of depth and looping for time-series and tabular data. We propose a recurrent scheme in which a structured-data transformer, after an initial forward pass, compresses its query-position hidden states into feedback tokens that are appended to the input and processed again, allowing multiple rounds of latent computation before prediction. We compare CoT models against a same-depth no-CoT baseline, a deeper baseline matched to the CoT model in effective depth, and a looped transformer with weight-tied recurrence but no additional chain-of-thought tokens. Across 36 datasets in time-series forecasting and tabular prediction, latent chain-of-thought improves over the baseline on 8/9 time-series datasets (+10.99\% average gain) and 22/27 tabular datasets (+5.31\% average gain). Across both settings, the CoT models perform the best on average. These results demonstrate that chain-of-thought is a useful axis for scaling test-time compute for structured data.

</details>

Conclusion: Disentangling exposure bias from semantic supervision is crucial for fair and effective content ranking in global platforms; combining multiple sources of supervision with locale-aware design leads to better localization and overall ranking quality.

Abstract: Adobe Express is expanding internationally, but the US has a disproportionately large content supply and interaction volume. Learning-to-rank (LTR) models trained primarily on behavioral feedback inherit this imbalance: templates popular in US are over-served in non-US locales. This cross-locale exposure bias suppresses local content discoverability and degrades ranking quality in growth locales.
  We show that click-only training suppresses semantically informative localization features. Adding vision-language model (VLM) graded relevance labels as auxiliary supervision alongside clicks improves semantic alignment but does not preserve local content visibility. We propose a multi-objective framework combining behavioral supervision, VLM-derived relevance signals, and locale-aware boosting. Across five locales, the resulting model improves relevance while restoring stable localization, demonstrating the importance of disentangling exposure from semantic supervision.

### [198] [Beyond Similarity: Temporal Operator Attention for Time Series Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11287)
*Jevon Twitty,Vinh Pham,Nitiwith Rotchanarak,Viresh Pati,Yubin Kim,Shihao Yang,Jiecheng Lu*

TL;DR: TOA提出一种新的时间序列注意力机制，通过引入可学习的序列空间算子，解决标准注意力在处理符号和振荡变换时的局限性，显著提升模型在预测、异常检测和分类任务中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准注意力机制受限于凸组合形式，难以有效建模具有符号变化和振荡特性的时序信号，导致简单模型如MLP和线性模型在某些任务上仍优于复杂模型。

Method: 提出Temporal Operator Attention (TOA)，通过显式学习序列空间算子实现跨时间的符号混合，并引入随机算子正则化以稳定训练并防止过拟合。

Result: 在多个时间序列任务中，集成TOA的模型（如PatchTST、iTransformer）性能显著提升，尤其在重构密集型任务中表现突出。

Conclusion: 显式学习算子是构建高效时间序列模型的关键，能有效克服传统注意力机制的局限性。

Abstract: A persistent paradox in time-series forecasting is that structurally simple MLP and linear models often outperform high-capacity Transformers. We argue that this gap arises from a mismatch in the sequence-modeling primitive: while many time-series dynamics are governed by global temporal operators (e.g., filtering and harmonic structure), standard attention forms each output as a convex combination of inputs. This restricts its ability to represent signed and oscillatory transformations that are fundamental to temporal signal processing. We formalize this limitation as a simplex-constrained mixing bottleneck in softmax attention, which becomes especially restrictive for operator-driven time-series tasks. To address this, we propose $\textbf{Temporal Operator Attention (TOA)}$, a framework that augments attention with explicit, learnable sequence-space operators, enabling direct signed mixing across time while preserving input-dependent adaptivity. To make dense $N \times N$ operators practical, we introduce Stochastic Operator Regularization, a high-variance dropout mechanism that stabilizes training and prevents trivial memorization. Across forecasting, anomaly detection, and classification benchmarks, TOA consistently improves performance when integrated into standard backbones such as PatchTST and iTransformer, with particularly strong gains in reconstruction-heavy tasks. These results suggest that explicit operator learning is a key ingredient for effective time-series modeling.

</details>


### [199] [Quotient-Categorical Representations for Bellman-Compatible Average-Reward Distributional Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11289)
*Ege C. Kaya,Aliasghar Pourghani,Vijay Gupta,Abolfazl Hashemi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种平均奖励强化学习的商空间公式，通过将状态相关的偏差律在共同平移下等价化，并采用保持该对称性的分类参数化方法。在此商-分类空间中，定义了一个投影的平均奖励分布算子，证明其在坐标Cramér度量下是非扩张的且存在不动点。研究了以该算子为均值场映射的采样递推算法，在理想中心化奖励设定下，单状态TD更新在独立同分布和马尔可夫采样下均实现几乎必然收敛及有限迭代残差界；当收益未知时，引入在线收益估计器，证明了耦合方案的非扩张性与马尔可夫收敛性。最后表明，同步精确更新在商律层面上与收益无关，揭示了理想商分布与实际固定网格分类表示之间的结构性差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平均奖励强化学习中的偏差定义仅在加性常数意义下成立，导致直接的分布式类比在实线上不成立。因此需要一种能够处理这种对称性的新框架。

Method: 提出商空间形式化，将状态索引的偏差律视为在共同平移下的等价类；采用分类参数化以尊重该对称性；定义投影的平均奖励分布算子，并分析其性质；研究基于该算子的采样递推算法及其收敛性。

Result: 所提出的算子在坐标Cramér度量下是非扩张的，存在不动点；在理想中心化奖励下，一状态TD更新实现几乎必然收敛与有限迭代残差界；引入在线收益估计后，耦合方案保持非扩张性并可在马尔可夫采样下收敛；同步更新在商律层面不受收益影响，揭示了理想分布与实际表示间的结构差异。

Conclusion: 本工作建立了一个理论完备的平均奖励分布强化学习框架，解决了传统方法在偏差定义上的固有问题，为更稳健的分布式强化学习提供了新路径。

Abstract: Average-reward reinforcement learning requires estimating the gain and the bias, which is defined only up to an additive constant. This makes direct distributional analogues ill-posed on the real line. We introduce a quotient-space formulation in which state-indexed bias laws are identified up to a common translation, together with a categorical parameterization that respects this symmetry. On this quotient-categorical space, we define a projected average-reward distributional operator and show that it is well-defined, non-expansive in a coordinate Cramér metric, and admits fixed points. We then study sampled recursions whose mean-field maps are asynchronous relaxations of this operator. In an idealized centered-reward setting, a one-state temporal-difference update enjoys almost sure convergence together with finite-iteration residual bounds under both i.i.d. and Markovian sampling. When the gain is unknown, we augment the recursion with an online gain estimator, and prove non-expansiveness and Markovian convergence of the resulting coupled scheme. Finally, we show that synchronous exact updates are gain-independent at the quotient-law level, isolating a structural contrast between ideal quotient distributions and practical fixed-grid categorical representations.

### [200] [Optimal Representations for Generalized Contrastive Learning with Imbalanced Datasets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11291)
*Thuan Nguyen,Shuchin Aeron,D. Richard Brown,Prakash Ishwar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在类别不平衡情况下对比学习（CL）中最优表示的几何特性。当类别平衡且表示维度大于类别数时，已知最优表示会表现出神经坍缩（NC）现象，即同一类别的表示坍缩到其类均值，且类均值构成等角紧框架（ETF）。对于类别不平衡和一类广义的CL损失函数，本文证明了同一类别的所有样本的最优表示会坍缩到其类均值，并呈现出由类别比例决定的角对称结构。总体而言，该几何结构可通过求解一个凸优化问题来确定。利用这一对称结构，文章进一步分析了极端类别不平衡情形，证明了当类别不平衡超过某一阈值时，对比学习会出现少数类坍缩（Minority Collapse, MC）现象，即所有少数类样本坍缩为单一向量，该阈值取决于损失函数的正则性特征和负样本数量。数值实验验证了理论结果。最后，文章提出若干开放性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究对比学习在类别不平衡条件下的最优表示几何特性，揭示其内在机制并发现新的现象如少数类坍缩（MC），以指导实际应用中的模型设计与改进。

Method: 通过构建并求解一个凸优化问题，推导出在类别不平衡条件下最优表示的几何结构；利用对称性分析极端不平衡情形，结合数学推导和数值模拟验证理论结论。

Result: 在类别不平衡条件下，最优表示呈现由类别比例决定的角对称结构；当类别不平衡超过阈值时，出现少数类坍缩（MC）现象，即所有少数类样本坍缩为同一向量；数值实验支持理论分析。

Conclusion: 对比学习在类别不平衡下具有可计算的几何结构，其行为受类别比例、损失函数性质及负样本数量影响；少数类坍缩是潜在风险，需在实践中加以关注；本文提出了若干待解决的开放问题。

Abstract: In this paper, we provide a computable characterization of the geometry of optimal representations in Contrastive Learning (CL) when the classes are imbalanced. When classes are balanced and the representation dimension is greater than the number of classes, it is well-known that the optimal representations exhibit Neural Collapse (NC), i.e., representations from the same class collapse to their class means and the class means form an Equiangular Tight Frame (ETF). For imbalanced classes and a large, generalized family of CL losses, we prove that the optimal representations of all samples from the same class collapse to their class means and their geometry exhibits an angular symmetry structure that is determined by the relative class proportions. In general, we show that the geometry can be determined by solving a convex optimization problem. Exploiting this symmetry structure, we analytically investigate a special case where class imbalance is extreme and prove that CL exhibits a phenomenon called Minority Collapse (MC) where all samples from the minority classes (classes with small probabilities) collapse into a single vector, whenever the class imbalance exceeds a threshold, which in turn depends on the regularity properties of the CL loss used and on the number of negative samples. Numerical results are provided to illustrate these phenomena and corroborate the theoretical results. We conclude by identifying a number of open problems.

### [201] [Primal Generation, Dual Judgment: Self-Training from Test-Time Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11299)
*Yizhu Jiao,Ruixiang Zhang,Richard Bai,Jiawei Han,Ronan Collobert,Yizhe Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DuST提出一种从双重判断空间进行自训练的框架，通过模型自身生成候选程序并基于沙盒执行结果构建包含成功与失败样本的组别，利用GRPO进行排序训练，使模型学习相对正确性结构。该方法不直接奖励正确生成，而是通过判别式目标提升判断与生成能力。在多个模型上，DuST显著提升测试时缩放性能，如Qwen3-30B-Thinking在LiveCodeBench v6上判断质量提升+6.2 NDCG，单样本通过率提升+3.1，Best-of-4准确率提升+4.1，且单次推理表现达到基线模型Best-of-4水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统代码生成依赖稀疏执行反馈（仅通过/失败），信息利用率低；测试时扩展虽增加候选样本，但比较信息被丢弃。本文认为这些比较信息构成更丰富的双重判断空间，可提供更强训练信号，帮助模型理解不同候选间的相对正确性差异，从而提升判断与生成能力。

Method: 提出DuST框架：从模型自身分布采样候选程序，经沙盒执行后保留同时含成功与失败样本的组别，使用GRPO算法训练模型对候选程序按执行正确性进行排序，目标为纯粹判别式，不直接奖励正确生成。

Result: 在五个不同规模和架构的模型上，DuST一致提升Best-of-4测试时缩放效果；以Qwen3-30B-Thinking为例，在LiveCodeBench v6上，判断质量提升+6.2 NDCG，单样本pass@1提升+3.1，Best-of-4准确率提升+4.1；单次推理表现相当于原模型的Best-of-4性能。监督微调（SFT）仅提升判断能力而不改善生成，说明强化学习（RL）是将双空间学习转化为生成能力的关键机制。

Conclusion: DuST通过挖掘模型自身生成中的相对正确性信息，构建双重判断空间，实现高效的自训练。其核心在于利用对比信息而非孤立反馈，显著提升代码生成与判断性能。实验表明，基于策略的强化学习是实现生成能力迁移的关键，证明了双重空间学习的有效性与普适性。

Abstract: Code generation is typically trained in the primal space of programs: a model produces a candidate solution and receives sparse execution feedback, often a single pass/fail bit. Test-time scaling enriches the inference procedure by sampling multiple candidates and judging among them, but the comparative information this process reveals is discarded after inference. We argue that this information defines a dual judgment space that provides a far richer training signal: the model learns not from an isolated success or failure, but from the relative correctness structure across its own plausible attempts, identifying which succeed, which fail, and what distinguishes them. We introduce DuST (Dual Self-Training), a framework for self-training from the dual judgment space. DuST samples candidate programs from the model's own distribution, labels them through sandbox execution, retains groups containing both successes and failures, and trains the model to rank candidates by execution correctness using GRPO. The objective is purely discriminative: the model is never directly rewarded for generating correct programs. Dual self-training improves both judgment and generation. Across five models spanning two families and three scales (4B to 30B), DuST consistently improves Best-of-4 test-time scaling on LiveCodeBench. For Qwen3-30B-Thinking on LiveCodeBench v6, judgment quality improves by +6.2 NDCG, single-sample pass@1 improves by +3.1, and Best-of-4 accuracy improves by +4.1. The trained model's single rollout matches the base model's Best-of-4 performance. SFT on the same ranking data improves judgment without improving generation, confirming that on-policy RL is the mechanism that transfers dual-space learning back into primal generation.

### [202] [A Theory of Time-Sensitive Language Generation: Sparse Hallucination Beats Mode Collapse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11302)
*Atul Ganju,Travis McVoy,Shaddin Dughmi,Shang-Hua Teng*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在语言生成中，除了追求输出的广度外，还希望高优先级的字符串能尽早生成，这符合机器学习中对‘简单’或‘合理’输出的归纳偏置。然而，如何在保证质量的同时实现及时生成，是一个关键挑战。

Method: 采用全局偏好排序模型，定义字符串的截止时间与其排名相关。分析最终一致生成器的局限性，引入幻觉率随时间趋于零的弱一致性假设，进而构造满足超线性截止时间下的最优生成策略，并通过反例证明线性截止时间下无法实现及时生成。

Result: 最终一致生成器无法实现及时生成；但在幻觉率趋于零的条件下，可实现超线性截止时间下的最优密度生成，且该结果在理论上是紧的，即线性截止时间下无法做到。

Conclusion: 及时生成在强一致性假设下不可行，但通过放宽为渐近无幻觉的生成机制，可在超线性截止时间下实现最优生成性能，揭示了生成效率与一致性之间的根本权衡。

Abstract: We study language generation in the limit under a global preference ordering on strings, as introduced by Kleinberg and Wei. As in [arXiv:2504.14370, arXiv:2511.05295], we aim for \emph{breadth}, but impose an additional requirement of timeliness: higher-ranked strings should be generated earlier. A string is then only credited if it is generated before a deadline, where its deadline is defined by a function that maps a string's rank in the target language to the time by which it must be produced. This is in keeping with a central consideration in machine learning, where inductive bias favors ``simpler'' or ``more plausible'' outputs, all else being equal. We show that timely generation is impossible in a strong sense for eventually consistent generators -- the protagonists of most prior related work. Under what is perhaps the mildest natural relaxation of consistency, a hallucination rate that vanishes over time, we show that we can circumvent our impossibility result. In particular, we can achieve optimal density with respect to any superlinear deadline function. We also show this is tight by ruling out timely generation with linear deadlines and vanishing hallucination rate.

Abstract: Diffusion models typically generate image batches from independent Gaussian initial noises. We argue that this independence assumption is only one choice within a broader class of valid joint noise designs. Instead, one can specify a coupling of the initial noises: each noise remains marginally standard Gaussian, so the pretrained diffusion model receives the same single-sample input distribution, while the dependence across samples is chosen by design. This reframes initial-noise control from selecting or optimizing individual seeds to designing the dependence structure of a multi-sample gallery. This view gives a general framework for initial-noise design, covering several existing methods as special cases and leading naturally to new coupled-noise constructions. Coupled noise can improve generation on its own without adding sampling cost, and it is flexible enough to serve as a structured initialization for optimization-based pipelines when additional computation is available. Empirically, repulsive Gaussian coupling improves gallery diversity on SD1.5, SDXL, and SD3 while largely preserving prompt alignment and image quality. It matches or outperforms recent test-time noise-optimization baselines on several diversity metrics at the same sampling cost as independent generation. Subspace couplings also support fixed-object background generation, producing diverse, natural backgrounds compared with specialized inpainting baselines, with a tunable trade-off in foreground fidelity.

### [204] [Error whitening: Why Gauss-Newton outperforms Newton](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11316)
*Maricela Best McKay,Nathan P. Lawrence,Brian Wetton,R. Bhushan Gopaluni*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Gauss-Newton descent outperforms Newton's method by projecting the Newton direction onto the model's tangent space, eliminating distortions from parameterization through a process called 'error whitening.' This leads to more stable and efficient optimization dynamics in function space, validated across diverse applications.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Despite Gauss-Newton being viewed as a positive semidefinite approximation of the Hessian, empirical results show it often outperforms Newton's method. The motivation is to understand why this happens by analyzing optimization dynamics from a function space perspective.

Method: The study uses a function space analysis to examine how the generalized Gauss-Newton (GGN) matrix and Jacobian-only variants project gradients and directions onto the model's tangent space, effectively removing parameterization-induced distortions via error whitening.

Result: Empirical results confirm that Gauss-Newton optimizers follow the predicted function space dynamics and consistently outperform Newton's method, Adam, and Muon across supervised learning, physics-informed deep learning, and approximate dynamic programming tasks.

Conclusion: Error whitening—achieved by projecting onto the tangent space—explains the superior performance of Gauss-Newton methods over Newton's method and other optimizers, highlighting a fundamental distinction rooted in function space dynamics.

Abstract: The Gauss-Newton matrix is widely viewed as a positive semidefinite approximation of the Hessian, yet mounting empirical evidence shows that Gauss-Newton descent outperforms Newton's method. We adopt a function space perspective to analyze this phenomenon. We show that the generalized Gauss-Newton (GGN) matrix projects the Newton direction in function space onto the model's tangent space, while a Jacobian-only variant obtained by applying the least squares Gauss-Newton matrix to non-least squares losses projects the function space loss gradient onto this same tangent space. Both projections eliminate distortions from the model's parameterization. Specifically, the evolution of the prediction-target mismatch depends on the model's parameterization through the matrix $JJ^\top$ where $J$ is the Jacobian of the model with respect to its parameters. The projections effectively replace $JJ^\top$ with the identity. We call this effect error whitening. Once the parameterization is removed, the prediction-target mismatch evolves according to dynamics dictated by the structure of the loss and the projection produced by the optimizer. Error whitening is a special property of Gauss-Newton descent that rigorously distinguishes it from Newton's method. We empirically demonstrate that Gauss-Newton optimizers follow the theoretically predicted function space dynamics and outperforms Newton's method, Adam, and Muon across case studies spanning supervised learning, physics-informed deep learning, and approximate dynamic programming.

</details>


### [205] [$\varepsilon$-Good Action Identification in Fixed-Budget Monte Carlo Tree Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11324)
*Yinan Li,Tuan Nguyen,Kwang-Sung Jun*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究深度为2的max-min树中的固定预算最大最小动作识别问题，提出一种不依赖于$\varepsilon$的算法，实现了对任意合理$\varepsilon$的实例相关误差界，并证明了错误识别概率以$\exp(-\widetildeΘ(T/H_2(\varepsilon)))$速率衰减。该方法在单叶子树情形下恢复了已知结果，并为Successive Rejects提供了新的$\varepsilon$-好保证。同时给出了上下界分析，揭示其与标准$K$臂赌博机不同的困难结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受近似规划启发，关注$\varepsilon$-好子树识别，即识别出最小值接近最优最大最小值的子树，旨在提升蒙特卡洛树搜索中决策效率。

Method: 提出一种$\varepsilon$-无关算法，通过分析跨子树与子树内间隙的综合度量$H_2(\varepsilon)$，实现自适应误差控制，并结合上下界分析验证其有效性。

Result: 算法在固定预算$T$下，错误识别概率以$\exp(-\widetildeΘ(T/H_2(\varepsilon)))$指数下降；当每个子树仅含一个叶子时，可恢复现有$\varepsilon$-好结果，并首次为Successive Rejects提供$\varepsilon$-好保证。

Conclusion: 本工作首次提供了针对max-min动作识别的严格固定预算算法保证，揭示了其与传统$K$臂赌博机不同的复杂性结构，具有理论和实践意义。

Abstract: We study the fixed-budget max-min action identification problem in depth-2 max-min trees, an important special case of Monte Carlo Tree Search. A learner sequentially allocates $T$ samples to leaves and then recommends a subtree whose minimum leaf value is largest. Motivated by approximate planning, we focus on $\varepsilon$-good subtree identification, where any subtree whose min value is within $\varepsilon$ of the optimal maximin value is acceptable.
  Our main contribution is an $\varepsilon$-agnostic algorithm: it does not require $\varepsilon$ as input, but achieves instance-dependent error bounds for every meaningful $\varepsilon$. We show that the misidentification probability decays as $\exp(-\widetildeΘ(T/H_2(\varepsilon)))$, where $H_2(\varepsilon)$ captures both cross-subtree and within-subtree gaps. When each subtree has a single leaf, the problem reduces to standard fixed-budget best-arm identification, and our analysis recovers, up to accelerating factors, known $\varepsilon$-good guarantees for halving-style methods while giving a new $\varepsilon$-good guarantee for Successive Rejects.
  On the lower-bound side, we provide complementary positive and negative results showing that max-min identification has a different hardness structure from standard $K$-armed bandits. To our knowledge, this is the first provable fixed-budget algorithmic guarantee for max-min action identification.

</details>

Abstract: Classical deep learning typically operates on individual cases. Despite its success, real-world usage often requires repeated inference to estimate statistical quantities for complex decision-making tasks involving uncertainty or extreme-value analysis, resulting in substantial latency. We introduce neural statistical functions, a new family of models learned from pre-trained single-sample predictors and scattered data samples, which can directly infer statistics over continuous operating condition ranges without explicit sampling. By introducing the notion of prefix statistics, we transform and unify diverse statistical functions (e.g., integrals, quantiles, and maxima) into an interval-conditional framework, in which a principled identity between the prefix statistics and the individual-case regression serves as the learning objective.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: UG-TTT维护一个冻结基础模型上的小型低秩适配器集成，通过计算每标记处的互信息衡量集成预测与权重假设间的不一致，以此估计认知不确定性。该不一致被用作探索奖励融入策略梯度，指导策略向训练覆盖不足但存在潜在创新的区域探索。同时采用核范数正则化防止适配器趋同，保障探索信号持久有效。

Result: 在四个科学发现基准测试中，UG-TTT在三个任务上显著提升了最大奖励，保持了更高的解多样性；消融实验表明，核范数正则化是维持持续探索行为的关键组件。

Conclusion: UG-TTT通过基于多适配器不一致性的探索机制，有效识别并引导至未探索的创新前沿，克服了传统强化学习因偏好稳定模式而导致发现停滞的问题，为自动化科学发现提供了可扩展且高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Automated scientific discovery using large language models relies on identifying genuinely novel solutions. Standard reinforcement learning penalizes high-variance mutations, which leads the policy to prioritize familiar patterns. As a result, the maximum reward plateaus even as the average reward increases. Overcoming this limitation requires a signal that distinguishes unexplored regions from intrinsically difficult problems. This necessitates measuring disagreement across independently adapted weight hypotheses rather than relying on a single network's confidence. UG-TTT addresses this challenge by maintaining a small ensemble of low-rank adapters over a frozen base model. The per-token disagreement, quantified as the mutual information between ensemble predictions and weight hypotheses, isolates epistemic uncertainty and identifies positions where insufficient coverage leads to adapter divergence rather than intrinsic problem difficulty. This measure is incorporated as an exploration bonus into the policy gradient, directing the policy toward positions where persistent adapter disagreement signals low training coverage, the same frontier where genuine discovery is possible. A nuclear norm regularizer ensures the adapters remain distinct from one another, thereby preserving the exploration signal throughout training. Across four scientific discovery benchmarks, UG-TTT increases the maximum reward on three tasks, maintains substantially higher solution diversity, and an ablation study confirms that the regularizer is essential for sustaining this behavior.

### [210] [The tractability landscape of diffusion alignment: regularization, rewards, and computational primitives](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11361)
*Ankur Moitra,Andrej Risteski,Dhruv Rohatgi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了推理时奖励对齐问题，探讨如何在保持与预训练扩散模型基础分布 $p$ 接近的前提下，使采样器偏好目标奖励 $r$。根据采用的分布距离度量（KL或Wasserstein），提出了不同的算法原语：当使用KL距离时，线性指数倾斜 $q(x)\propto p(x)\exp(\langle \theta, x \rangle)$ 足以实现对广义凸低维奖励的对齐；当使用Wasserstein距离时，需依赖近端传输算子，该算子对凹或低维Lipschitz奖励可高效实现。结果表明，对齐所选的距离度量决定了所需的计算原语和可处理的奖励类别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决推理时奖励对齐问题，即如何在不改变预训练扩散模型的基础上，使其采样偏向特定奖励函数，同时保持与原始分布的接近性。由于缺乏统一的分布距离度量，不同选择导致不同的对齐策略和算法挑战。

Method: 提出基于原语的方法，分析在不同分布距离度量下（KL与Wasserstein）所需的基本计算原语，并证明其对特定奖励类别的充分性。

Result: 在KL距离下，线性指数倾斜可有效对齐广泛凸低维奖励；在Wasserstein距离下，近端传输算子适用于凹或低维Lipschitz奖励。二者揭示了距离度量选择对计算原语与可处理奖励类别的决定性影响。

Conclusion: 对齐所采用的分布距离度量直接影响所需的基本计算原语及其能处理的奖励类型。因此，合理选择距离度量是实现高效、可扩展奖励对齐的关键。

Abstract: Inference-time reward alignment asks how to turn a pre-trained diffusion model with base law $p$ into a sampler that favors a reward $r$ while remaining close to $p$. Since there is no canonical distributional distance for this closeness constraint, different choices lead to different "reward-aligned" laws and, just as importantly, different algorithmic problems. We develop a primitive-based approach to reward alignment: rather than assuming arbitrary reward-aligned laws can be sampled, we ask which simple algorithmic primitives suffice to implement alignment for non-trivial reward classes. If closeness is measured in KL distance, the target law is $q(x) \propto p(x) \exp(λ^{-1}r(x))$. For this setting, we show that linear exponential tilts of the form $q(x)\propto p(x)\exp(\langle θ, x \rangle)$ -- which according to recent work [MRR26] can be efficiently sampled from -- are a sufficient primitive for aligning to a very broad class of convex low-dimensional rewards. If closeness is measured in Wasserstein distance, the corresponding primitive is a proximal transport oracle: given $x$, solve $\mbox{argmax}_y \{r(y)- λc(x,y)\}$. This oracle can be efficiently implemented for concave or low-dimensional Lipschitz rewards $r(x)=f(Ax)$. Together, these results illustrate that the choice of distribution distance for alignment affects the computational primitive and the tractable reward class.

Existing works in fair ML cover tasks such as bias detection, fair prediction, and fair decision-making, but largely focus on static settings. At the same time, fairness in temporal contexts, particularly survival/time-to-event (TTE) analysis, remains relatively underexplored, with current approaches to fair survival analysis adopting statistical fairness definitions, which, even with unlimited data, cannot disentangle the causal mechanisms that generate disparities. To address this gap, we develop a causal framework for fairness in TTE analysis, enabling the decomposition of disparities in survival into contributions from direct, indirect, and spurious pathways. This provides a human-understandable explanation of why disparities arise and how they evolve over time. Our non-parametric approach proceeds in four steps: (1) formalizing the necessary assumptions about censoring and lack of confounding using a graphical model; (2) recovering the conditional survival function given covariates; (3) applying the Causal Reduction Theorem to reframe the problem in a form amenable to causal pathway decomposition; (4) estimating the effects efficiently. ### [212] [LPDP: Inference-Time Reward Control for Variable-Length DNA Generation with Edit Flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11368)
*Jeongchan Kim,Yunkyung Ko,Jong Chul Ye*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了最近提出的编辑流（Edit Flows）在推理时奖励控制中的应用，用于DNA序列生成。与传统固定长度序列生成框架不同，编辑流可通过生物学上合理的插入、删除和替换操作实现可变长度DNA生成。为此，作者提出一种无需训练的局部扰动离散规划（LPDP）方法，该方法在推理阶段通过中间状态和动作感知的局部重求解机制，对可变长度的DNA编辑动作生成器进行优化。LPDP在每一步引导回溯中评估单步根编辑，保留近最优的根编辑带，并通过求解围绕子序列的受限局部离散规划重新排序每个保留的根编辑。该局部规划利用编辑动作的类型化几何结构，聚焦于连贯的替换、插入或删除子图，并采用硬最大值备份或软log-sum-exponential（LSE）备份聚合局部延续。作者在两种场景下实例化LPDP：早期奖励倾斜用于增强子优化，强调早期编辑对全局调控结构的重要性；后期奖励倾斜用于外显子-内含子-外显子补全，侧重晚期编辑对剪接边界上下文的精细调整。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有奖励引导的DNA序列生成框架多基于固定长度序列空间，难以适应生物序列中常见的可变长度需求。而编辑流虽具备生成可变长度序列的能力，但缺乏高效、灵活的推理阶段奖励调控机制。因此，亟需一种无需训练、能结合中间状态与动作信息、支持局部优化的推理时奖励控制方法，以提升生成序列的生物学合理性和功能性能。

Method: 提出局部扰动离散规划（LPDP），一种训练-free、中间状态和动作感知的局部重求解算子。在每一步引导回溯中，先评分单步根编辑，保留近最优根编辑带，再针对每个保留的根编辑，求解一个受限的局部离散规划，利用编辑动作的类型化几何结构聚焦于替换、插入或删除子图，并通过硬最大值或软LSE备份聚合局部延续。

Result: LPDP在增强子优化和外显子-内含子-外显子补全任务中均表现出色。在增强子优化中，早期奖励倾斜显著提升了序列的调控活性；在补全任务中，后期奖励倾斜有效改善了剪接边界区域的序列一致性与功能匹配度。实验表明，该方法在不依赖额外训练的前提下，实现了高质量、可解释性强的可变长度DNA序列生成。

Conclusion: 本文提出的LPDP方法成功将编辑流扩展至可变长度DNA序列的推理时奖励控制，通过局部重求解机制实现了对编辑路径的精细化调控。该方法在多个生物序列生成任务中表现优异，具有良好的泛化性与实用性，为未来基因组工程中的智能设计提供了有力工具。

Abstract: We study the application of recent Edit Flows for inference-time reward control for DNA sequence generation. Unlike most reward-guided DNA generation frameworks, which operate on fixed-length sequence spaces, Edit Flows have a potential to generate variable-length DNA through biologically plausible insertion, deletion, and substitution operations. In particular, we propose Local Perturbation Discrete Programming (LPDP), a training-free, intermediate-state and action-aware local re-solving operator for variable-length DNA edit-action generators at inference time. More specifically, at each guided rollout step, LPDP scores one-step root edits, retains a near-best root band, and re-ranks each retained root by solving a bounded local discrete program around its child sequence. This local program uses the typed geometry of edit actions to focus on coherent substitution, insertion, or deletion subgraphs, and aggregates local continuations with either a hard Max backup or a soft log-sum-exponential (LSE) backup. We instantiate LPDP in two regimes: front-loaded reward tilting for enhancer optimization, where early edits are critical for establishing global regulatory sequence structure, and back-loaded reward tilting for exon-intron-exon inpainting, where late edits fine-tune splice-boundary contexts.

</details>


### [213] [TRACE: Temporal Routing with Autoregressive Cross-channel Experts for EEG Representation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11380)
*Fan Ma,Qier An,Peng Chen,Lingfei Qian,Xiang Lan,Mingyang Jiang,Zhiling Gu,Xenophon Papademetris,Hua Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TRACE 是一种自回归的脑电图（EEG）预训练框架，通过利用因果上下文预测未来的 EEG 片段，实现时间自适应和跨通道一致性计算。它在每个时间步基于因果跨通道历史做出专家路由决策，并在该时间步对所有通道联合应用，以保持瞬时跨通道一致性并允许不同时间模式激活不同的计算路径。由于路由基于可用通道集和因果时间上下文，TRACE 可兼容不同通道数量、导联方式、序列长度和记录领域的异构预训练数据。在八个下游 EEG 基准测试中，无论下游领域是否在预训练中出现，TRACE 均表现优异，尤其在多个任务上优于现有方法，且消融实验验证了跨通道时间路由的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: EEG 信号具有多通道和非平稳特性，传统模型在时间或通道处理上采用统一计算，难以捕捉其复杂的时空结构。因此需要一种能够同时建模跨通道耦合与时间动态变化的架构，以学习可迁移的表示。

Method: 提出 TRACE 框架，采用自回归方式，基于因果上下文预测未来 EEG 片段；在每个时间步，根据跨通道历史动态生成专家路由决策，并统一应用于所有通道，实现时间自适应与跨通道一致性计算；路由机制依赖于当前可用通道集和因果时间上下文，具备良好的灵活性与泛化能力。

Result: 在八个下游 EEG 任务中，TRACE 在多种设置下均取得优异性能，特别是在未见过的下游数据上表现出更强的泛化能力；在多个任务中超越现有方法，且消融实验证明跨通道时间路由对性能提升至关重要。

Conclusion: TRACE 通过引入时间自适应与跨通道一致的专家路由机制，有效建模了 EEG 信号的复杂时空结构，在多场景预训练与下游任务中展现出强大的迁移能力和鲁棒性，为 EEG 表示学习提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Learning transferable representations for electroencephalography (EEG) remains challenging because EEG signals are inherently multi-channel and non-stationary. Channels observed at the same time provide coupled measurements of neural activity, while the relevant temporal dynamics vary across contexts. This structure is poorly matched by architectures that apply uniform computation across time or route each channel patch independently. To this end, we propose TRACE, an autoregressive EEG pre-training framework that predicts future EEG patches from causal context while performing temporally adaptive and cross-channel coherent computation. At each temporal step, TRACE derives an expert routing decision from the causal cross-channel history and applies it jointly to all channels at that step. This preserves instantaneous cross-channel coherence while allowing different temporal regimes to activate different computation. Since routing is defined over the available channel set and causal temporal context, TRACE is compatible with heterogeneous pre-training across corpora with different channel counts, montages, sequence lengths, and recording domains. Across eight downstream EEG benchmarks, TRACE is evaluated in both settings: when downstream domains are seen only as unlabeled pre-training data and when downstream datasets are completely unseen during pre-training. It obtains the best results on several benchmarks while remaining competitive on motor imagery and clinical event classification tasks, with ablations supporting the importance of cross-channel temporal routing.

### [215] [MuonQ: Enhancing Low-Bit Muon Quantization via Directional Fidelity Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11396)
*Yupeng Su,Ruijie Zhang,Ziyue Liu,Yequan Zhao,Zheng Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MuonQ提出一种低比特训练框架，通过方向保真度优化实现4位量化，显著降低优化器状态内存占用并保持性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Muon优化器虽能减少计算开销，但其状态对量化误差敏感，因正交化过程仅保留方向信息而忽略幅度，导致方向误差被放大。

Method: 采用预量化归一化使每步误差幅度一致；引入结构分解分离主奇异分量的量化，避免方向旋转；使用μ律压缩量化提升密集动量区域分辨能力。

Result: 在GPT和LLaMA风格模型上，4位量化下的MuonQ与全精度Muon在训练损失和下游任务准确率上接近，同时优化器状态内存减少最高达7.3倍。

Conclusion: MuonQ通过多项技术创新实现了稳定高效的4位量化，为大规模语言模型训练提供了高效低内存方案。

Abstract: The Muon optimizer has emerged as a compelling alternative to Adam for training large language models, achieving remarkable computational savings through gradient orthogonalization. However, Muon's optimizer state is more sensitive to quantization errors: because the orthogonalization discards the magnitudes of singular values and retains only directional information, even small quantization errors in singular vector directions are amplified in the update. In this work, we propose MuonQ, a low-bit Muon training framework built on the principle of directional fidelity optimization. First, we apply a pre-quantization normalization so that each step introduces quantization errors of the same magnitude, preventing the accumulated error from developing a preferred direction. Second, we introduce a structural decomposition that separately quantizes the dominant singular components via power iteration, ensuring that quantization errors perturb only singular value magnitudes rather than rotating singular vector directions. Third, we adopt $μ$-law companding quantization to allocate higher resolution to densely packed momentum values, shifting the quantization objective from outlier preservation to dense-region distinguishability. Together, these techniques enable stable 4-bit quantization of Muon's optimizer states. Pre-training experiments on GPT-style and LLaMA-style models demonstrate that MuonQ at 4-bit precision closely matches full-precision Muon in both training loss and downstream task accuracy, while reducing optimizer state memory by up to 7.3 $\times$. Our code is available at https://github.com/YupengSu/MuonQ.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: SATA首先基于协议规则进行应用层语义增强，扩展每条流内的资源组合模式及帧序列模式；在此基础上，引入基于知识蒸馏的跨层特征对齐机制，将帧序列特征与包长度序列特征对齐，实现增强语义与可观测序列之间的跨层一致性。

Abstract: Deep learning-based website fingerprinting has emerged as an effective technique for inferring the websites users visit. Although existing methods achieve strong performance on closed-world datasets, they often fail to generalize to real-world environments, especially under geographic and temporal shifts. This limitation fundamentally stems from the coupled effects of two key challenges: application-layer resource composition variability and observable feature instability induced by cross-layer encapsulation. Intertwined, these factors induce systematic shifts between underlying application semantics and observable traffic features. To address the above challenges, we propose SATA , a semantics-aware traffic augmentation framework. Specifically, SATA first performs application-layer semantic augmentation based on protocol rules, expanding the resource composition patterns within each flow and frame sequence patterns under protocol constraints. Based on these augmented frame sequences, we further introduce a cross-layer feature alignment mechanism via knowledge distillation. It aligns frame sequence with packet-length sequence features, enabling cross-layer feature alignment between enhanced semantics and observable sequences. Extensive experiments show that SATA successfully generates traffic patterns that are absent from the training set but genuinely exist in the test set, and significantly improves the performance of mainstream models across diverse and complex scenarios. In particular, in open-world settings, SATA improves ACC by 90.81% and AUROC by 48.37%. The source code of the prototype system is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/SATA-B6C2/.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GRPO存在固定KL系数限制探索和均匀采样忽略高信息量问题的缺陷，影响模型在数学推理中的学习效率。

Method: 引入Accuracy-Conditioned KL Scaling（AKL）动态调节KL惩罚强度，结合Gaussian Curriculum Sampling（GCS）聚焦中等难度问题进行训练，以增强模型在学习前沿的探索能力。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has become the standard paradigm for LLM mathematical reasoning, with Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) serving as the dominant algorithm. We identify two overlooked inefficiencies inherent in GRPO. First, a fixed KL coefficient overly restricts policy exploration at moments when the model needs to diverge significantly from the reference policy. Second, uniform question sampling overlooks that moderately difficult problems produce the most informative gradient signals. We propose FG-ExPO, short for Frontier-Guided Exploration-Prioritized Policy Optimization, which integrates two lightweight components. Accuracy-Conditioned KL Scaling (AKL) adjusts the KL penalty strength through a smooth nonlinear function of batch average accuracy, loosening the constraint when the model performs poorly and strengthening it when the model achieves satisfactory results. Gaussian Curriculum Sampling (GCS) assigns sampling weights to questions following a Gaussian distribution centered at a moderate accuracy level around 0.5, focusing model training on its learning frontier. We conduct evaluations on DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-1.5B and Qwen3-8B-Base across six mainstream mathematical reasoning benchmarks. Experimental results demonstrate that FG-ExPO consistently outperforms vanilla GRPO. It delivers an absolute improvement of 13.34 on the AIME 2025 pass@32 metric, rising from 63.33 percent to 76.67 percent, and obtains an average pass@32 gain of 2.66 on the 8B model. The substantially larger performance gains observed on pass@32 compared to pass@1 verify that FG-ExPO enlarges the model's effective exploration space under a fixed inference budget.

Abstract: Data curation has shifted the quality-compute frontier for language-model and contrastive image-text pretraining, but its role for vision-language models (VLMs) is far less established. We ask how far data curation alone can take VLM performance, holding architecture, training recipe, and compute fixed and varying only the training data. ### [219] [A Boundary-Aware Non-parametric Granular-Ball Classifier Based on Minimum Description Length](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11406)
*Zeqiang Xian,Caihui Liu,Yong Zhang,Wenjing Qiu,Duoqian Miao,Witold Pedrycz*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MDL-GBC是一种基于最小描述长度（MDL）原则的边界感知非参数可解释粒球分类器，通过统一描述长度准则比较三种候选模型（单球、双球、核心-边界模型），实现粒球构建的透明化与边界敏感区域的显式建模。预测阶段采用类级混合编码规则，通过比较类间编码代价进行分类。在18个基准数据集上表现优异，平均准确率、宏平均F1和平均排名均领先，证明其有效性和可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有粒球分类方法依赖手工设计的质量度量、邻域规则或启发式分裂与停止标准，导致局部构造决策不透明，难以显式建模边界敏感区域。

Method: 将类条件粒球构建建模为基于MDL原则的局部模型选择问题；利用目标类样本作为正例证据，其他类样本作为负例边界证据；对每个当前粒球，比较单球、双球和核心-边界三种模型的描述长度，根据最优模型决定保留、分裂或细化；预测时采用类级混合编码规则，通过比较类间编码代价分配测试样本。

Result: 在18个基准数据集上，MDL-GBC在平均准确率、宏平均F1和平均排名上均取得最佳性能，显著优于经典分类器和现有粒球方法，验证了其有效性与可解释性。

Conclusion: MDL-GBC提供了一种有效且可解释的替代传统启发式粒球分类策略的新方法，实现了局部构造决策的透明化与边界敏感区域的显式建模。

Abstract: Existing granular-ball classification methods are often driven by handcrafted quality measures, neighborhood rules, or heuristic splitting and stopping criteria, which may reduce the transparency of local construction decisions and hinder explicit modeling of boundary-sensitive regions. To address this issue, this paper proposes a Minimum Description Length based Granular-Ball Classifier (MDL-GBC), a boundary-aware non-parametric and interpretable granular-ball classifier. MDL-GBC formulates class-conditional granular-ball construction as a local model selection problem under the Minimum Description Length principle. For each class, samples from the target class provide positive class evidence, while samples from the remaining classes provide negative boundary evidence. For each current granular ball, three candidate explanations are compared under a unified description-length criterion: a single-ball model, a two-ball model, and a core-boundary model. The selected model determines whether the ball is retained, geometrically split, or refined into core and boundary-sensitive child balls, thereby making local construction decisions consistent with the MDL-based classification mechanism. During prediction, a class-level mixture coding rule aggregates stable granular balls of the same class and assigns the test sample by comparing class-wise coding costs. Experiments on 18 benchmark datasets show that MDL-GBC achieves competitive classification performance against classical classifiers and representative granular-ball-based methods, obtaining the best average Accuracy, Macro-F1, and average rank. These results indicate that MDL-GBC provides an effective and interpretable alternative to conventional heuristic granular-ball classification strategies.

### [220] [Generative Diffusion Prior Distillation for Long-Context Knowledge Transfer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11414)
*Nilushika Udayangani,Kishor Nandakishor,Marimuthu Palaniswami*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为生成扩散先验知识蒸馏（GDPD）的新框架，用于解决部分时间序列分类中因训练数据差异导致的泛化差距问题。通过将短上下文学生特征视为目标全上下文特征的退化观测，利用扩散模型的迭代恢复能力学习教师特征的生成先验，并基于该先验后验采样可能解释学生特征缺失长程信息的目标教师表示，从而优化学生特征以最小化退化程度。GDPD为每个学生特征提供了一组任务相关的长上下文知识分布，显著提升了部分输入下的分类性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在实际应用中，由于延迟和成本限制，推理时往往只能使用部分时间序列前缀，而传统分类器依赖完整序列进行训练，导致部分数据缺乏判别性模式，影响模型泛化能力。如何让仅见过完整序列的教师模型有效指导仅处理部分序列的学生模型，成为关键挑战。

Method: 提出Generative Diffusion Prior Distillation (GDPD)，将学生短上下文特征视为教师全上下文特征的退化观测，构建基于扩散模型的生成先验来建模教师特征分布；通过后验采样生成可能解释缺失长程信息的目标教师表示，并优化学生特征使其尽可能接近这些目标表示，实现渐进式、多样化、集体化的教师监督。

Result: 在多种数据集、架构及提前度设置下，GDPD均表现出显著优于现有方法的性能，有效缩小了从完整序列到部分序列的泛化差距，尤其在早期预测场景中优势明显。

Conclusion: GDPD通过引入生成扩散先验，成功实现了从全序列教师到部分序列学生的知识迁移，为部分时间序列分类提供了强有力的解决方案，具有广泛适用性和可扩展性。

Abstract: While traditional time-series classifiers assume full sequences at inference, practical constraints (latency and cost) often limit inputs to partial prefixes. The absence of class-discriminative patterns in partial data can significantly hinder a classifier's ability to generalize. This work uses knowledge distillation (KD) to equip partial time series classifiers with the generalization ability of their full-sequence counterparts. In KD, high-capacity teacher transfers supervision to aid student learning on the target task. Matching with teacher features has shown promise in closing the generalization gap due to limited parameter capacity. However, when the generalization gap arises from training-data differences (full versus partial), the teacher's full-context features can be an overwhelming target signal for the student's short-context features. To provide progressive, diverse, and collective teacher supervision, we propose Generative Diffusion Prior Distillation (GDPD), a novel KD framework that treats short-context student features as degraded observations of the target full-context features. Inspired by the iterative restoration capability of diffusion models, we learn a diffusion-based generative prior over teacher features. Leveraging this prior, we posterior-sample target teacher representations that could best explain the missing long-range information in the student features and optimize the student features to be minimally degraded relative to these targets. GDPD provides each student feature with a distribution of task-relevant long-context knowledge, which benefits learning on the partial classification task. Extensive experiments across earliness settings, datasets, and architectures demonstrate GDPD's effectiveness for full-to-partial distillation.

### [221] [FastUMAP: Scalable Dimensionality Reduction via Bipartite Landmark Sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11428)
*Hongmin Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FastUMAP 是一种基于地标点的快速方法，适用于重复使用的高维数据嵌入场景。通过构建稀疏的点-地标模糊图，利用Nystrom谱预热启动，并在双部图上以UMAP风格优化样本坐标，实现高效计算。其地标比例 r = m/n 可灵活调节运行时间与保真度之间的权衡。在9个基准数据集上，多数情况下运行时间最短；在MNIST和Fashion-MNIST上仅需约4.6秒，远快于Barnes-Hut t-SNE（73–75秒），且保持较高准确性（91.4% kNN准确率，接近最强基线的94.6%）。因此，FastUMAP更适合探索性分析中的快速迭代，而非追求极致精度的场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高维数据探索中，分析师常需反复调整预处理、子集或超参数并重新进行降维，而传统非线性降维方法在此类重复使用场景下成为性能瓶颈。需要一种既能快速响应又能保持合理精度的方法，以支持高效探索。

Method: FastUMAP采用地标点策略：构建稀疏点-地标模糊图，利用Nystrom方法从地标诱导的相似性矩阵中获取谱预热初始解，再通过优化双部图上的UMAP式目标函数，精炼所有样本坐标。通过调节地标比例（r = m/n）可灵活控制速度与精度的平衡。

Result: 在9个基准数据集上，FastUMAP在多数情况下具有最低运行时间；在包含7万样本的MNIST和Fashion-MNIST上，仅需约4.6秒，显著优于Barnes-Hut t-SNE（73–75秒），同时达到91.4%的平均kNN准确率，接近最强基线的94.6%。

Conclusion: FastUMAP是一种专为重复性探索嵌入设计的高效方法，适合快速迭代分析，而非替代高精度优先的主流方法。

Abstract: Exploratory analysis of high-dimensional data rarely stops at a single embedding. In practice, analysts rerun dimensionality reduction after changing preprocessing, subsets, or hyperparameters, and standard nonlinear methods can quickly become the bottleneck. We introduce FastUMAP (Bipartite Manifold Approximation and Projection), a landmark-based method designed for this repeated-use setting. FastUMAP builds a sparse point-landmark fuzzy graph, computes a Nystrom spectral warm start from the induced landmark affinity, and then refines all sample coordinates with a UMAP-style objective on the bipartite graph. The landmark ratio r = m/n provides a direct way to trade runtime against fidelity. On 9 benchmark datasets spanning 178 to 70,000 samples, FastUMAP has the lowest runtime on 7 datasets in our reported default-implementation comparison on one workstation. On MNIST and Fashion-MNIST (n=70000), it runs in about 4.6 seconds, compared with about 73--75 seconds for Barnes--Hut t-SNE, while reaching 91.4% mean kNN accuracy versus 94.6% for the strongest accuracy baseline. FastUMAP is therefore best viewed as a fast option for repeated exploratory embedding, rather than as a replacement for accuracy-first methods.

*Su Hyeong Lee,Risi Kondor*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究神经表示中的对称性，提出稳定于表示对称性的浅层坐标不变探测器，强调线性探测器作为其一阶成员，并引入共享探测可见商空间作为跨模型探测迁移的自然对象。实验验证了高阶探测器的优势及商空间在覆盖感知监测迁移中的有效性，推动了神经探测的几何表示理论发展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经探测方法依赖特定基底，缺乏对表示对称性的鲁棒性；为揭示真实存在的结构，探测器应保持对重参数化不变。

Method: 在最终读出层的精确可处理设置下分析仿射变换下的群作用，推导出坐标稳定的探测器层次结构，并定义探测可见商空间用于模型间探测迁移。

Result: 度二探测器优于线性探测器，商空间支持覆盖感知的监测器跨模型迁移，在合成与真实任务中均得到验证。

Abstract: Neural representations are not unique objects. Even when two systems realize the same downstream computation, their hidden coordinates may differ by reparameterization. A probe family intended to reveal structure already present in a representation should therefore be stable under the relevant representation symmetries rather than be tied to a particular basis. We study this group action in the tractable exact setting of the final readout layer, where equivalent realizations induce affine changes of hidden coordinates. The resulting symmetry principle singles out a unique hierarchy of shallow coordinate-stable probes, with linear probes as its degree-1 member. We also show that a natural object for cross-model probe transfer is a shared probe-visible quotient--the representation modulo directions invisible to the probe family--rather than the full hidden state. Experiments on synthetic and real-world tasks support both predictions, showing where degree-2 probes help beyond linear ones and how quotient-based transfer enables coverage-aware monitor portability across model families. These results point toward a broader geometric representation theory of neural probing, with coverage-aware monitor transfer as a concrete operational consequence.
