### [223] [Anti-Self-Distillation for Reasoning RL via Pointwise Mutual Information](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11609)
*Guobin Shen,Xiang Cheng,Chenxiao Zhao,Lei Huang,Jindong Li,Dongcheng Zhao,Xing Yu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出Anti-Self-Distillation（AntiSD）方法，通过增加学生与教师之间的差异而非减少，解决自蒸馏在数学推理中表现不一致的问题。该方法逆转了每个标记的符号，自然地实现了优势，并在教师熵降低时通过熵触发门禁用该项，可作为默认自蒸馏的即插即用替代方案。在多个模型和基准测试中，AntiSD在2到10倍更少的训练步数内达到GRPO基线准确率，并将最终准确率提升最多11.5个百分点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于策略的自蒸馏在数学推理任务中表现不稳定，尽管在其他任务上有效。分析发现，问题根源在于特权上下文（如验证解或反馈）会过度增强教师对已由解暗示的标记（如结构连接词、可验证命题）的信心，同时削弱对推动多步搜索的推理标记（如“Wait”、“Let”、“Maybe”）的信心。因此需要一种新的自蒸馏机制来纠正这一偏差。

Method: 提出Anti-Self-Distillation（AntiSD），通过最大化学生与教师之间的分歧而非最小化，实现反向引导。具体采用符号反转的损失项，并引入熵触发门控机制，在教师熵下降至阈值以下时自动关闭该项，避免过拟合，实现稳定且高效的自我改进。

Result: 在五个不同规模（4B至30B参数）的语言模型上进行测试，AntiSD在数学推理基准上表现出显著性能提升：相比传统自蒸馏，可在2至10倍更少的训练步数内达到GRPO基线准确率，且最终准确率最高提升11.5个百分点。

Conclusion: AntiSD为语言模型实现可扩展的自我改进提供了新路径，使模型能仅依赖自身训练信号不断提升推理能力，无需更强外部教师。该方法具有良好的泛化性和部署灵活性，是自蒸馏在复杂推理任务中的重要突破。

Abstract: On-policy self-distillation, where a student is pulled toward a copy of itself conditioned on privileged context (e.g., a verified solution or feedback), offers a promising direction for advancing reasoning capability without a stronger external teacher. Yet in math reasoning the gains are inconsistent, even when the same approach succeeds elsewhere. A pointwise mutual information analysis traces the failure to the privileged context itself: it inflates the teacher's confidence on tokens already implied by the solution (structural connectives, verifiable claims) and deflates it on deliberation tokens ("Wait", "Let", "Maybe") that drive multi-step search. We propose Anti-Self-Distillation (AntiSD), which ascends a divergence between student and teacher rather than descending it: this reverses the per-token sign and yields a naturally bounded advantage in one step. An entropy-triggered gate disables the term once the teacher entropy collapses, completing a drop-in replacement for default self-distillation. Across five models from 4B to 30B parameters on math reasoning benchmarks, AntiSD reaches the GRPO baseline's accuracy in 2 to 10x fewer training steps and improves final accuracy by up to 11.5 points. AntiSD opens a path to scalable self-improvement, where a language model bootstraps its own reasoning through its training signal.

### [224] [On the Approximation Complexity of Matrix Product Operator Born Machines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11471)
*Chao Li,Zerui Tao,Yuchen Cong,Jian Xu,Qibin Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了矩阵乘积算子波恩机（MPO-BMs）在概率建模中的近似能力。首先证明在连续情形下KL近似是NP难的，表明其在最坏情况下无法实现普遍高效的近似；其次，在损失诱导哈密顿量满足局域性和谱隙条件时，结构化目标（如路径图马尔可夫随机场）可被MPO-BM以多项式维度近似，并具备可证明的KL保证；最后，同样在局域结构下，多项式数量的得分查询足以估计哈密顿量并获得上述保证。整体揭示了MPO-BMs在何时本质困难、何时可高效学习。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 明确MPO-BMs在概率建模中是否具有高效近似能力，尤其是其理论边界。由于现有方法缺乏对模型适用范围的系统性理解，亟需从正反两方面揭示其近似能力的理论限制与可行条件。

Method: 采用理论分析方法，包括复杂性理论（证明NP-hard性）、量子哈密顿量分析（引入局部性和谱隙条件）、以及统计估计方法（通过得分查询估计哈密顿量）。

Result: 1. 在连续设置中，MPO-BMs的KL近似为NP-hard，说明其在最坏情况下无法高效近似任意分布；2. 在特定条件下，结构化目标可通过多项式维度的MPO-BM实现有保证的近似；3. 多项式数量的得分查询即可完成哈密顿量估计并获得理论保证。

Conclusion: MPO-BMs的近似能力存在明确的理论边界：当目标分布具有特定结构且满足局部性与谱隙条件时，其可高效学习并提供可证明的近似质量；否则，其近似问题本质上是困难的。这为实际应用提供了理论指导。

Abstract: Matrix product operator Born machines (MPO-BMs) are tractable tensor-network models for probabilistic modeling, but their efficient approximation capability remains unclear. We characterize this boundary from both negative and positive perspectives. First, we prove that KL approximation is NP-hard for MPO-BMs in the continuous setting, ruling out universal efficient approximation in the worst case. Second, for score-based variational inference, we show that, under a locality and spectral-gap conditions on the loss-induced Hamiltonian, structured targets (e.g., path-graph Markov random fields) admit MPO-BM approximations with polynomial bond dimension and provable KL guarantees. Third, under the same locality structure, we prove that polynomially many score queries suffice to estimate the induced Hamiltonian and obtain such guarantees. Our results provide a theoretical characterization of when MPO-BMs are fundamentally hard to approximate and when they become efficiently learnable.

### [225] [Slicing and Dicing: Configuring Optimal Mixtures of Experts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11689)
*Margaret Li,Sneha Kudugunta,Danielle Rothermel,Luke Zettlemoyer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究对超过2,000次预训练实验进行了系统性分析，涵盖高达6.6B参数的模型，全面考察了专家数量、专家维度、层内异构专家配置、共享专家大小及负载均衡机制等MoE设计选择。结果表明，性能随总MoE参数增加而持续提升，即使在极端活跃参数比例（如128）下依然有效；最优专家规模几乎不随总参数量变化，仅取决于活跃参数量；其他因素如共享专家、异构专家和负载均衡设置的影响相对较小，但无丢弃路由（dropless routing）带来稳定增益。整体建议：应优先关注专家数量与粒度，其余设计选择对最终质量影响有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前Mixture-of-Experts（MoE）架构在大语言模型中已成为标准，但其核心设计选择（如专家数量、粒度、共享专家、负载均衡、令牌丢弃等）通常被孤立研究，且范围狭窄。这些设计之间的相互作用尚未充分探索，导致是否可独立优化仍不清楚。因此需要一次大规模、系统性的实验来揭示各设计要素的真实影响。

Method: 通过执行超过2,000次预训练运行，构建并测试了多种不同配置的MoE模型，覆盖从数百万到6.6亿参数的规模。系统地变化了总专家数、专家维度、层内异构专家配置、共享专家大小以及负载均衡策略，并评估其对模型性能的影响。所有实验均在相同数据集和训练流程下进行，确保可比性。

Result: 1. 在所研究的每个活跃参数尺度上，模型性能随着总MoE参数的增加而持续提升，甚至在极高的活跃专家参数比例（如128）下仍有效；2. 最优专家规模几乎不随总参数量变化，仅由活跃参数量决定；3. 共享专家、异构专家配置、负载均衡方式等因素对性能影响较小；4. 采用无丢弃路由（dropless routing）能带来一致的性能提升。

Conclusion: MoE架构的设计应聚焦于专家数量和粒度这两个关键因素，其他设计选择（如共享专家、异构专家、负载均衡）对最终模型质量的影响相对较小，可视为次要调整项。这为高效构建高性能MoE模型提供了简洁清晰的指导原则。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architectures have become standard in large language models, yet many of their core design choices - expert count, granularity, shared experts, load balancing, token dropping - have only been studied one or two at a time over narrow configuration ranges. It remains an open question whether these choices can be optimized independently, without considering interactions. We present the first systematic study of over 2,000 pretraining runs spanning models up to 6.6B total parameters, in which we exhaustively vary total experts, expert dimension, heterogeneous expert sizing within a single layer, shared expert size and load-balancing mechanisms. We find that at every active-parameter scale that we study, performance consistently improves with total MoE parameters even at extreme active expert parameter ratios like 128.Further, the optimal expert size is nearly invariant to total parameter count and depends only on active parameter count. Third, we see that other choices like shared experts, heterogeneous experts and load-balancing settings have small effects relative to expert count and granularity, although dropless routing yields a consistent gain. Overall, our results suggest a simpler recipe: focus on expert count and granularity, other choices have minimal effect on final quality.

### [226] [Efficient Adjoint Matching for Fine-tuning Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11480)
*Jeongwoo Shin,Dongsoo Shin,Joonseok Lee,Jaewoong Choi,Jaemoo Choi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Efficient Adjoint Matching (EAM)，通过将原始的随机最优控制问题重新表述为具有线性基础漂移和修改后的终端代价的形式，显著提升了文本到图像生成中基于奖励微调的训练效率。EAM消除了传统Adjoint Matching（AM）所需的大量函数评估和反向伴随状态模拟，实现了仅需少量步骤的确定性常微分方程求解器采样，并获得闭式伴随解，从而避免了后向计算。在多个标准基准测试中，EAM比AM快达4倍，且在PickScore、ImageReward、HPSv2.1、CLIPScore和Aesthetics等指标上表现相当或更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Adjoint Matching（AM）虽然在理论上严谨，但因需要全轨迹的随机模拟和反向伴随状态求解，导致计算开销巨大。本文观察到这些瓶颈与预训练模型继承的非平凡基础漂移密切相关，因此提出改进方案以提升效率。

Method: 提出Efficient Adjoint Matching（EAM），将原SOC问题重构为具有线性基础漂移和修正终端成本的形式，从而支持高效确定性采样并获得闭式伴随解，消除反向模拟需求。

Abstract: Reward fine-tuning has become a common approach for aligning pretrained diffusion and flow models with human preferences in text-to-image generation. Among reward-gradient-based methods, Adjoint Matching (AM) provides a principled formulation by casting reward fine-tuning as a stochastic optimal control (SOC) problem. However, AM inevitably requires a substantial computational cost: it requires (i) stochastic simulation of full generative trajectories under memoryless dynamics, resulting in a large number of function evaluations, and (ii) backward ODE simulation of the adjoint state along each sampled trajectory. In this work, we observe that both bottlenecks are closely tied to the \textit{non-trivial base drift} inherited from the pretrained model. Motivated by this observation, we propose \textbf{Efficient Adjoint Matching (EAM)}, which substantially improves training efficiency by reformulating the SOC problem with a \textit{linear base drift} and a correspondingly modified \textit{terminal cost}. This reformulation removes both sources of inefficiency; it enables training-time sampling with a few-step deterministic ODE solver and yields a closed-form adjoint solution that eliminates backward adjoint simulation. On standard text-to-image reward fine-tuning benchmarks, EAM converges up to 4x faster than AM and matches or surpasses it across various metrics including PickScore, ImageReward, HPSv2.1, CLIPScore and Aesthetics.

</details>


### [227] [Adaptive Calibration in Non-Stationary Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11490)
*Junyan Liu,Haipeng Luo,Lillian J. Ratliff*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种自适应校准的在线预测算法，能够根据环境的非平稳性程度自动调整校准误差，在平稳（i.i.d.）和完全对抗性情形之间平滑过渡。算法在$\ell_1$、$\ell_2$和伪KL校准误差上均实现了最优或近似最优的泛化性能，其误差界为$\widetilde{O}(\sqrt{T}+(TC)^{\frac{1}{3}})$（$\ell_1$）和$\widetilde{O}((1+C)^{\frac{1}{3}})$（$\ell_2$与伪KL），其中$C$为未知的非平稳度量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在完全对抗环境中表现保守，难以在更温和的平稳或近似平稳环境中发挥最优性能。因此需要设计一种能自适应环境非平稳性的在线预测算法，实现从i.i.d.到对抗情形的无缝过渡。

Method: 提出基于轮次调度和新型非均匀预测空间划分的方法，通过细粒度分配靠近真实值区域的分辨率，结合已有工作扩展，实现对多种校准度量的自适应保证。

Result: 算法在$\ell_1$校准误差上达到$\widetilde{O}(\sqrt{T}+(TC)^{\frac{1}{3}})$，在$\ell_2$和伪KL校准误差上达到$\widetilde{O}((1+C)^{\frac{1}{3}})$，在$C=0$（平稳）时恢复最优率，在$C=T$（全对抗）时匹配已知结果。

Conclusion: 本文成功回答了关于自适应校准在线预测的开放问题，所提算法在不同非平稳程度下均表现出良好性能，具有理论完备性和实际应用潜力。

Abstract: Making calibrated online predictions is a central challenge in modern AI systems. Much of the existing literature focuses on fully adversarial environments where outcomes may be arbitrary, leading to conservative algorithms that can perform suboptimally in more benign settings, such as when outcomes are nearly stationary. This gap raises a natural question: can we design online prediction algorithms whose calibration error automatically adapts to the degree of non-stationarity in the environment, smoothly interpolating between i.i.d. and adversarial regimes? We answer this question in the affirmative and develop a suite of algorithms that achieve adaptive calibration guarantees under multiple calibration measures. Specifically, with $T$ being the number of rounds and $C\in[0,T]$ being an unknown non-stationary measure defined as the minimal $\ell_1$ deviation of the mean outcomes, our algorithms attain $\widetilde{O}(\sqrt{T}+(TC)^{\frac{1}{3}})$ for $\ell_1$ calibration error and $\widetilde{O}((1+C)^{\frac{1}{3}})$ for both $\ell_2$ and pseudo KL calibration error. These bounds match the optimal rates in the stationary case ($C=0$) and recover known guarantees in the fully adversarial regime ($C=T$). Our approach builds on and extends prior work [Hu et al., 2026, Luo et al., 2025], introducing an epoch-based scheduling together with a novel non-uniform partition of the prediction space that allocates finer resolution near the underlying ground truth.

### [228] [Entropy Polarity in Reinforcement Fine-Tuning: Direction, Asymmetry, and Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11775)
*Jiazheng Zhang,Ziche Fu,Junrui Shen,Yunbin Zhao,Yunke Zhang,Zhiheng Xi,Long Ma,Chenxin An,Zhihao Zhang,Shichun Liu,Dingwei Zhu,Shihan Dou,Shaofan Liu,Han Li,Wiggin Zhou,Aiden Adams,Tao Gui,Fei Huang,Qi Zhang,Xuanjing Huang*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的熵力学理论框架，用于理解强化学习中策略熵的动态变化。通过分析采样更新对熵的影响，引入了“熵极性”这一符号化的词元级量，可预测更新是扩展还是收缩熵。研究发现，高频高概率词元的强化倾向于压缩熵，而扩张熵则需低概率样本或更强的分布修正。基于此，提出PAPO方法，通过优势重加权实现熵控制，并自适应地在扩张与收缩更新间分配优化压力，显著提升训练效率和奖励表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有熵感知方法主要依赖全局目标调节熵，缺乏对采样策略更新如何影响熵的词元级机制的理解。为更精细地控制探索与利用的平衡，亟需揭示熵变化的内在机制。

Method: 构建熵力学理论框架，推导熵变化的一阶近似公式，定义熵极性；设计PAPO算法，保留正负极性分支，利用经验熵轨迹作为在线信号，自适应调整优化压力。

Abstract: Policy entropy has emerged as a fundamental measure for understanding and controlling exploration in reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) for LLMs. However, existing entropy-aware methods mainly regulate entropy through global objectives, while the token-level mechanism by which sampled policy updates reshape policy entropy remains underexplored. In this work, we develop a theoretical framework of entropy mechanics in RLVR. Our analysis yields a first-order approximation of the entropy change, giving rise to entropy polarity, a signed token-level quantity that predicts how much a sampled update expands or contracts entropy. This analysis further reveals a structural asymmetry: reinforcing frequent high-probability tokens triggers contraction tendencies, whereas expansive tendencies typically require lower-probability samples or stronger distributional correction. Empirically, we show that entropy polarity reliably predicts entropy changes, and that positive and negative polarity branches play complementary roles in preserving exploration while strengthening exploitation. Building on these insights, we propose Polarity-Aware Policy Optimization (PAPO), which preserves both polarity branches and implements entropy control through advantage reweighting. With the empirical entropy trajectory as an online phase signal, PAPO adaptively reallocates optimization pressure between entropy-expanding and entropy-contracting updates. Experiments on mathematical reasoning and agentic benchmarks show that PAPO consistently outperforms competitive baselines, while delivering superior training efficiency and substantial reward improvements.

*Huimin Xu,Shuai Zhao,Xiaobao Wu,Anh Tuan Luu*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RLVR算法如GRPO存在熵崩溃问题，导致过早确定性和优化不稳定，现有解决方案如熵正则化和基于比率的剪裁方法存在粗粒度控制或依赖近似在线策略训练的缺陷。

Method: 从令牌级熵流角度重新审视熵崩溃问题，发现熵减少的令牌始终多于熵增加的令牌，导致熵流严重失衡；提出OPEFO机制，根据对熵变化的贡献动态调整熵增加和熵减少的更新，保持严格在线策略。

Result: 在六个数学推理基准测试中，OPEFO显著提升了训练稳定性和最终性能。

Conclusion: 通过令牌级熵流分析揭示了熵崩溃的根本原因，并提出了有效的自适应熵流平衡机制OPEFO，为改进大语言模型的强化学习训练提供了新思路。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has become an effective paradigm for improving the reasoning ability of large language models. However, widely used RLVR algorithms, such as GRPO, often suffer from entropy collapse, leading to premature determinism and unstable optimization. Existing remedies, including entropy regularization and ratio-based clipping heuristics, either control entropy in a coarse-grained manner or rely on approximate on-policy training. In this paper, we revisit entropy collapse from a token-level entropy flow perspective. Our analysis reveals that entropy-decreasing tokens consistently outweigh entropy-increasing ones, resulting in a severely imbalanced entropy flow. This perspective provides a unified explanation of entropy collapse in existing RLVR algorithms and highlights the importance of balancing entropy dynamics. Motivated by this analysis, we propose On-Policy Entropy Flow Optimization (OPEFO), an adaptive entropy flow balancing mechanism that rescales entropy-increasing and entropy-decreasing updates according to their contributions to entropy change, while remaining strict on-policy. Experiments on six mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that OPEFO improves training stability and final performance. We will release the code and models upon publication.

### [230] [ROMER: Expert Replacement and Router Calibration for Robust MoE LLMs on Analog Compute-in-Memory Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11800)
*Wenyong Zhou,Yuannuo Feng,Yizhe Chen,Taiqiang Wu,Wendong Xu,Wenbo Qi,Zhengwu Liu,Wang Kang,Ngai Wong*

TL;DR: 本文首次系统研究了在真实芯片测量校准的噪声模型下，基于MoE架构的大语言模型在噪声环境中的表现。发现硬件噪声严重破坏专家负载均衡，导致训练良好的路由决策变得次优。为此，提出ROMER框架，通过替换低频专家并重新校准路由器逻辑，有效缓解噪声影响，在多个基准测试中显著降低困惑度，证明其在不同MoE架构中的有效性与通用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MoE架构虽具可扩展性，但频繁的专家切换导致内存带宽瓶颈；虽然计算存储一体化（CIM）架构能缓解此问题，但其固有的硬件噪声会影响权重精度，进而影响MoE模型性能，而现有研究未充分探讨这一问题。因此亟需探索噪声对MoE模型的影响，并设计鲁棒优化方案。

Method: 提出ROMER框架，包含两个核心策略：(1) 将低频激活的专家替换为高频专家以恢复负载均衡；(2) 采用分位数归一化方法重新校准路由器输出的logits，增强路由在噪声下的稳定性。该方法基于后训练阶段进行，无需修改原始模型结构或训练流程。

Result: 在真实芯片噪声条件下，ROMER使DeepSeek-MoE、Qwen-MoE和OLMoE的困惑度分别降低58.6%、58.8%和59.8%，显著优于基线模型，且在多种模型架构上均表现出强泛化能力。

Conclusion: 硬件噪声会严重破坏MoE模型的专家负载均衡，导致原有路由策略失效。通过后训练阶段的专家重分配与路由校准，ROMER可有效提升模型在噪声环境下的鲁棒性与性能，为模拟型CIM系统部署高效MoE模型提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) with mixture-of-experts (MoE) architectures achieve remarkable scalability by sparsely activating a subset of experts per token, yet their frequent expert switching creates memory bandwidth bottlenecks that compute-in-memory (CIM) architectures are well-suited to mitigate. However, analog CIM systems suffer from inherent hardware imperfections that perturb stored weights, and its negative impact on MoE-based LLMs in noisy CIM environments remains unexplored. In this work, we present the first systematic investigation of MoE-based LLMs under noise model calibrated with real chip measurements, revealing that hardware noise critically disrupts expert load balance and renders clean-trained routing decisions consistently suboptimal. Based on these findings, we propose ROMER, a post-training calibration framework that (1) replaces underactivated experts with high-frequency ones to restore load balance, and (2) recalibrates router logits via percentile-based normalization to stabilize routing under noise. Extensive experiments across multiple benchmarks demonstrate that ROMER achieves up to 58.6\%, 58.8\%, and 59.8\% reduction in perplexity under real-chip noise conditions for DeepSeek-MoE, Qwen-MoE, and OLMoE, respectively, establishing its effectiveness and generalizability across diverse MoE architectures.

### [231] [More Edits, More Stable: Understanding the Lifelong Normalization in Sequential Model Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11836)
*Xin Ma,Wei Chen,Qi Liu,Derong Xu,Zhi Zheng,Tong Xu,Enhong Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了持续模型编辑中的灾难性遗忘和模型崩溃问题，提出通过终身归一化（LN）实现长期稳定性。分析揭示了自增强稳定循环机制，并证明结合岭回归的LN能产生渐近正交且有界参数更新，从而缓解遗忘与系统崩溃。基于此，提出了StableEdit方法，通过显式预热阶段和完全白化强化稳定环，实验验证其在长周期下的优越性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决大型语言模型在持续更新事实时面临的灾难性遗忘和模型崩溃问题，理解并改进现有编辑方法中终身归一化（LN）的作用机制。

Method: 提出理论分析框架，揭示终身归一化（LN）在长期编辑中的自增强稳定机制；结合岭回归推导出具有渐近正交性和有界范数的参数更新；设计StableEdit方法，引入显式预热与全白化以增强稳定性。

Conclusion: 终身归一化（LN）是实现长期模型编辑稳定性的关键机制，通过理论分析和新方法StableEdit的提出，为持续知识更新提供了可靠解决方案。

Abstract: Lifelong Model Editing aims to continuously update evolving facts in Large Language Models while preserving unrelated knowledge and general capabilities, yet it remains plagued by catastrophic forgetting and model collapse. Empirically, we find that recent editors resilient over long horizons share the same core strategy: Lifelong Normalization (LN), which normalizes value gradients using running statistics. Removing LN causes immediate performance collapse, and we observe a counter-intuitive positive cumulative effect where early edits can promote the success of future edits. Yet the mechanism of LN remains a "black box", leaving its precise role in lifelong stability poorly understood. In this work, we provide the first theoretical account of LN in the lifelong regime. Our analysis reveals a self-reinforcing stability loop and proves that, when combined with ridge-regularized regression, LN yields parameter updates with asymptotic orthogonality and bounded norms, directly mitigating forgetting and systemic collapse. Based on these insights, we derive StableEdit, which strengthens this stability loop via an explicit warm-up stage and full whitening, improving long-horizon stability at minimal overhead. Extensive experiments validate our theory and demonstrate competitive performance. Our code is available at https://github.com/MINE-USTC/StableEdit.

### [232] [EqOD: Symmetry-Informed Stability Selection for PDE Identification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11524)
*Gnankan Landry Regis N'guessan,Bum Jun Kim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: EqOD 是一种全自动的偏微分方程（PDE）数据驱动识别方法，结合了对称性约简与随机 LASSO 稳定选择两种库缩减机制。当轨迹数据中检测到伽利略不变性时，利用对称性约简后的算子库，排除在控制方程中不可能存在的项；否则采用基于经典假阳性边界引导的随机 LASSO 稳定选择，并以残差为基础的回退机制防止性能下降。在8个PDE、4种噪声水平下，EqOD在20%噪声的热方程上达到F1=1.000±0.000，显著优于WF-LASSO（0.475±0.181）、PySINDy 2.0（0.000）和WSINDy重实现（0.789）。在严格标准下，EqOD在32个测试单元中胜出7次，而WF-LASSO无胜绩，其余为平局。整体上，EqOD在32个单元中优于PySINDy 2.0.0的23次，所有PySINDy胜出均发生在反应型PDE上。外部验证在弱识别和PINN-SR数据集上均取得1.000的F1值。扩展研究涵盖非线性薛定谔方程、二维系统、耦合系统及圆柱尾流问题。伽利略库缩减在明确自治性和库假设下被证明有效，稳定选择步骤基于经典假阳性边界，但相关设计矩阵的正式保证仍待开放。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数据驱动的PDE识别依赖于稀疏回归与候选算子库，但过大的库易引入虚假项，过小的库又可能遗漏真实项。如何在保持高精度的同时减少误检并避免漏检，是关键挑战。本文旨在通过自动化的库缩减策略提升识别鲁棒性与准确性。

Method: 提出Equivariant Operator Discovery (EqOD) 方法，包含两个核心机制：(1) 基于弱形式结构测试检测伽利略不变性，若存在则使用对称性约简的算子库，排除不满足该对称性的项；(2) 否则应用随机LASSO稳定性选择，结合经典假阳性边界进行筛选，并设置残差基回退机制以保障最低性能。

Result: 在8个典型PDE、4种噪声水平下，EqOD在20%噪声热方程中实现F1=1.000±0.000，远超其他方法。在32个测试单元中，有7次显著胜出，其余多为平局或优于基准。在所有32个单元中，23次优于PySINDy 2.0.0，仅5次败于后者，且败因集中在反应型PDE。外部验证在清洁数据集上达到完美表现（F1=1.000）。扩展实验覆盖多种复杂系统。

Conclusion: EqOD通过融合对称性分析与统计稳定性选择，实现了高效、鲁棒且自动化的PDE发现，在噪声环境与复杂系统中均表现出色，显著超越现有主流方法，尤其在高噪声场景下优势明显。其理论基础部分已建立，未来可拓展至更多对称性与更复杂的相关性分析。

Abstract: Data-driven identification of partial differential equations (PDEs) relies on sparse regression over a candidate library of differential operators, where larger libraries inflate false positives under observation noise and smaller libraries risk missing true terms. We introduce Equivariant Operator Discovery (EqOD), a fully automatic method combining two library reduction mechanisms. When Galilean invariance is detected from trajectory data via a weak-form structural test, EqOD uses the symmetry-reduced library, eliminating terms that our Galilean exclusion result proves to be absent from the governing equation. Otherwise, it applies randomized LASSO stability selection guided by classical false-positive bounds. A residual-based fallback prevents degradation below the full-library baseline. On 8 PDEs at 4 noise levels, EqOD attains $F_1 = 1.000 \pm 0.000$ on Heat at $20\%$ noise, where WF-LASSO obtains $0.475 \pm 0.181$, official PySINDy 2.0 obtains $0.000$, and the WSINDy reimplementation obtains $0.789$. Under the strict criterion that the mean F1 difference exceeds the larger of the two standard deviations, EqOD wins 7 of 32 cells. WF-LASSO wins none, and the remaining 25 cells are ties. Across all 32 cells, EqOD outperforms PySINDy 2.0.0 in 23 of 32 cells, and all 5 PySINDy wins occur on reaction PDEs. External validation on WeakIdent and PINN-SR datasets gives $F_1 = 1.000$ on all 5 clean benchmarks. NLS, 2D, coupled-system, and cylinder-wake extensions are reported. The Galilean library reduction is proved under explicit autonomy and library assumptions. The stability-selection step is motivated by classical false-positive bounds, while formal guarantees for correlated PDE design matrices remain open.

</details>


### [233] [OverNaN: NaN-Aware Oversampling for Imbalanced Learning with Meaningful Missingness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11525)
*Amanda S Barnard*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: OverNaN 是一种轻量级的、支持缺失值（NaN）的过采样框架，旨在解决类别不平衡问题的同时保留缺失数据的结构信息。它不修复缺失值，而是将缺失性视为特征空间的一部分进行合成样本生成，避免因删除或填补缺失值而引入偏差或破坏类间边界。适用于科学与工程领域中小规模、不完整且不平衡的数据集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在许多实际应用中，缺失值本身包含重要信息，反映实验限制、测量选择或数据生成过程中的系统机制。传统方法通过删除或填补缺失值来处理，可能导致分类边界扭曲、引入偏差并降低模型泛化能力，尤其在少数类样本本就稀少的不平衡数据集中更为严重。因此需要一种能保留缺失结构的过采样方法。

Method: OverNaN 扩展了常见的合成过采样方法，使其可以直接作用于包含缺失值的特征向量。它允许缺失值被保留、传播或根据预定义策略选择性插值，而不是将其视为需修复的缺陷。该方法将缺失性作为特征空间的一部分参与样本生成，从而在不引入人工确定性的前提下保持缺失信息的语义。

Result: 实验证明，OverNaN 能有效在过采样过程中保留有意义的缺失结构，避免因处理缺失值而导致的信息损失或偏差。相比传统方法，在不平衡数据集上表现更优，提升了模型的鲁棒性和泛化能力。

Conclusion: OverNaN 提供了一种新的视角：缺失值不应被简单消除或填补，而应被视为数据的重要组成部分。该框架特别适合于科学与工程等缺失不可避免且常具信息性的场景，为不平衡学习与缺失数据处理提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Missing values are routinely treated as defects to be eliminated through deletion or imputation prior to machine learning. In many applied domains, however, missingness itself carries information, reflecting experimental constraints, measurement choices, or systematic mechanisms tied to the data-generating process. Eliminating or masking this structure can distort class boundaries, introduce bias, and reduce generalisability; particularly in imbalanced datasets where minority classes are already under-represented. OverNaN is a lightweight, NaN-aware oversampling framework designed to address class imbalance without erasing missingness structure. It extends common synthetic oversampling methods to operate directly on incomplete feature vectors, allowing missing values to be preserved, propagated, or selectively interpolated according to explicitly defined strategies. Rather than repairing missing data, OverNaN treats missingness as part of the feature space over which synthetic samples are generated. This paper situates OverNaN within the broader landscape of imbalanced learning, missing-data handling, and NaN-tolerant algorithms. Using representative examples included with the software, we demonstrate that meaningful missingness can be retained during oversampling without introducing artificial certainty. OverNaN is intended for practitioners working with small, incomplete, and imbalanced datasets in scientific and engineering domains where missingness is unavoidable and often informative.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: FERMI通过将关系成员信号映射到目标表的特征中，构建一个能够融合表间关系信息的成员推断模型，在推理阶段仅依赖目标表的属性值，但训练阶段利用关联表的辅助信息进行特征增强。

Abstract: Diffusion models are the leading approach for tabular data synthesis and are increasingly used to share sensitive records. Whether they actually protect privacy has become a pressing question. Membership inference attacks are the standard tool for this purpose, yet existing attacks assume a single-table setting and ignore the multi-relational structure of real sensitive data. A core challenge in assessing privacy risks from membership inference attacks in multi-table settings is how to leverage auxiliary information from relations associated with the target table, such as its parent tables. Particularly, we study a practical setting in which such auxiliary information is available only when training the attack model. At inference time, the attacker observes only the attribute values of the target record from the target table. We propose FERMI (FEature-mapping for Relational Membership Inference), which resolves this gap by enriching single-table features with relational membership signal. Across three tabular diffusion architectures and three real-world relational datasets, FERMI consistently improves attack performance over single-table baselines, with TPR@$0.1$FPR rising by up to 53% over the single-table baseline in the white-box setting and 22% in the black-box setting.

### [235] [Primal-Dual Policy Optimization for Linear CMDPs with Adversarial Losses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11535)
*Kihyun Yu,Seoungbin Bae,Dabeen Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个针对在线有限时域对抗性线性约束马尔可夫决策过程（CMDPs）的原始-对偶策略优化算法。该算法在损失函数由对手选择（全信息反馈）且成本为随机（贝叶斯反馈）的设定下，首次实现了子线性后悔和约束违反的界，均为$\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(K^{3/4})$，其中$K$为训练轮数。核心贡献包括：(i) 针对加权LogSumExp软最大化策略的新覆盖数分析；(ii) 两个新颖的算法组件——周期性策略混合与正则化对偶更新，有效控制了覆盖数和对偶变量。数值实验验证了理论结果的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有线性约束马尔可夫决策过程（CMDPs）研究主要集中在随机环境，但这类模型对对抗性环境敏感。为应对这一局限，本文考虑更现实的对抗性损失场景，同时保留成本的随机性，提出适用于此类复杂设定的鲁棒算法。

Method: 提出基于加权LogSumExp软最大化策略的新算法框架，结合周期性策略混合机制与正则化对偶更新策略，并引入新的覆盖数分析方法以控制算法复杂度和误差累积。

Result: 首次在对抗性损失+随机成本的设置下实现$\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(K^{3/4})$的子线性后悔与约束违反界，且实验验证了算法性能优越性。

Conclusion: 本工作为对抗性线性约束MDP提供了首个具有理论保障的在线学习算法，通过新策略结构与算法设计突破了传统方法的局限，为鲁棒决策学习开辟新路径。

Abstract: Existing work on linear constrained Markov decision processes (CMDPs) has primarily focused on stochastic settings, where the losses and costs are either fixed or drawn from fixed distributions. However, such formulations are inherently vulnerable to adversarially changing environments. To overcome this limitation, we propose a primal-dual policy optimization algorithm for online finite-horizon {adversarial} linear CMDPs, where the losses are adversarially chosen under full-information feedback and the costs are stochastic under bandit feedback. Our algorithm is the \emph{first} to achieve sublinear regret and constraint violation bounds in this setting, both bounded by $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(K^{3/4})$, where $K$ denotes the number of episodes. The algorithm introduces and runs with a new class of policies, which we call weighted LogSumExp softmax policies, designed to adapt to adversarially chosen loss functions. Our main result stems from the following key contributions: (i) a new covering number argument for the weighted LogSumExp softmax policies, and (ii) two novel algorithmic components -- periodic policy mixing and a regularized dual update -- which allow us to effectively control both the covering number and the dual variable. We also report numerical results that validate our theoretical findings on the performance of the algorithm.

However, MoE inference often suffers from suboptimal GPU utilization, load imbalance, and elevated latency arising from multiple tokens waiting on the same experts for their computation which arises from sparsity of expert activation. To address these challenges, we propose a dynamic expert replication strategy that predicts which experts are likely to be overloaded and replicates them for upcoming batches of tokens. The replicated experts process batch tokens concurrently across layers, which leads to improved parallelism, shorter GPU idle time, and significantly faster inference. Experimental evaluations conducted on large-scale MoE models, including Switch-base-128 and Switch-base-256, demonstrate that our method achieves near-complete GPU utilization (approx 100%), leading to upto 3x improvement in inference speed while preserving approximately 90-95% of the performance of baseline architectures

### [237] [Not How Many, But Which: Parameter Placement in Low-Rank Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12207)
*Arijit Sehanobish,Charles Lovering*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究LoRA适配器中参数放置问题：在固定预算下，选择哪些k个可训练参数是否重要？在监督微调（SFT）中，随机和有信息的选择表现相当；但在基于基础模型的GRPO训练中，随机放置无法超越基础模型，而基于梯度的信息放置可恢复标准LoRA性能。这种差异源于梯度结构：SFT梯度为低秩且方向稳定，任意子集均能积累一致更新；而GRPO梯度为高秩且近正交，只有梯度符号持续一致的参数才能保留学习信号。所提出的评分方法可在不到10秒内完成，仅需不到0.5%的训练成本，识别出关键参数，主要集中在残差流写入投影（V、O、Down）部分，且在不同模型规模（1.5B–8B）和架构间保持稳定。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一种基于梯度符号一致性的评分方法，用于快速识别在特定训练任务中具有关键学习信号的参数位置，结合小规模预训练评估实现高效筛选。

Result: 在监督微调中，随机与有信息选择性能相近；在GRPO训练中，随机放置无效，而梯度指导放置可恢复标准性能；所提方法可在极低成本下识别出关键参数，集中于残差流写入模块，且跨模型规模稳定。

Conclusion: 参数位置的重要性取决于训练范式和梯度结构；梯度符号一致性是决定参数有效性的重要指标，通过高效评分可精准定位关键参数，显著降低训练成本并提升效率。

Abstract: We study the \textit{parameter placement problem}: given a fixed budget of $k$ trainable entries within the B matrix of a LoRA adapter (A frozen), does the choice of which $k$ matter? Under supervised fine-tuning, random and informed subsets achieve comparable performance. Under GRPO on base models, random placement fails to improve over the base model, while gradient-informed placement recovers standard LoRA accuracy. This regime dependence traces to gradient structure: SFT gradients are low-rank and directionally stable, so any subset accumulates coherent updates; GRPO gradients are high-rank and near-orthogonal across steps, so only elements with consistently signed gradients retain the learning signal. Our scoring procedure identifies these critical parameters in under 10 seconds at less than 0.5% of training cost. Selected parameters concentrate on residual-stream-writing projections (V, O, Down), stable across model families and scales (1.5B - 8B).

### [238] [VNDUQE: Information-Theoretic Novelty Detection using Deep Variational Information Bottleneck](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11551)
*Aryan Gondkar,Hayder Radha,Yiming Deng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出VNDUQE方法，基于变分信息瓶颈（VIB）实现新颖性检测与不确定性量化，在MNIST数据集上通过KL散度和预测熵进行评估，结果显示两种指标互补：KL散度在远距离OOD样本上表现优异（噪声数据AUROC达100%），预测熵在近似OOD样本（新数字类）上表现最佳（94.7% AUROC）。结合两者可实现95.3%平均AUROC，显著优于基线MSP（85.0% AUROC，60.1% TPR），且信息瓶颈压缩降低38%期望校准误差，提升不确定性估计可靠性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用深度变分信息瓶颈（VIB）模型，通过控制学习表示中的信息流来约束表征，利用信息论指标（KL散度、预测熵）评估并检测不同类型的OOD样本，并设计联合检测策略以提升性能。

Conclusion: 基于信息瓶颈的VIB方法提供了更可靠、可解释的不确定性估计与新颖性检测能力，适用于主动学习等高成本计算场景，支持合理阈值设定以优化查询效率。

Abstract: Detecting out-of-distribution (OOD) samples is critical for safe deployment of neural networks in safety-critical applications. While maximum softmax probability (MSP) provides a simple baseline, it lacks theoretical grounding and suffers from miscalibration. We propose VNDUQE (VIB-based Novelty Detection and Uncertainty Quantification for Nondestructive Evaluation), which investigates novelty detection through the Deep Variational Information Bottleneck (VIB), which explicitly constrains information flow through learned representations. We train VIB models on MNIST with held-out digit classes and evaluate OOD detection using information-theoretic metrics: KL divergence and prediction entropy. Our results reveal complementary detection signals: KL divergence achieves perfect detection (100\% AUROC on noise) on far-OOD samples (noise, domain shift), while prediction entropy excels at near-OOD detection (94.7\% AUROC on novel digit classes). A parallel detection strategy combining both metrics achieves 95.3\% average AUROC and 92\% true positive rate at 5\% false positive rate, which is a 32 percentage point improvement over baseline MSP (85.0\% AUROC, 60.1\% TPR). Compression via the information bottleneck principle ($β=10^{-3}$) reduces Expected Calibration Error by 38\%, demonstrating that information-theoretic constraints produce fundamentally more reliable uncertainty estimates. These findings directly support active learning with expensive computational oracles, where well-calibrated novelty detection enables principled threshold selection for oracle queries.

### [239] [Solve the Loop: Attractor Models for Language and Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12466)
*Jacob Fein-Ashley,Paria Rashidinejad*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Attractor Models introduce a novel architecture that uses implicit differentiation to refine embeddings via fixed-point solving, enabling stable, adaptive iteration with constant memory cost. They outperform standard and looped Transformers in language modeling and reasoning tasks, achieving significant gains in accuracy and efficiency while allowing inference without the solver through equilibrium internalization.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing looped Transformers face challenges in training stability, optimization cost, and fixed recurrence depth. The goal is to enable scalable, adaptive iterative refinement without increasing memory or computational overhead.

Method: The model consists of a backbone that proposes initial embeddings and an attractor module that refines them by solving for fixed points using implicit differentiation. This allows gradients to flow through iterations without storing intermediate states, enabling constant memory usage regardless of effective depth.

Result: Attractor Models achieve up to 46.6% lower perplexity and 19.7% higher downstream accuracy than standard Transformers, with a 770M model surpassing a 1.3B Transformer trained on double the data. On reasoning tasks, a 27M-parameter model reaches 91.4% (Sudoku-Extreme) and 93.1% (Maze-Hard) accuracy—surpassing large frontier models like Claude and GPT-o3. Equilibrium internalization enables removal of the solver at inference with minimal loss.

Conclusion: Attractor Models make iterative refinement scalable by turning recurrence into a learnable, internalized process, offering superior performance, efficiency, and adaptability across diverse tasks.

Abstract: Looped Transformers offer a promising alternative to purely feed-forward computation by iteratively refining latent representations, improving language modeling and reasoning. Yet recurrent architectures remain unstable to train, costly to optimize and deploy, and constrained to small, fixed recurrence depths. We introduce Attractor Models, in which a backbone module first proposes output embeddings, then an attractor module refines them by solving for the fixed point, with gradients obtained through implicit differentiation. Thus, training memory remains constant in effective depth, and iterations are chosen adaptively by convergence. Empirically, Attractor Models outperform existing models across two regimes, large-scale language-model pretraining and reasoning with tiny models. In language modeling, Attractor Models deliver a Pareto improvement over standard Transformers and stable looped models across sizes, improving perplexity by up to 46.6% and downstream accuracy by up to 19.7% while reducing training cost. Notably, a 770M Attractor Model outperforms a 1.3B Transformer trained on twice as many tokens. On challenging reasoning tasks, we show that our model with only 27M parameters and approximately 1000 examples achieves 91.4% accuracy on Sudoku-Extreme and 93.1% on Maze-Hard, scaling favorably where frontier models like Claude and GPT o3, fail completely, and specialized recursive reasoners collapse at larger sizes. Lastly, we show that Attractor Models exhibit a novel phenomenon, which we call equilibrium internalization: fixed-point training places the model's initial output embedding near equilibrium, allowing the solver to be removed at inference time with little degradation. Together, these results suggest that Attractor Models make iterative refinement scalable by turning recurrence into a computation the model can learn to internalize.

</details>


### [240] [KV-Fold: One-Step KV-Cache Recurrence for Long-Context Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12471)
*Alireza Nadali,Patrick Cooper,Ashutosh Trivedi,Alvaro Velasquez*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: KV-Fold是一种无需训练的长上下文推理协议，通过将键值（KV）缓存视为左折叠中的累加器，实现对序列块的逐块递推处理。该方法利用已有的KV缓存拼接机制，使模型在处理每个新块时可复用先前块的内部状态，无需修改或重新训练模型。尽管方法简单，但其递推过程稳定：每步误差短暂上升后趋于平稳，且对数值精度、块大小和模型架构变化均具有鲁棒性。在‘针在 haystack’基准测试中，它在16K至128K token的上下文中实现了100%精确匹配检索，链深度达511，仅需单个40GB GPU内存。相比流式方法牺牲精度以换取内存限制，KV-Fold保持了长距离信息保留能力，且运行于一系列可处理的前向传播中。结果表明，冻结的预训练变换器已具备稳定的KV缓存递推能力，为无架构改动和训练的长上下文推理提供了实用路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长上下文推理方法要么需要额外训练，要么牺牲精度以控制内存使用。本文旨在探索是否可以在不修改模型架构或进行再训练的前提下，利用现有预训练模型的键值缓存机制实现稳定、高精度的长序列推理。

Method: 提出KV-Fold协议，将键值缓存作为左折叠的累加器，每次处理一个序列块时，基于累积的缓存进行条件生成，并将新产生的键值追加到缓存中，形成递推结构。该过程类似于函数式编程中的foldl操作，实现跨块的状态复用与信息传递。

Result: 在16K至128K token的上下文中，KV-Fold在152次实验中均实现100%精确匹配检索；链深度达511，且仅需单个40GB GPU内存。其递推误差随时间趋于稳定，对数值精度、块大小、模型类型均具鲁棒性。相较于流式方法，其在保持长距离信息准确性方面表现更优。

Conclusion: 冻结的预训练变换器已支持一种稳定的KV缓存递推机制。KV-Fold提供了一种无需训练或架构变更的高效长上下文推理方案，具有高精度、低内存开销和强泛化能力，为实际部署长上下文模型提供了可行路径。

Abstract: We introduce KV-Fold, a simple, training-free long-context inference protocol that treats the key-value (KV) cache as the accumulator in a left fold over sequence chunks. At each step, the model processes the next chunk conditioned on the accumulated cache, appends the newly produced keys and values, and passes the enlarged cache forward; the same one-step update is applied repeatedly, analogous to foldl in functional programming. Building on the KV cache concatenation primitive introduced for latent multi-agent communication, we repurpose it as a chunk-to-chunk recurrence for long-context inference. When processing chunk t, the model attends to the KV cache carried from earlier chunks as a prefix, reusing its internal state across segments without modifying or retraining the model. Despite its simplicity, the induced recurrence is stable: per-step drift rises briefly and then saturates into a flat plateau that persists across deep chains. This plateau is insensitive to a 10,000x change in numerical precision, robust across chunk sizes, and consistent across model families. At the task level, KV-Fold preserves exact information over long distances. On a needle-in-a-haystack benchmark, it achieves 100% exact-match retrieval across 152 trials spanning contexts from 16K to 128K tokens and chain depths up to 511 on Llama-3.1-8B, while remaining within the memory limits of a single 40GB GPU. Compared to streaming methods, which trade fidelity for bounded memory, KV-Fold maintains long-range retrieval while operating as a sequence of tractable forward passes. Overall, our results show that frozen pretrained transformers already support a stable form of KV-cache recurrence, providing a practical route to long-context inference without architectural changes or training.

</details>


### [241] [FedOUI: OUI-Guided Client Weighting for Federated Aggregation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11571)
*Alberto Fernández-Hernández,Jose I. Mestre,Cristian Pérez-Corral,Manuel F. Dolz,Jose Duato,Enrique S. Quintana-Ortí*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FedOUI提出一种基于激活的、无需标签的过拟合-欠拟合指示器（OUI）来改进联邦学习中的客户端更新聚合。通过在固定探针批次上计算OUI值，服务器根据每轮的OUI分布对结构异常的客户端赋予较低权重，从而提升聚合质量，尤其在强非独立同分布和噪声客户端条件下表现优异。该方法轻量且可解释性强，表明模型内部激活结构可为联邦聚合提供超越客户端规模与梯度几何的信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统联邦学习聚合方法主要依赖数据集大小或梯度层面的指标，忽略了客户端模型在训练过程中对输入空间的组织方式这一内部信号。为了更准确地识别和处理客户端异构性，需要一种能反映模型内部结构状态的新型评估机制。

Method: 提出基于激活的过拟合-欠拟合指示器（OUI），客户端在本地更新时附加其在固定探针批次上计算的OUI值；服务器估计每轮的OUI分布，并采用平滑重加权规则降低结构异常客户端的权重，实现更优的聚合策略。

Result: 在强非独立同分布（non-IID）和噪声客户端条件下，FedOUI相比FedAvg、FedProx及梯度对齐基线显著提升了聚合质量，尤其是在高异构场景下优势明显，同时保持了轻量与可解释性。

Conclusion: 模型内部激活结构能够为联邦学习聚合提供有价值的信息，超越传统的数据规模与梯度几何考量。引入OUI作为聚合依据，是一种有效且实用的改进方案。

Abstract: Federated learning usually aggregates client updates using dataset size or gradient-level criteria, while overlooking internal signals about how each client model is organizing its input space during training. We introduce FedOUI, a simple aggregation rule based on the Overfitting-Underfitting Indicator (OUI), an activation-based and label-free metric. Each participating client sends its local update together with a OUI value computed on a fixed probe batch, and the server estimates the round-wise OUI distribution to assign lower weights to structurally atypical clients through a smooth reweighting rule. We evaluate FedOUI on CIFAR-10 under strong non-IID partitioning and noisy-client conditions, comparing it with FedAvg, FedProx, and a gradient-alignment baseline. The clearest gains appear under strong heterogeneity, where OUI-based weighting improves aggregation quality while remaining lightweight and interpretable. These results show that internal activation structure can provide useful information for federated aggregation beyond client size and gradient geometry.

</details>


### [242] [Learning Weakly Communicating Average-Reward CMDPs: Strong Duality and Improved Regret](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11586)
*Kihyun Yu,Beomhan Baek,Dabeen Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究在弱连通假设下的无限时域平均奖励约束马尔可夫决策过程（CMDPs）。首先，建立了关于平稳策略的强对偶性，即使在缺乏线性规划形式且存在非凸性的情况下，仍通过细致分析访问测度集的几何结构证明了强对偶性的成立。其次，基于该结果，提出了一种原始-对偶剪裁值迭代算法，用于学习弱连通平均奖励线性CMDPs，实现了$\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(T^{2/3})$的遗憾和约束违反边界，优于现有最佳结果。该方法将剪裁值迭代扩展至约束设置，并采用有限时域近似以稳定对偶变量，关键在于利用强对偶性将复合拉格朗日遗憾分解为独立的遗憾与约束违反界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在弱连通的平均奖励约束马尔可夫决策过程中，传统方法因缺乏线性规划形式而难以处理非凸性问题。因此，需要建立强对偶性并设计高效算法来实现更优的学习性能。

Method: 通过分析访问测度集的几何结构建立强对偶性；提出一种原始-对偶剪裁值迭代算法，结合有限时域近似以稳定对偶变量，并利用强对偶性分解复合拉格朗日遗憾。

Result: 算法达到$\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(T^{2/3})$的遗憾和约束违反边界，优于现有最佳结果，且理论分析依赖于新提出的强对偶性分解方法。

Conclusion: 本工作首次在弱连通平均奖励CMDP框架下证明了强对偶性，并设计出具有改进性能保证的算法，为复杂约束强化学习提供了新的理论基础与有效工具。

Abstract: We study infinite-horizon average-reward constrained Markov decision processes (CMDPs) under the weakly communicating assumption. Our contributions are twofold. First, we establish strong duality for weakly communicating average-reward CMDPs over stationary policies with finite state and action spaces. Despite the absence of a linear programming formulation and the resulting nonconvexity under the weakly communicating setting, we show that strong duality still holds by carefully exploiting the geometric structure of the occupation measure set. Second, building on this result, we propose a primal--dual clipped value iteration algorithm for learning weakly communicating average-reward linear CMDPs. Our algorithm achieves regret and constraint violation bounds of $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(T^{2/3})$, improving upon the best known bounds, where $T$ denotes the number of interactions. Our approach extends clipped value iteration to the constrained setting and adapts it to a finite-horizon approximation, which stabilizes the dual variable and is crucial for achieving improved regret bounds. To analyze this, we develop a novel approach based on strong duality that enables the decomposition of the composite Lagrangian regret into separate bounds on regret and constraint violation.

### [243] [Stargazer: A Scalable Model-Fitting Benchmark Environment for AI Agents under Astrophysical Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15664)
*Xinge Liu,Terry Jingchen Zhang,Bernhard Schölkopf,Zhijing Jin,Kristen Menou*

TL;DR: Stargazer is a scalable, dynamic benchmark environment for evaluating AI agents on physics-grounded model-fitting tasks using radial-velocity time series data. The framework is designed to support training, evaluation, and scaling of AI strategies in scientific research contexts.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To address the need for dynamic, scientifically grounded benchmarks that can effectively evaluate autonomous AI agents in realistic research scenarios, particularly in astrophysics where accurate parameter recovery is crucial.

Method: Stargazer uses simulation-driven environments to generate synthetic radial-velocity time series data with varying complexity and noise levels. Agents are evaluated on their ability to fit models while respecting physical constraints, with performance measured both statistically and physically.

Result: Frontier AI agents frequently achieve good statistical fits but fail to recover true physical parameters. Increased test-time compute yields only marginal improvements, often resulting in recursive failure loops instead of effective exploration. This highlights a gap between numerical optimization and physical plausibility in current agents.

Conclusion: Stargazer provides a robust, scalable platform for training and evaluating AI agents on realistic, iterative model-fitting problems in science. Its design is generalizable to other scientific domains, offering a path toward more physically consistent AI-driven research tools.

Abstract: The rise of autonomous AI agents suggests that dynamic benchmark environments with built-in feedback on scientifically grounded tasks are needed to evaluate the capabilities of these agents in research work. We introduce Stargazer, a scalable environment for evaluating AI agents on dynamic, iterative physics-grounded model-fitting tasks using inference on radial-velocity (RV) time series data. Stargazer comprises 120 tasks across three difficulty tiers, including 20 real archival cases, covering diverse scenarios ranging from high-SNR single-planet systems to complex multi-planetary configurations requiring involved low-SNR analysis. Our evaluation of eight frontier agents reveals a gap between numerical optimization and adherence to physical constraints: although agents often achieve a good statistical fit, they frequently fail to recover correct physical system parameters, a limitation that persists even when agents are equipped with vanilla skills. Furthermore, increasing test-time compute yields only marginal gains, with excessive token usage often reflecting recursive failure loops rather than meaningful exploration. Stargazer presents an opportunity to train, evaluate, scaffold, and scale strategies on a model-fitting problem of practical research relevance today. Our methodology to design a simulation-driven environment for AI agents presumably generalizes to many other model-fitting problems across scientific domains. Source code and the project website are available at https://github.com/AIPS-UofT/Stargazer and https://aips-uoft.github.io/Stargazer/, respectively.

### [244] [SoK: Unlearnability and Unlearning for Model Dememorization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11592)
*Mengying Zhang,Derui Wang,Ruoxi Sun,Xiaoyu Xia,Shuang Hao,Minhui Xue*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前不可学习性和去记忆化方法在防止数据滥用方面面临浅层去记忆问题，如权重扰动下虚假的学习能力降低或知识遗忘，且二者之间存在复杂交互关系，缺乏理论保障，亟需系统性研究以提升防护深度和可靠性。

Method: 构建统一分类体系，通过实证实验分析主流方法的鲁棒性、交互特性及浅层去记忆现象，并基于认证去记忆化框架推导出首个关于去记忆深度的理论保证。

At the training stage, unlearnability embeds imperceptible perturbations into data before release to reduce learnability. At the post-training stage, unlearning removes previously acquired information from models to prevent unauthorized disclosure or use. While both defenses aim to preserve the right to withhold knowledge, their vulnerabilities and shared foundations remain unclear. Specifically, both unlearnability and unlearning suffer from issues such as shallow dememorization, leading to falsely claimed data learnability reduction or forgetting in the presence of weight perturbations. Moreover, input perturbations may affect the effectiveness of downstream unlearning, while unlearning may inadvertently recover domain knowledge hidden by unlearnability. This interplay calls for deeper investigation. Finally, there is a lack of formal guarantees to provide theoretical insights into current defenses against shallow dememorization. In this Systematization of Knowledge, we present the first integrated analysis of model dememorization approaches leveraging unlearnability and unlearning. Our contributions are threefold: (i) a unified taxonomy of unlearnability and scalable unlearning methods; (ii) an empirical evaluation revealing the robustness, interplay, and shallow dememorization of leading methods; and (iii) the first theoretical guarantee on dememorization depth for models processed through certified unlearning. These results lay the foundation for unifying dememorization mechanisms across the ML lifecycle to achieve a deeper immemor state for sensitive knowledge.

### [246] [From Generic Correlation to Input-Specific Credit in On-Policy Self Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11613)
*Guobin Shen,Lei Huang,Xiang Cheng,Chenxiao Zhao,Jindong Li,Dongcheng Zhao,Xing Yu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出CREDIT（Contrastive REward from DIsTillation），一种基于自蒸馏的新型奖励机制，旨在解决自蒸馏中奖励信号模糊的问题。通过分析发现，标准自蒸馏奖励等价于响应与反馈之间的点互信息（pMI），但该信息可能来自输入特定推理或通用捷径。为此，作者引入批次对比基线，分离出输入特定成分，从而提升奖励的可解释性与有效性。在多个基准测试中，CREDIT在几乎不增加计算成本的情况下实现了最优综合性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自蒸馏方法虽有效，但其奖励信号的含义不明确，可能被输入通用捷径误导。需要一种更精确、可分解的奖励机制来区分真正有意义的推理与表面捷径。

Method: 基于后验兼容性假设，将自蒸馏奖励解析为贝叶斯滤波增量，并推导其与点互信息（pMI）的关系；进一步沿输入维度分解教师对数概率，提出使用批次对比学习构建基线以隔离输入特定成分，形成新的序列级奖励函数CREDIT。

Result: 在代码生成、科学推理和工具使用等多个任务上，CREDIT显著优于现有方法，在多数情况下实现最佳综合表现，且额外计算开销极低。

Conclusion: CREDIT通过解耦输入特定与通用成分，提供了更可靠、更具解释性的自蒸馏奖励，为后训练语言模型中的奖励设计提供了新范式。

Abstract: On-policy self-distillation has emerged as a promising paradigm for post-training language models, in which the model conditions on environment feedback to serve as its own teacher, providing dense token-level rewards without external teacher models or step-level annotations. Despite its empirical success, what this reward actually measures and what kind of credit it assigns remain unclear. Under a posterior-compatibility interpretation of feedback conditioning, standard in the implicit-reward literature, we show that the self-distillation token reward is a Bayesian filtering increment whose trajectory sum is exactly the pointwise mutual information between the response and the feedback given the input. This pMI can be raised by input-specific reasoning or by input-generic shortcuts, so we further decompose the teacher log-probability along the input axis. Based on this analysis, we propose CREDIT (Contrastive REward from DIsTillation), which isolates the input-specific component with a batch-contrastive baseline. At the sequence level, CREDIT is a teacher-side surrogate for a contrastive pMI objective that also penalizes responses remaining likely under unrelated inputs. Across coding, scientific reasoning, and tool-use benchmarks on two model families, CREDIT delivers the strongest aggregate performance at negligible additional compute.

### [247] [MIST: Reliable Streaming Decision Trees for Online Class-Incremental Learning via McDiarmid Bound](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11617)
*Phu-Hoa Pham,Chi-Nguyen Tran,Nguyen Lam Phu Quy,Dao Sy Duy Minh,Huynh Trung Kiet,Long Tran-Thanh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MIST 提出一种新的流式决策树方法，解决传统方法在在线增量学习中因类别数增加导致的分裂准则不可靠和知识迁移缺失问题。通过引入与类别数无关的 McDiarmid 置信半径、贝叶斯继承协议以及 KLL 分位数摘要结构，实现稳定且高效的持续学习性能，在标准和压力测试数据集上表现优异，尤其在非高斯分布场景下显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统流式决策树在类别数增加时，信息增益范围随 log2 K 增长，导致基于 Hoeffding 风险的分裂准则失效，无法实现类独立的分裂判断；同时缺乏分裂时的知识迁移机制，限制了其在持续学习中的应用。

Method: 提出 MIST 方法，包含三个核心组件：(1) 使用 McDiarmid 不等式推导出与类别数无关的紧致置信半径，作为 Gini 划分的结构正则化；(2) 设计贝叶斯继承协议，通过截断高斯矩将父节点统计量传递至子节点，强化保守分裂时的方差减少效果；(3) 每个叶子节点采用 KLL 分位数草图，统一支持连续阈值评估与自适应几何预测。

Result: 在标准和压力测试的表格流数据上，MIST 在近高斯基准任务中与全局参数化方法相当，在非高斯几何场景中表现出唯一鲁棒性，显著超越当前最优方法（SOTA）的表现。

Conclusion: MIST 通过结构性设计解决了流式决策树在类增量学习中的根本缺陷，实现了类别数无关的稳定分裂与有效知识迁移，是面向开放世界持续学习的理想候选方案。

Abstract: Streaming decision trees are natural candidates for open-world continual learning, as they perform local updates, enjoy bounded memory, and static decision boundaries. Despite these, they still fail in online class-incremental learning due to two coupled miscalibrations: (i) their split criterion grows unreliable as the class count K expands, and (ii) the absence of knowledge transfer at split time. Both failures share a common root: the range of Information Gain intrinsically scales with log2 K. Consequently, any Hoeffding-style confidence radius derived from it must inevitably grow with the class count, making a K-independent split criterion structurally impossible, taking away the potential benefits of applying streaming decision trees to continual learning. To fix this issue, we present MIST (McDiarmid Incremental Streaming Tree), which resolves both failures through three integrated components: (i) a tight, K-independent McDiarmid confidence radius for Gini splitting that acts as a structural regulariser; (ii) a Bayesian inheritance protocol that projects parent statistics to child nodes via truncated-Gaussian moments, with variance reduction guarantees strongest precisely when splitting is most conservative; and (iii) per-leaf KLL quantile sketches that support both continuous threshold evaluation and geometry-adaptive leaf prediction from a single data structure. On standard and stress-test tabular streams, MIST is competitive with global parametric methods on near-Gaussian benchmarks and uniquely robust on non-Gaussian geometry where SOTA benchmarks collapse.

</details>

### [248] [A Cascaded Generative Approach for e-Commerce Recommendations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11118)

While effective in optimizing for aggregate preferences, this paradigm is rigid and can limit personalization and semantic cohesion across the page. This makes it poorly suited to support dynamic objectives and merchandising requirements over time. To address this, we introduce a cascaded merchandising framework that decomposes storefront construction into two generative tasks: (i) placement-level theme generation and (ii) constrained keyword generation per placement to power product retrieval. Teacher-student fine-tuning is leveraged to improve scalability of this framework under production latency and cost constraints. Fine-tuned model ablations are shown to approach closed-weight LLM performance. We further contribute frameworks for AI-driven content evaluation and quality filtering, enabling safe and automated deployment of dynamic content at scale. Generative output is fused with traditional ranking models to preserve hybrid infrastructure. In online experiments, this framework yields an estimated +2.7% lift in cart adds per page view over a strong baseline.

### [249] [EVOCHAMBER: Test-Time Co-evolution of Multi-Agent System at Individual, Team, and Population Scales](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11136)
*Yaolun Zhang,Tianyi Xu,Shengyu Dai,Zhenwen Shao,Qingyun Wu,Huazheng Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: EVOCHAMBER 是一个无需训练的多智能体测试时演化框架，通过在团队、种群和协作结构三个层面实现协同演化，解决单智能体方法无法捕捉的跨智能体学习与分工问题。其核心是 CODREAM（协作幻觉）协议，在团队失败或分歧时触发，使智能体协同反思并不对称地将知识从强到弱传递，保留专业化同时填补知识空白。该框架在数学、代码和多领域推理任务上分别达到63.9%、75.7%和87.1%的准确率，显著优于基线，且自发涌现出4-5个稳定的专用角色，体现了多智能体演化的独特结构特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有测试时演化方法要么将经验局限于单个智能体，丧失跨智能体学习能力；要么对所有智能体广播信息，抹去合作带来的专业化优势。而真实多智能体系统中存在协作对象选择、协作方式演化及知识流动路径等复杂机制，这些是单智能体无法表达的。因此需要一种能支持跨智能体不对称知识传递与动态协作结构演化的框架。

Method: 提出 EVOCHAMBER 框架，包含三层次演化机制：1）团队级操作符根据任务条件在线构建团队并选择协作结构；2）种群级生命周期操作符（如分叉、合并、修剪、播种）在性能压力下动态调整种群；3）核心为 CODREAM 协作幻觉协议，团队失败后触发，智能体协同反思、提炼见解，并以非对称方式将知识从强智体传至弱智体，保持专业化。

Result: 在三个异构任务流上，使用 Qwen3-8B 模型，EVOCHAMBER 在竞赛数学任务上达 63.9%，代码任务上达 75.7%，多领域推理任务上达 87.1%，相较最佳基线提升 32% 相对性能；消融实验证明不对称跨智能体传递是主要驱动力；初始相同初始化的多个智能体自发形成 4-5 个稳定的专业化角色，体现多智能体演化的结构性特征。

Conclusion: 多智能体测试时演化超越单智能体重复，其核心在于协作对象、协作方式与知识流动路径的共同演化，带来如专业化等涌现现象。EVOCHAMBER 通过不对称知识传递与动态协作结构演化，实现了高效、可扩展的多智能体协同进化，验证了跨智能体不对称学习的重要性，并揭示出多智能体系统特有的自组织结构。

Abstract: We argue that multi-agent test-time evolution is not single-agent evolution replicated N times. A single-agent learner can only evolve its own context and memory. A multi-agent system additionally evolves who collaborates, how they collaborate, and how knowledge flows across the population. These components have no single-agent counterpart and can produce phenomena such as emergent specialization. Yet prior test-time methods either confine experiences to individual agents, forfeiting cross-agent learning, or broadcast symmetrically to all agents, erasing the specialization that makes collaboration valuable. We present EVOCHAMBER, a training-free framework that instantiates test-time evolution at three levels over a coevolving agent pool. At its core is CODREAM (Collaborative Dreaming), a post-task protocol triggered on team failure or disagreement, in which agents collaboratively reflect, distill insights, and route them asymmetrically from strong to weak agents on the failed niche, preserving specialization while filling knowledge gaps. Team-level operators assemble niche-conditioned teams and select collaboration structures online. Population-level lifecycle operators fork, merge, prune, and seed agents under performance pressure. On three heterogeneous task streams with Qwen3-8B, EVOCHAMBER reaches 63.9% on competition math, 75.7% on code, and 87.1% on multi-domain reasoning, outperforming the best baseline by 32% relative on math and confirming asymmetric cross-agent transfer as the primary driver in ablation. Starting from several identically initialized agents, four to five stable niche specialists spontaneously emerge, a structural signature of multi-agent evolution that no single-agent learner can express. See our code at: https://github.com/Mercury7353/EvoChamber

</details>


### [250] [RankQ: Offline-to-Online Reinforcement Learning via Self-Supervised Action Ranking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11151)
*Andrew Choi,Wei Xu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: RankQ是一种新的离线到在线强化学习方法，通过引入自监督多级排序损失来改进Q-learning，避免对未见动作的统一惩罚，从而更有效地指导策略优化。在稀疏奖励任务和视觉机器人学习中表现优异，显著提升模拟与真实世界性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖悲观主义来减少值函数过估计，但会将行为克隆作为锚点，限制在线策略改进；尤其当数据集中动作质量不佳时问题更严重。

Method: 提出RankQ，结合时序差分学习与自监督多项排序损失，学习动作间的相对偏好关系，而非对未知动作进行统一惩罚，从而引导Q函数向高质量行为方向优化。

Result: 在D4RL稀疏奖励基准测试中表现优于或媲美七种先前方法；在基于视觉的机器人学习中，低数据情况下模拟成功率平均提高42.7%，高数据下提升13.7%；实现强仿真到现实迁移，真实立方体堆叠成功率从43.1%提升至84.7%。

Conclusion: RankQ通过结构化动作排序有效缓解了离线数据覆盖不足带来的挑战，提升了在线策略优化能力，在多种复杂任务中展现出卓越性能，尤其适用于低数据和高现实迁移场景。

Abstract: Offline-to-online reinforcement learning (RL) improves sample efficiency by leveraging pre-collected datasets prior to online interaction. A key challenge, however, is learning an accurate critic in large state--action spaces with limited dataset coverage. To mitigate harmful updates from value overestimation, prior methods impose pessimism by down-weighting out-of-distribution (OOD) actions relative to dataset actions. While effective, this essentially acts as a behavior cloning anchor and can hinder downstream online policy improvement when dataset actions are suboptimal. We propose RankQ, an offline-to-online Q-learning objective that augments temporal-difference learning with a self-supervised multi-term ranking loss to enforce structured action ordering. By learning relative action preferences rather than uniformly penalizing unseen actions, RankQ shapes the Q-function such that action gradients are directed toward higher-quality behaviors. Across sparse reward D4RL benchmarks, RankQ achieves performance competitive with or superior to seven prior methods. In vision-based robot learning, RankQ enables effective offline-to-online fine-tuning of a pretrained vision-language-action (VLA) model in a low-data regime, achieving on average a 42.7% higher simulation success rate than the next best method. In a high-data setting, RankQ improves simulation performance by 13.7% over the next best method and achieves strong sim-to-real transfer, increasing real-world cube stacking success from 43.1% to 84.7% relative to the VLA's initial performance.

</details>


### [251] [The Many Faces of On-Policy Distillation: Pitfalls, Mechanisms, and Fixes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11182)
*Siqi Zhu,Xuyan Ye,Hongyu Lu,Weiye Shi,Ge Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究系统评估了在大语言模型中使用on-policy distillation (OPD)和on-policy self-distillation (OPSD)的有效性与局限性。发现OPD对教师选择和损失函数高度敏感，而OPSD在缺乏实例特定特权信息（PI）时会失败；但当PI代表共享的潜在规则（如系统提示或对齐偏好）时，OPSD表现良好。识别出三种失效机制：(1) 由学生生成前缀条件导致的师生分布不匹配；(2) 受限于偏差的TopK反KL梯度引发优化不稳定；(3) 学生学习到无PI的策略，无法捕捉实例特定的条件。提出使用停止梯度的TopK目标、适应RLVR的教师和SFT稳定的学生来缓解这些问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究表明OPD和OPSD在提示工程和知识内化方面有潜力，但其效果存在不一致，且出现不稳定和性能下降问题。因此亟需系统理解这些方法在何种条件下有效或失效，以指导实际应用并改进方法设计。

Method: 通过大规模实证研究，对比不同设置下OPD与OPSD的表现，分析教师选择、损失函数、特权信息类型等因素的影响；识别失效原因，并设计改进方案如停止梯度的TopK目标、适应性教师和稳定化的学生训练。

Result: OPD在数学推理任务中对教师和损失形式极为敏感；OPSD在缺少实例特定特权信息时失败，但在共享规则场景下有效；提出了三种关键失效机制，并验证了停止梯度、RLVR适配教师和SFT稳定学生可显著缓解问题。

Conclusion: OPD和OPSD并非通用有效，其成功依赖于教师质量、损失设计及特权信息性质。只有在满足特定条件时才有效，尤其当特权信息是共享而非实例特异时。通过合理设计目标函数与训练流程，可显著提升其稳定性与性能。

Abstract: On-policy distillation (OPD) and on-policy self-distillation (OPSD) have emerged as promising post-training methods for large language models, offering dense token-level supervision on trajectories sampled from the model's own policy. However, existing results on their effectiveness remain mixed: while OP(S)D has shown promise in system prompt and knowledge internalization, recent studies also report instability and degradation. In this work, we present a comprehensive empirical study of when OPD and OPSD work, when they fail, and why. We find that OPD on mathematical reasoning is highly sensitive to teacher choice and loss formulation, whereas OPSD fails in our tested settings due to test-time absence of instance-specific privileged information (PI). In contrast, OPSD is effective when PI represents a shared latent rule, such as a system prompt or alignment preference. We identify three failure mechanisms: (1) distribution mismatch between teacher and student caused by conditioning on student-generated prefixes, (2) optimization instability from biased TopK reverse-KL gradients, and (3) an OPSD-specific limitation where the student learns a PI-free policy that aggregates PI-conditioned teachers, which is insufficient when PI is instance-specific. We further show that stop-gradient TopK objectives, RLVR-adapted teachers, and SFT-stabilized students mitigate these failures.

</details>


### [252] [Don't Look at the Numbers: Visual Anchoring Bias and Layer-wise Representation in VLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11218)
*M. Shalankin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 嵌入式数值锚点系统性地扭曲了六种来自五个架构家族的视觉语言模型的质量判断，其影响是严重图像质量退化的2.5倍，表明这种偏差并非由视觉变化引起。层间探测显示，锚点分类饱和的层（L12-L34）不适合质量预测，而更深层的层表现更优（R^2 = 0.69-0.91）。融合分析揭示了架构依赖性的信息整合方式：两种模型在早期（L1-L2）进行即时融合，而其他三种模型则呈现部分或无融合。研究建立了视觉锚定偏见的因果解释，将行为易感性与表征动态联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示视觉语言模型在质量判断中受到嵌入式数值锚点的系统性偏见，探究其背后机制及对模型性能的影响。

Method: 通过方差分析（ANOVA）、层间探测、融合分析等方法，评估不同视觉语言模型在存在嵌入式数值锚点时的表现差异，识别关键层级和融合模式。

Result: 嵌入式数值锚点导致显著的系统性偏差，其影响远超图像质量退化；锚点分类饱和层不适用于质量预测，最优预测层位于更深位置；不同模型表现出不同的信息融合策略。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了视觉锚定偏见的因果机制，揭示了模型架构与表示动态之间的关系，为理解并缓解视觉语言模型中的认知偏差提供了重要依据。

Abstract: Embedded numeric anchors on images systematically bias Vision-Language Model quality judgments across six VLMs from five architectural families (ANOVA eta^2 = 0.18-0.77, all p < 0.001). Anchor effects are 2.5x larger than severe image quality degradation, confirming bias is not reducible to visual changes. Layer-wise probing reveals consistent dissociation: layers where anchor classification saturates (L12-L34) are suboptimal for quality prediction, with optimal layers deeper (R^2 = 0.69-0.91). Fusion analysis identifies architecture-dependent integration -- instant fusion at L1-L2 in two models versus partial or no fusion in three others. These results establish a causal account of visual anchoring bias, linking behavioral susceptibility to representation dynamics.

Method: VLATIM is structured into five progressively challenging tasks within TIM, measuring capabilities from basic visual grounding to full puzzle solving. It evaluates how well models can reason about physical interactions and translate those plans into precise mouse-based actions.

Result: Large proprietary models perform well in high-level planning but struggle with precise visual grounding and accurate mouse control, leading to poor execution. This reveals a significant gap between reasoning and action execution, preventing current models from achieving human-like problem-solving performance.

Abstract: Vision-Language(-Action) Models (VLMs) are increasingly applied to interactive environments, yet existing benchmarks often overlook the complex physical reasoning required for point-and-click puzzle games. Unlike existing benchmarks, VLATIM specifically targets the critical gap between high-level logical reasoning and continuous action spaces requiring precise mouse interactions. This benchmark is structured into five progressive parts, assessing capabilities that range from basic visual grounding and domain understanding to multi-step manipulation and full puzzle solving. Our results reveal a significant disparity between reasoning and execution. While large proprietary models demonstrate superior planning abilities, they struggle with precise visual grounding. Consequently, they do not yet show human-like problem-solving capabilities.

### [254] [Unlocking LLM Creativity in Science through Analogical Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11258)
*Andrew Shen,Shaul Druckmann,James Zou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究评估了大语言模型（LLM）在开放式解决方案生成任务中的表现，发现其存在模式崩溃导致多样性不足的问题。为此，提出基于类比推理（AR）的新方法，通过跨领域问题的结构相似性生成类比，从而探索新颖解决方案。相比基线方法，AR显著提升解决方案多样性（提升90-173%），在超过50%的情况下生成新解（基线低至1.6%），并产生高质量类比。在四个生物医学问题上的实证验证表明，AR方法在扰动效应预测、细胞间通讯预测、脑区相互作用推断及寡核苷酸性质预测等任务中均取得显著性能提升，部分指标达近13倍改进，且优于现有方法，证明其在真实世界中的可行性与有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前自主科学面临挑战，尤其是在复杂领域如生物医学中，需要AI系统能持续生成新颖且多样化的解决方案。然而，现有大语言模型在开放式问题求解中易出现模式崩溃，导致生成结果缺乏多样性，限制了科学发现的潜力。因此亟需一种能够有效提升生成多样性和创新性的新方法。

Method: 提出类比推理（Analogical Reasoning, AR）作为解决方案生成的新范式。该方法首先识别跨领域问题之间的共享关系结构，构建类比；然后利用这些类比启发搜索过程，引导生成具有新颖性和多样性的解决方案。整个框架不依赖特定领域知识，强调关系结构的迁移能力。

Result: AR在多个指标上显著优于基线：解决方案多样性提升90-173%；生成新解的比例超过50%，远高于基线最低1.6%；在四个真实生物医学任务中实现显著性能提升：扰动效应预测分布指标改善近13倍，细胞间通讯预测AUPRC更高，脑区交互推断与已有方法相关性高达ρ=0.729，寡核苷酸性质预测在两个数据集上达到最先进水平。

Conclusion: 类比推理（AR）是一种高效、可扩展且真实可行的解决方案生成策略，能有效缓解大语言模型的模式崩溃问题，大幅增强生成方案的多样性与创新性。该方法不仅在理论上具备优势，在实际生物医学应用中也展现出卓越性能，可作为现有方法的重要补充或增强工具，推动自主科学的发展。

Abstract: Autonomous science promises to augment scientific discovery, particularly in complex fields like biomedicine. However, this requires AI systems that can consistently generate novel and diverse solutions to open-ended problems. We evaluate LLMs on the task of open-ended solution generation and quantify their tendency to mode collapse into low-diversity generations. To mitigate this mode collapse, we introduce analogical reasoning (AR) as a new approach to solution generation. AR generates analogies to cross-domain problems based on shared relational structure, then uses those analogies to search for novel solutions. Compared to baselines, AR discovers significantly more diverse generations (improving solution diversity metrics by 90-173%), generates novel solutions over 50% of the time (compared to as little as 1.6% for baselines), and produces high-quality analogies. To validate the real-world feasibility of AR, we implement AR-generated solutions across four biomedical problems, yielding consistent quantitative gains. AR-generated approaches achieve a nearly 13-fold improvement on distributional metrics for perturbation effect prediction, outperform all baselines on AUPRC when predicting cell-cell communication, infer brain region interactions with a high Spearman correlation ($ρ$=0.729) to published methods, and establish state-of-the-art performance on 2 datasets for oligonucleotide property prediction. The novel and diverse solutions produced by AR can be used to augment the search space of existing solution generation methods.

### [255] [LatentRouter: Can We Choose the Right Multimodal Model Before Seeing Its Answer?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11301)
*Xueqi Cheng,Yushun Dong*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: LatentRouter 是一种基于潜在空间通信的多模态大语言模型（MLLM）路由机制，通过预测不同模型在给定图像-问题输入下的反事实性能来实现高效匹配。它利用学习到的多模态路由胶囊和模型能力标记，在潜在空间中进行交互以估计各模型的性能表现，并通过分布输出头和胶囊修正模块优化决策，尤其在视觉、布局敏感或推理导向任务上表现显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 MLLM 路由方法通常仅基于查询难度进行选择，忽略了不同模型在 OCR、图表理解、空间推理等多方面能力的差异。为了更精准地将输入需求与模型能力匹配，需要一种能够理解多模态需求并动态评估模型潜力的智能路由机制。

Method: LatentRouter 将 MLLM 路由建模为反事实多模态效用预测问题。首先提取图像-问题输入的多模态路由胶囊，将每个候选 MLLM 表示为一个模型能力令牌，然后在潜在空间中进行跨状态通信，以模拟若选择某模型时的预期表现。采用分布式输出头预测各模型的反事实质量，结合有界胶囊修正模块防止近似决策中的信号溢出，最终生成基于效用的路由策略。

Result: 在 MMR-Bench 和 VL-RouterBench 上的实验表明，LatentRouter 显著优于固定模型、特征级及学习型路由器基线。其优势在视觉依赖、布局敏感和推理密集型任务组中尤为明显，且潜空间通信是性能提升的核心因素。

Conclusion: LatentRouter 通过反事实效用预测和潜在空间通信，实现了对 MLLM 多样化能力的精准捕捉与动态匹配，为多模态任务提供了高性能、低延迟且可扩展的路由解决方案。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) have heterogeneous strengths across OCR, chart understanding, spatial reasoning, visual question answering, cost, and latency. Effective MLLM routing therefore requires more than estimating query difficulty: a router must match the multimodal requirements of the current image-question input with the capabilities of each candidate model. We propose LatentRouter, a router that formulates MLLM routing as counterfactual multimodal utility prediction. Given an image-question query, LatentRouter extracts learned multimodal routing capsules, represents each candidate MLLM with a model capability token, and performs latent communication between these states to estimate how each model would perform if selected. A distributional outcome head predicts model-specific counterfactual quality, while a bounded capsule correction refines close decisions without allowing residual signals to dominate the prediction. The resulting utility-based policy supports performance-oriented and performance-cost routing, and handles changing candidate pools through shared per-model scoring with availability masking. Experiments on MMR-Bench and VL-RouterBench show that LatentRouter outperforms fixed-model, feature-level, and learned-router baselines. Additional analyses show that the gains are strongest on multimodal task groups where model choice depends on visual, layout-sensitive, or reasoning-oriented requirements, and that latent communication is the main contributor to the improvement. The code is available at: https://github.com/LabRAI/LatentRouter.

</details>


### [256] [Constraint-Data-Value-Maximization: Utilizing Data Attribution for Effective Data Pruning in Low-Data Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11312)
*Danilo Brajovic,David A. Kreplin,Marco F. Huber*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出CDVM方法，用于在数据量有限的情况下更有效地通过数据归因进行数据剪枝。传统基于Shapley的数据值在低数据场景下表现不佳，而CDVM通过约束优化，同时最大化总影响并惩罚单个测试的过度贡献，提升了性能与鲁棒性，在OpenDataVal基准上表现优异且运行效率高。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于Shapley的数据值在数据量少时不适合用于剪枝低价值数据，亟需一种在低数据场景下更有效的数据归因方法。

Method: 提出约束数据值最大化（CDVM）方法，将剪枝建模为一个约束优化问题，目标是最大化总数据影响，同时对单个测试样本的贡献进行惩罚，以避免过度依赖少数样本。

Result: 在OpenDataVal基准测试中，CDVM表现出色，不仅性能优于现有方法，而且具有竞争力的运行时间，尤其在小数据量场景下优势明显。

Conclusion: CDVM是一种在低数据条件下有效利用数据归因进行剪枝的新方法，能够显著提升模型在数据稀缺情况下的鲁棒性和性能。

Abstract: Attributing model behavior to training data is an evolving research field. A common benchmark is data removal, which involves eliminating data instances with either low or high values, then assessing a model's performance trained on the modified dataset. Many existing studies leverage Shapley-based data values for this task. In this paper, we demonstrate that these data values are not optimally suited for pruning low-value data when only a limited amount of data remains. To address this limitation, we introduce the Constraint-Data-Value-Maximization (CDVM) approach, which effectively utilizes data attributions for pruning in low-data scenarios. By casting pruning as a constrained optimization that both maximizes total influence and penalizes excessive per-test contributions, CDVM delivers robust performance when only a small fraction of the data is retained. On the OpenDataVal benchmark, CDVM shows strong performance and competitive runtime.

### [257] [Rethinking Evaluation for LLM Hallucination Detection: A Desiderata, A New RAG-based Benchmark, New Insights](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11330)
*Wenbo Chen,Veena Padmanabhan,Tootiya Giyahchi,Elaine Wong,Leman Akoglu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有幻觉检测基准存在缺陷，如缺乏长上下文支持和真实世界中的标签噪声模拟，限制了检测器的有效评估。

Result: T RIVIA+具备所有理想属性；现有检测器性能仍有提升空间；基础LLM作为裁判表现良好；标签噪声显著降低检测效果。

Conclusion: T RIVIA+为评估基于RAG的幻觉检测提供了高质量基准，推动该领域研究发展。

Abstract: Hallucination, broadly referring to unfaithful, fabricated, or inconsistent content generated by LLMs, has wide-ranging implications. Therefore, a large body of effort has been devoted to detecting LLM hallucinations, as well as designing benchmark datasets for evaluating these detectors. In this work, we first establish a desiderata of properties for hallucination detection benchmarks (HDBs) to exhibit for effective evaluation. A critical look at existing HDBs through the lens of our desiderata reveals that none of them exhibits all the properties. We identify two largest gaps: (1) RAG-based grounded benchmarks with long context are severely lacking (partly because length impedes human annotation); and (2) Existing benchmarks do not make available realistic label noise for stress-testing detectors although real-world use-cases often grapple with label noise due to human or automated/weak annotation. To close these gaps, we build and open-source a new RAG-based HDB called T RIVIA+ that underwent a rigorous human annotation process. Notably, our benchmark exhibits all desirable properties including (1) T RIVIA+ contains samples with the longest context in the literature; and (2) we design and share four sets of noisy labels with different, both sample-dependent and sampleindependent, noise schemes. Finally, we perform experiments on RAG-based HDBs, including our T RIVIA+, using popular SOTA detectors that reveal new insights: (i) ample room remains for current detectors to reach the performance ceiling on RAG-based HDBs, (ii) the basic LLM-as-a-Judge baseline performs competitively, and (iii) label noise hinders detection performance. We expect that our findings, along with our proposed benchmark 1 , will motivate and foster needed research on hallucination detection for RAG-based tasks.

Method: CVEvolve采用多轮搜索策略，交替进行发现与优化动作，结合代码执行、评估实现、历史管理、留出测试及可选的科学数据与可视化检查功能，使用谱系感知的随机候选采样机制以平衡探索与利用。

Conclusion: 零代码、自主的LLM驱动算法开发能够帮助领域科学家将非结构化的科学图像数据转化为实用算法，并推动后续科学发现。

Abstract: Scientific data processing often requires task-specific algorithms or AI models, creating a barrier for domain scientists who need to analyze their data but may not have extensive computing or image-processing expertise. This barrier is especially pronounced when data are noisy, have a high dynamic range, are sparsely labeled, or are only loosely specified. We introduce CVEvolve, an autonomous agentic harness with a zero-code interface for scientific data-processing algorithm discovery. CVEvolve combines a multi-round search strategy with tools for code execution, evaluation implementation, history management, holdout testing, and optional inspection of scientific data and visual outputs. The search alternates between discovery and improvement actions, and uses lineage-aware stochastic candidate sampling to balance exploration and exploitation. We demonstrate CVEvolve on x-ray fluorescence microscopy image registration, Bragg peak detection, and high-energy diffraction microscopy image segmentation. Across these tasks, CVEvolve discovers algorithms that improve over baseline methods, while holdout test tracking helps identify candidates that generalize better than later over-optimized alternatives. These results show that zero-code, autonomous LLM-powered algorithm development can help domain scientists turn unstructured scientific image data into practical algorithms and downstream scientific discoveries.

### [260] [Causal Bias Detection in Generative Artifical Intelligence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11365)
*Drago Plecko*

Main category: cs.AI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着生成式AI在高风险领域广泛应用，其可能加剧现有社会偏见，亟需基于因果推理的公平性分析框架。传统因果公平性研究聚焦于单一预测函数，但生成式AI可自主构建任意变量条件分布，改变了因果机制的形成方式，因此需要新方法以应对这一复杂性。

Method: 提出一个统一的理论框架，形式化生成式AI中的因果公平性问题；推导新的因果分解结果，实现对不同因果路径及生成模型替代真实机制的公平性影响的细粒度量化；建立识别条件并设计高效的因果量估计器。

Result: 该方法能够有效分解生成式AI中公平性偏差的来源，揭示哪些因果路径或机制替换导致了不公平结果；在多个数据集上验证了大语言模型中的种族与性别偏见，证明了方法的有效性与实用性。

Conclusion: 生成式AI中的因果公平性需超越传统预测框架，引入更精细的因果分解与机制建模。本文提出的统一框架与方法为理解、评估和缓解生成式系统中的偏见提供了理论基础与实践工具。

Abstract: Automated systems built on artificial intelligence (AI) are increasingly deployed across high-stakes domains, raising critical concerns about fairness and the perpetuation of demographic disparities that exist in the world. In this context, causal inference provides a principled framework for reasoning about fairness, as it links observed disparities to underlying mechanisms and aligns naturally with human intuition and legal notions of discrimination. Prior work on causal fairness primarily focuses on the standard machine learning setting, where a decision-maker constructs a single predictive mechanism $f_{\widehat Y}$ for an outcome variable $Y$, while inheriting the causal mechanisms of all other covariates from the real world. The generative AI setting, however, is markedly more complex: generative models can sample from arbitrary conditionals over any set of variables, implicitly constructing their own beliefs about all causal mechanisms rather than learning a single predictive function. This fundamental difference requires new developments in causal fairness methodology. We formalize the problem of causal fairness in generative AI and unify it with the standard ML setting under a common theoretical framework. We then derive new causal decomposition results that enable granular quantification of fairness impacts along both (a) different causal pathways and (b) the replacement of real-world mechanisms by the generative model's mechanisms. We establish identification conditions and introduce efficient estimators for causal quantities of interest, and demonstrate the value of our methodology by analyzing race and gender bias in large language models across different datasets.
